11|53|Ɓe wi'i: "Ko an yo Huudu, kala ko addan-ɗaa men e ɓanngannduyee, menen men wonaali accooɓe reweteeɗi amen ɗin fii konngol maa ngol, menen men wonaali gomɗinooɓe ma
11|54|Men wi'atah si wanaa yoga e reweteeɗi amen ɗin meminirii ma bone". O maaki: "Min miɗo seedina Alla -seeditee onon kadi- wonnde min, ko mi daɗndiiɗo e kon ko sirkoton
11|55|gaanin Makko. Fewjanee lam on denndaangal, refti wata on fadee kam
11|56|Min mi fawike e Alla, Joomi am e Joomi mon. Alaa e ruugayngel si wanaa ko O nannguɗo jubuuru maggel. Pellet, Joomi am no e laawol focciingol
11|57|Si on huccitii, gomɗii mi yottinanii kon ko mi nulidaa e mooɗon. Joomi am lontinay yimɓe goo ɓe wonaa onon, on lorrirtaa Mo hay e huunde. Pellet, Joomi am ko deeno kala huunde
11|58|Nde yamiroore Amen nden ari, Men daɗndiri Huudi e ɓen gomɗimɓe wonnduɓe e makko yurmeende Amen. Men daɗndi ɓe lepte tiiɗuɗe
11|59|Ɓen ko Aadinkooɓe. Ɓe yedduno Aayeeje Joomi amɓɓe ɗen, ɓe yeddi Nulaaɓe maɓɓe ɓen, ɓe jokki yamiroore kala dunndaranke sanndolɗinɗo
11|60|Ɓe jokkindinaa ka aduna ɗoo, kuddi, e Ñalnde Darngal. Anndee pellet, Aadinkooɓe ɓen yeddi Joomi maɓɓe. Anndee goɗɗal woodanii Aadi'en, yimɓe Huudi
11|61|[Men Nulii] kadi e Samuuda'en, musiɗɗo maɓɓe Saalih, o maaki: "Ko onon yo yimɓe am, rewee Alla. Reweteeɗo alanaano on ko woori Mo. Ko Kanko fuɗɗi on ka leydi, O wuurni on e mayri. Insinanee Mo, refti tuubon ka Makko. Pellet Joomi am ko ɓaɗiiɗo, jaabotooɗo
11|62|Ɓe wi'i: "Ko an yo Saalihu, gomɗii a woniino hakkunde amen yaakoraaɗo ado ɗum ɗoo. E a haɗay men rewugol ko baabiraaɓe amen rewatno? Menen non, men wonii e sikke e huunde nde noddataa men e mun (sikke) jaaliiɗe
11|63|O maaki: "Ko onon yo yimɓe! Yeetee lam, si mi laatike e ɓanngannduyee immorde ka Joomi am, O okkii lam immorde ka Makko yurmeende, ko hommbo faabotoo mi ka Alla si mi yeddii Mo? On ɓeydataa lam si wanaa hayrugol
11|64|Ko onon yo yimɓe am, mbaa ɗoo ko ngelooba wonannde on maande. Tertee mba, mba ñaama ka leydi Alla. Wata on memir-mba bone, lepte ɓaɗtiiɗe heɓa on
11|65|Ɓe mborii-mba. o maaki: "Dakmitee ka galleeji mon balɗe tati! Ɗum ko fodoore nde fennetaake
11|66|Nde yamiroore Alla nden arunoo, Men daɗndiri Saalihu e ɓen gomɗimɓe wonduɓe e makko, yur-meende immorde ka Amen- e koyeera nden ñalnde Pellet Joomi maa, ko Kanko woni Doolnuɗo, Fooluɗo
11|67|Haacaango ngon nanngi tooñuɓe ɓen.Ɓe waɗtini ka galleeji maɓɓe jicciiɓe
11|68|A sikkay ɓe ñiiɓaano ɗon. Anndee pellet Samuudu en yedduno Joomi maɓɓe, anndee goɗɗal yurmee- nde (Alla) woodanii Samuuda'en
11|69|Gomɗii Nulaaɓe Amen ɓen addanii Ibraahiima welo-welo, ɓe wi'i: "Kisal (e mon)". O maaki: "Kisal (e mon). Neeɓaali o ardi e ngaari juɗaandi
11|70|Nde o yi'unoo juuɗe maɓɓe ɗen yottaaki ndi, o faytiɓe (o sikkitii), o soomi kulol e maɓɓe. Ɓe wi'i: "Wata a hulu, ko men nulaaɓe e yimɓe Luuti ɓen
11|71|Tawi suddiiɗo makko on no darii, o jali, Men weltiniri mo Ishaaqa, e ɓaawo Ishaaqa, Yaaquube
11|72|[Debbo on] wi'i: "Ee jalla am! E mi jibinay e hoore ko mi nayeejo, e hino oo ɗoo gorko am ko nayeejo? Pellet ɗum ɗoo ko huunde haawniinde
11|73|Ɓe wi'i: "E a haawete fiyaaku Alla on? Yurmeende Alla e barkiiji Makko wonii e mon, yimɓe nduu suudu. Pellet ko O Yettiniiɗo Tedduɗo
11|74|Nde kulol ngol iwunoo e Ibraahiima, welo-welo ngon ari e makko, himo yeddandira e Amen fii yimɓe Luuti ɓen
11|75|Pellet, Ibraahiima ko muññiiɗo, heewuɗo yankina-gol, tuuboowo
11|76|Ko an yo Ibraahiima, ɗuurno gaayi e ɗum; gomɗii yamiroore Joomi maa nden arii, e pellet, lepte aray e maɓɓe lepte ɗe ruttetaake
11|77|Nde Nulaaɓe Amen ɓen arunoo ka Luuti, o sunanii ɓe, o ɓiɗtori fonndo makko ngon fii maɓɓe, o maaki: "Ndee ɗoo ko ñalaande saɗtunde
11|78|Yimɓe makko ɓen ari e makko e yaccoo. Ado ɗum hari hiɓe gollaynoo bonɗi. O maaki: "Ko onon yo yimɓe am, ɓee ɗoo ko jwiɓe am: ko kamɓe ɓuri laaɓannde on. Hulee Alla, wata on hersinam e hoɓ- ɓe am. E gorko feewuɗo alaa e mo'on
11|79|Ɓe wi'i: "Pellet hiɗa anndi haaju alanah men e jiwɓe maa ɓen, pellet hiɗa anndi kadi ko men faalaa
11|80|O maaki: "Sinno miɗo marunoo doole e mon! Maa mi fattinoo(moolo) e soɓɓundu sattundu(jookdu)
11|81|[Hoɓɓe ɓen] wi'i: "Ko an yo Luutu, pellet ko men Nulaaɓe Joomi maa. Ɓe hewtataa ma. Yaltinir ɓeynguure maa nden e taƴunnde jemma, wata gooto e mo'on yeƴƴito si wanaa suddiiɗo maa on, ko fii heɓay mo ko heɓata ɓeya kon. Anndon fodoore maɓɓe nden ko ka subaka. E subaka on laataaki ɓaɗiido
11|82|Nde yamiroore Amen nden arunoo, Men waɗtiri dow [saare] nden ley mayre, Men caaƴini e mayre kaaƴe iwruɗe loope juɗaaɗe rewondirɗe
11|83|Maandinaaɗe ka Joomi maa. Ɗe wonaali woɗɗuɗe e tooñooɓe ɓen
11|84|[Men Nulii] kadi e Madyana'en, musiɗɗo maɓɓe on Shu'aybu, o maaki: "Ko onon yo yimɓe am, rewee Alla; reweteeɗo alanaa on ko woori Mo. Wata on ɗuytu ɓetu ngun e manndake ɗen. Min on miɗo yi'i on e moƴƴere. Min non miɗo hulani on lepte ñalaande fiiltiindede
11|85|Ko onon yo yimɓe am, hunniree ɓetu ngun e manndake ɗen nunɗal. Wata on ɗuytan yimɓe ɓen coggu maɓɓe ngun, wata on yahru ka leydi bonnugol
11|86|Ko keddiiɗe Alla ɗen ɓuri moƴƴannde on si on laatike gomɗimɓe. Mi wonaali reenoowo on
11|87|Ɓe wi'i: "Ko an yo Shu'aybu! E ko julde maa nden yamiru-maa nde men accata rewugol ko baabiraa- ɓe amen ɓen rewaynoo kon, maa nde men gollata huuwata e jawle amen ɗen ko men yiɗi? Pellet an ko a muññiiɗo feewuɗo
11|88|O maaki: "Ko onon yo yimɓe am, yeetee lam: si miɗo e ɓanngannduyee immorde ka Joomi am, O arsikii lam immorde ka Makko arsike moƴƴo?... Mi faandaaki lunndaade on e kon haɗay-mi on e muuɗum. Mi faandaaki si wanaa moƴƴingol fotde yeru am on. Kawral am wonaali si wanaa ka Alla. Ko e Makko mi fawii, ko ka Makko mi ruttotoo
11|89|Ko onon yo yimɓe am, wata ngayngu am defu on haa heɓa on sugu ko heɓunoo yimɓe Nuuhu maa yimɓe Huudi maa yimɓe Saalih. Yimɓe Luuti ɓen kan woɗɗitaaki on
11|90|Insinanee Joomi mon, refti tuubanon Mo. Pelet Joomi am ko Hinnotooɗo, Giɗo
11|91|Ɓe wi'i: "Ko an yo Shu'aybu, men alah faamude ko ɗuuɗi e kon ko wi'ataa; menen meɗen yi'e hakku-nde amen lo'uɗo. Si wanaano gorol maa ngol, men piyirteno keeƴe. An a wonaali tedduɗo e amen
11|92|O maaki: "E ko gorol am ngol ɓuri teddudo e mon diini Alla, on waɗtirii mo ɓaawo mon hawkaaɗo? Pellet Joomi am ko huɓindiiɗo(fiiltiido) ko huuwoton kon
11|93|Ko onon yom yimɓe am, gollee e nokku mo'on. Min kadi ko mi golloowo. Aray nde anndoton ko hombo lepte hoynooje arat e mu'u, e ko hommbo woni fenoowo on. (Jooni non) habbitee! Min kadi miɗo wondi e mon habbitiiɗo
11|94|Nde yamiroore Amen nden arunoo, Men daɗndiri Shu'aybu e ɓen gomɗimɓe wonnduɓe e makko yurmeende Amen. Haacaango ngon nanngi ɓen tooñuɓe, ɓe waɗtini ka cuuɗi maɓɓe jicciiɓe
11|95|A wi'ay ɓe ñiiɓaano ɗon. Anndee woɗɗineede yurmeende wonanii Madayana wano Samuuda'en woɗɗiniranoo
11|96|Gomɗii Men Nulirii Muusaa Aayeeje Amen ɗen e hujja ɓannguɗo
11|97|Ha e Fir'awna e mbatu mun. Ɓe jokkii yamiroore Fir'awna nden, yamiroore Fir'awna non wanaa feewunde
11|98|O ardoyto yimɓe makko ɓen Ñalnde Darngal, o jolna ɓe ka Yiite. (Nge)bonii jolirde jolaande
11|99|Ɓe jokkinaama kuddi e oo (aduna), e Ñalnde Darngal. Bonii ballal ngal ɓe jokkindiranaa
11|100|Ɗum ko jeyaaɗum e kumpite ca'e, Meɗen fillano maa ɗum: no e majje ñiiɓuɗe e conyaaɗe
11|101|Men tooñaali ɓe. Ko woni, ko kamɓe tooñi ko'e maɓɓe. Reweteeɗi maɓɓe ɗin ɗiɓe rewaynoo gaanin ɗin duncanaali ɓe hay e huunde, tuma nde yamiroore Joomi maa nden arunoo; ɗi ɓeydaali ɓe si wanaa hayrude
11|102|Ko wano nii nanngal Joomi maa ngal, si tawii O nanngii ca'e ɗen hara ko ɗe tooñuɗe. Pellet nanngal Makko ngal ko muusungal saɗtungal
11|103|Pellet tasakuyee wonii e ɗum ɗoo wonannde on hulɗo lepte laakara. Nden ko ñalaande aade en mooɓoyte e mun, nde kadi ko ñalaande seedoyteende
11|104|Men neɓnataa nde si wanah haa e lajal limangal
11|105|Ñalnde ngal arata, wonkii (woo) wowlatah si wanaa e duŋayee Makko. Hino e maɓɓe malkisaaɗo e malaaɗo
11|106|Si ko malkisaaɓe ɓen, ko ka Yiite; hino woodani ɓe nder ton ookaango e hiikaango
11|107|Ko ɓe luttinteeɓe nder magge fotde kammuuli ɗin e leydi ndin no duumii, si wanah si Joomii maa muuyii; pellet Joomi maa ko waɗoowo kala ko O faandii
11|108|Si tawii non ko malaaɓe ɓen, ko ka nder Aljanna woni ko duumintee e mun fotde kammuuli ɗin e leydi ndin no duumii, si wanaa si Joomi maa muuyii. (Ɗum) ko dokkal ngal taƴondirtaa
11|109|Wata a wonu e sikke e huunde ko ɓee rewata. Ɓe rewiraali si wanaa no baabiraaɓe maɓɓe rewiray- noo ko adii. Menen non, Men hunniranay ɓe geɓal maɓɓe ngal ko aldah e ɗuytugol
11|110|Gomɗii Men okkii Muusaa Deftere nden, luutondi- raa e mayre. Si wanaano konngol ardinoongol immorde ka Joomi maa, ñaaweteno hakkunde maɓɓe. Kamɓe kan hiɓe e sikke sikkitiiɗo e e mayre
11|111|Wonaali kala maɓɓe si wanaa Joomi maa hunna- nay ɓe (njoɓdi) kuuɗe maɓɓe. Pellet ko O humpitiiɗo ko ɓe gollata kon
11|112|Ñiiɓir [e focciingol ngol] wano yamiraɗaa non, e tuubuɓe wonnduɓe e maaɗa. Wata on bewu. Pellet ko O reenuɗo ko golloton kon
11|113|Wata on ooñor e tooñuɓe ɓen sakko Yiite ngen mema on. Alanah on gaanin Alla yiɗɓe. Refti on walloytaake
11|114|Ñinnu julde nden ka seraaji ɗiɗi ñalorma e saa'iiji jemma. Pellet moƴƴi ɗin hino monta bonɗi ɗin. Ɗum ko waaju wonannde ɓen waajitotooɓe
11|115|Muñño. Pellet Alla yeebataa njoɓdi moƴƴinooɓe ɓen
11|116|Ko haɗnoo wona e gire adinooɓe on ɓen, joomiraa- ɓe kedde, ɓe no haɗa e bonnugol ka leydi! si seeɗaaɓe e ɓen ɓe Men daɗndunoo e maɓɓe. Tooñuɓe ɓen jokki e ko ɓe neeminaa e mun kon, ɓe laatii bomɓe
11|117|Joomi maa siforaali halkiroowo ca'e e hoore tooñe tawa yimɓe maɓɓe ko moƴƴinooɓe
11|118|Sinno Joomi maa muuyiino, O waɗayno yimɓe ɓen moftal gootal. Ɓe seerataa ko ɓe luutondirooɓe
11|119|si wanaa ɓen ɓe Joomi maa yurmaa. Ko sabu ɗum O tagiri ɓe. Konngol Joomi maa ngol jojjii wonnde: "Pellet, Mi hebbiniray Jahannama jinna e yimɓe, ɓe denndaangal
11|120|Kala e mu'un, Meɗen fillano maa kabaruuji Nulaaɓe, ko Men tabintinra ɗum ɓernnde maa ngon. Aranii ma e ngol (cortewol) goonga e waaju e janntoore wonannde gomɗimɓe ɓen
11|121|Maakan ɓen ɓe gomɗinah: "Gollee e nokku mo'on. Menen kadi, ko men gollooɓe
11|122|Habbitee kadi. Menen ko men habbitiiɓe
11|123|Ko Alla heeranii wirniiɗi kammuuli ɗin e leydi ndin, ko ka Makko fiyaaku no fow ruttetee. Awa rewu Mo, fawo-ɗaa e Makko. Joomi maa wonaali welsindiiɗo e kon ko golloton
12|1|Alif, laam, raa. Ɗen ko Aayeeje Deftere ɓanngunde nden
12|2|Menen Men jippiniriinde janngeteende [e ɗemngal] Aarabu, belajo'o, on haqqilay
12|3|Menen Meɗen fillano maa ko ɓuri moƴƴude e fillayee, e kon ko Men wahayini e maaɗa ndee Alqur'aanaare, hay si woniino ado mayre, ko a jeyaaɗo e welsindiiɓe ɓen
12|4|Tuma nde Yuusufu maakannoo ben makko: "Ko onon yo baaba'en, mi yi'ii [e koyɗol] koode sappo e go'o, naange ngen kadi e lewru ndun; mi yi'ii ɗin no sujjana lam
12|5|[Ben makko] maaki: "Ko an yo ɓinngel am, wata a fillano musiɗɓe maa ɓen koyɗol maa ngol sakko ɓe fewjane feere; pellet seytaane ko gañoAade ɓannguɗo
12|6|Ko wano nii Joomi maa suɓoray maa, O anndine firo koyɗi, O timmina neema Makko on e maaɗa e ɓeynguure Yaaquuba nden, wano O timminirnoo mo e baabiraaɓe maa ɓen ɗiɗo: Ibraahiima e ishaaqa. Pellet Joomi maa ko Annduɗo Ñeeñuɗo
12|7|Gomɗii wonii e Yuusufa e musiɗɓe makko ɓen, taskuyeeji wonannde lanndotooɓe ɓen
12|8|tuma nde ɓe wi'unoo: "Pellet ko Yuusufa e neene-gooto mun on ɓuraa yiɗeede ka ben-men dii enen, enen le ko en jamaa ɗuuɗuɓe. Pellet ben-men wonii e majjere ɓanngunde
12|9|Waree Yuusufa maa feroɗon mo e leydi; yeeso ben mon ngon heeranoo on, wonton ɓaawo ɗum yimɓe moƴƴuɓe
12|10|Gooto e maɓɓe wi'i: "Wata on waru Yuusufa, weddee mo ka niɓe woyndu yoga e seteeɓe hoccay mo, si on laatike gllooɓe
12|11|Ɓe wi'i: "Ko an yo ben amen, ko heɓu-maa a hoolotaako men e fii Yuusufa? Menen le ko men laaɓamɓe mo reedu
12|12|Accitidu-mo e amen o ñaama, o fija. Menen ko men reenooɓe mo
12|13|O maaki: "Min no suninay lam nde yahdoton e makko; miɗo huli nde boyeeru ndu ñaamata-mo ka welsindi-ɗon e makko
12|14|Ɓe wi'i: "Pellet si saafaandu ñaamii mo e hoore ko men jamaa ɗuuɗuɓe, haray ko men hayruɓe
12|15|Nde ɓe yahdunoo e makko, ɓe fottani ukkugol mo ka niɓe woyndu, Men wahayini e makko: "Ma a yeetitoyo ɓe ɗee kuuɗe maɓɓe hara ɓe so'aa anndude
12|16|Ɓe arti ka ben maɓɓe kiikiiɗe hiɓe woya
12|17|Ɓe wi'i: "Ko an yo baaben amen, menen men yehii meɗen adondira, men acci Yuusufa ka kaake amen saafaandu ndun ñaami mo. A hoolotaako men non, hay si men wonii goonguɓe
12|18|Ɓe ardi e dolokke makko on hino moddi ƴiiƴam fenaande. O maaki: "Si ko woni, wonkiiji mon ɗin cuɗinanii on fiyaaku. Ko muñal moƴƴal [heddanii lam]! Ko Alla woni wallitorɗo e ko sifotoɗon kon
12|19|Seteeɓe ari, ɓe nuli ƴoogoowo maɓɓe on, o jippini baagal makko ngal. O wi'i: "Ee wel¨-welo am! E hino paykum!" Ɓe suuɗiri mo keyee maɓɓe. Alla non ko annduɗo ko ɓe gollata kon
12|20|Ɓe yeeyiri mo coggel famɗungel: dirhamu-woy limotoo-koy. Ɓe woni welsindiiɓe e fii makko
12|21|Sooduɗo mo on Misra wi'ani ɓeyngu makko: "Teddin jipporde makko. Hino gasa ka o nafa en maa jogitoɗe mo ɓiɗɗo". Ko nii Men hoɗniri Yuusufa ka leydi fii yo Men anndin mo firo koyɗi. Alla ko fooluɗo e fiyaaku Makko on: kono ko ɓuri ɗuuɗude e yimɓe ɓen anndaa
12|22|Nde o yottinoo sagatalaaku makko, Men okki mo faamu e anndal. Ko wano nii Men yoɓirta moƴƴinooɓe ɓen
12|23|On [debbo] mo on woni e suudu mun ɗaɓɓiri mo hoore-makko. O soki baafe ɗen o wi'i: "Mi heblanii-mo-ma!" O maaki: "Moolaare Alla! Jeyɗo lam on moƴƴinii weerde am. Si ko woni, tooñooɓe ɓen maletaake
12|24|Gomɗii [debbo] on himmanii oon. Kanko kadi o himmanayno mo si wanaa o yi'ii hujja Joomi makko on. Ko nii [Men gerdiri] fii yo Men yiltu mo e bone e pankare. Pellet ko o jeyaaɗo e jeyaaɓe amen laɓɓinaaɓe ɓen
12|25|Ɓe ɗiɗo kala ɓe adondiri ka baafal, o seekiri dolokke oya on ɓaawo. Ɓe tawi moodi makko ka baafal. [debbo] on wi'i: "Ko honɗum woni njoɓdi on faalanaaɗo ɓeynguure maa nden bonki si wanaa yo soke [o leptiree] lepte muusuɗe
12|26|[Yuusufu] maaki: "Ko kanko ɗaɓɓiri lam hoore-am". Tawanooɗo e yimɓe [debbo] on seeditii: "Si tawii dolokke mum on ko yeeso seekiraa, haray ko [debbo] on goongi, kanko [gorko] on ko jeyaaɗo e fenuɓe ɓen
12|27|Si tawii non dolokke makko on ka ɓaawo seekiraa, haray [debbo] on fenii, kanko [gorko] on ko o jeyaaɗo goonguɓe ɓen
12|28|Nde [moodi makko] yi'unoo dolokke on ko ɓaawo seekori, o wi'i: "Ɗum ko jeyaaɗum e pewje mon! Pellet pewje mon ɗen ko haawniiɗe
12|29|Yuusufa, ɗuurno gaayi e ɗum. An [debbo on], insinano junuubi(bakkaat) maa ɗin; tawde pellet a jeyaama e woopuɓe ɓen
12|30|Rewɓe ɓen ka saare wi'i: "Debbo laamɗo on ɗaɓɓirii kurkaadu makko ndun hoore-makko! Gomɗii giggol ɓurtirii mo. Menen dey meɗen yi'a oo [debbo] e majjere ɓanngunde
12|31|Nde o nanunoo pewje maɓɓe ɗen, o nulani ɓe, o hebilani ɓe ngawluuji, o jonni gooto kala e maɓɓe laɓi, o wi'i: "Yaltu e maɓɓe!". Nde ɓe yi'unoo mo, ɓe mawnini mo, ɓe hetti juuɗe maɓɓe ɗen, ɓe wi'i: "Kaawee Alla! Oo wanaa ɓanndinke, oo wonaali si wanaa malaa'ikaajo tedduɗo
12|32|O wi'i: "Ko oo mo'on felirɗon lam fii mun, gomɗii mi ɗaɓɓirii mo hoore-makko o haɗitii. Si wonii o waɗaali ko mi yamirta mo kon, ma o soke ma o laato jeyaaɗo e hoyɓe ɓen
12|33|O maaki: "Joomi am, Ko kaso ngon ɓurani lam e ko ɓe noddata lam e mun kon. Si a pottinaani lam pewje maɓɓe ɗen, mi ooñoto e maɓɓe, mi jeyee e majjuɓe ɓen
12|34|Joomi makko jaabinani mo, O firliti e makko pewje maɓɓe ɗen. Pellet, ko Kanko woni Nanoowo, Annduɗo On
12|35|Refti feeñani (rewɓe) ɓen ɓaawo nde ɓe yi'i maandeeji ɗin, ma o sok-mbo tigi haa e saa'i
12|36|Sukaaɓe ɗiɗo naatidi e makko ka kaso. Goɗɗo e maɓɓe wi'i: "Min mi hoyɗii hoore-am miɗo siiwa sanngara". Oya kadi wi': "Min mi hoyɗii hoore-am miɗo ronndii ka hoore-am cobbal, colli no ñaama e maggal". Humpitii men firo ɗin, menen men yi'ii ma jeyaaɗo e moƴƴinooɓe ɓen
12|37|O maaki: "Ñaametee mo wonaɗon okkoreede on aratah on si wanaa mi humpitay on firo mun ado o arde on. Ɗum mo'on ko jeyeeɗum e ko Joomi am anndini lam. Min mi ɗalii diina yimɓe ɓe gomɗinaa Alla, hara kamɓe e fii laakara ko ɓe yedduɓe
12|38|Jokku-mi diina baabiraaɓe am ɓen: Ibraahiima e Ishaaqa e Yaaquuba. Haananaa men nde men kafidata e Alla hay e huunde. Ɗum ko jeyaaɗum e ɓural Alla e dow amen e hoore yimɓe ɓen; kono ko ɓuri ɗuuɗude e yimɓe ɓen ɓe yettataa
12|39|Ko onon yo wondiiɓe am ɗiɗo ka kaso! E ko reweteeɗi sertuɗi ɓuri moƴƴude, kaa ko Alla Gooto Fooluɗo on
12|40|On alah e rewde gaanin Makko, si wanah inɗe ɗe innuɗon ɗum, onon e baabiraaɓe mon, Alla jippinanaali ɗen hujja. Ñaawoore nden alanah si wanaa Alla. O yamirii wata on rewu si wanaa Kanko. Ko ɗum ɗum woni diina ñiiɓuka kan; kono ko ɓuri ɗuuɗude e yimɓe ɓen ɓe anndaa
12|41|Ko onon yo wondiiɓe am ɗiɗo ka kaso! Goɗɗo e mo'on yarnay koohoo mun on sanngara; oya on, o fetee, colli ɗin ñaama ka hoore makko. Fiyaaku mo lanndiɗon fii mun on ñaawaama
12|42|O maakani on mo o sikke daɗay e maɓɓe kamɓe ɗiɗo: "Janto lam ka koohoojo maa on". Seytaane yejjintini mo jantanagol koohoojo makko on. [Yuusufu] ñiiɓiti ka kaso yoga e duuɓi
12|43|Laamɗo on wi'i: "Min mi yi'ii (e koyɗol) na'i jeeɗiɗi fayɗi, na nyaama fooƴuɗi jeeɗiɗi ɗin, e dukke jeeɗiɗi kecce, e goɗɗi goo yooruɗi. Ko onon yo dental, firtanee lam ngol koyɗol am, si on laatike firtooɓe koyɗi
12|44|Ɓe wi'i: "Ko jiiɓu-jaaɓu koyɗi ! Men wonaali annduɓe firo koyɗi
12|45|Daɗuɗo on e ɓeya ɗiɗo miijitii ɓaawo dumunna o wi'i: "Min mi humpitay on firo maggol. Nulee lam
12|46|Yuusufu, an yo goonguɗo! Yeetii men fii na'i jeeɗiɗi fayɗi, na nyaama fooƴuɗi jeeɗiɗi ɗin, e dukke jeeɗiɗi kecce, e goɗɗi goo yooruɗi, belajo'o mi ruttoo ka yimɓe ɓen, belajo'o, ɓe annday
12|47|O maaki: "On remay duuɗi jeeɗiɗi jokkondirɗi. Kala ko soñuɗon, accon ɗum ka dukkal(butaali) mun, si wanaa seeɗa e kon ko ñaamoton
12|48|Refti aroyay ɓaawo ɗum, duuɓi jeeɗiɗi saɗtuɗi, ɗin (duuɓi) no ñaama kon ko marnaɗon ɗi si wanaa seeɗa e ko maroton [fii awdi]
12|49|Refti aroya ɓaawo ɗum, hitaande, ko e mayre yimɓe ɓen toɓetee, ko e mayre kadi ɓe hamata
12|50|Laamɗo on wi'i: "Addanee lam on". Nde imminaaɗo on arunoo mo, o maaki: "Rutto ka koohoojo maa on lanndoɗaa mo: Ko woni fiyaaku ɓen rewɓe hettunooɓe juuɗe mun ɗen? Pellet Joomi am ko annduɗo pewje maɓɓe ɗen
12|51|[Laamɗo on] wi'i: "Ko honɗum wonunoo fiyaaku mon tuma ɗaɓɓirnoɗon Yuusufa hoore-makko?" Ɓe wi'i: "Moolaare Alla! Men anndiraa mo ko boni". Ɓeyngu laamɗo on wi'i: "Jooni goonga kan feeñii. Ko min ɗaɓɓirnoo mo hoore-makko, pellet ko o jeyaaɗo e goonguɓe ɓen
12|52|Ɗum ko fii yo o anndu wonnde mi janfaaki mo ka wirnii, e wonnde Alla fewnatah pewje janfotooɓe ɓen
12|53|Mi laɓɓinaa hoore-am, tawde wonkii ko heewuki yamirde bone, si wanah kin ki Joomi am yurmini. Joomi am ko Haforoowo Hinnotooɗo
12|54|Laamɗo on wi'i: "Addanee lam mo, mi heertinana mo hoore-am". Nde o yewtunoo mo, o wi'i: "An on hannde ka amen, ko a jom-nokku hoolaaɗo
12|55|O maaki: "Waɗam e hoore-ngaluuji leydi ndin: ko mi reenoowo annduɗo
12|56|Ko wano nii Men ñimnirani Yuusufa ka leydi, himo jippora e mayri nokku ka o yiɗi. Meɗen heɓnira yurmeende Amen nden on mo Men muuyi, men yeebataa njoɓdi moƴƴinooɓe ɓen
12|57|Pellet ko njoɓdi laakara ndin ɓuri moƴƴannde ɓen gomɗimɓe ɓe laatii gomɗuɓe
12|58|Baaba-gootooɓe Yuusufa ɓen ari ɓe naati ka makko. O annditi ɓe, kono kamɓe ɓe paayti mo
12|59|Tuma nde o hebllannooɓe doŋlle maɓɓe ɗen, o maaki: "Addanee lam musiɗɗo mon baaba-gooto. E on yi'aali miɗo timmina ɓetu ngun, e wonnde ko mi ɓurdo moƴƴude e weernooɓe ɓen
12|60|Si on addanaali lam mo, haray ɓetu alanaa on ka am ɗoo; wata on ɓado lam kadi
12|61|Ɓe wi'i: "Men ɗaɓɓiray mo ben makko, menen ko men gollooɓe (ɗum)
12|62|O maakani gollooɓe makko ɓen: "Waɗee coggeeli(njigguuji) maɓɓe ɗin ka doŋlle maɓɓe: belajo'o ɓe annditay ɗi si ɓe ruttike ka yimɓe maɓɓe ɓen, belajo'o ɓe yiltoto
12|63|Tuma nde ɓe ruttinoo ka ben maɓɓe, ɓe wi'i: "Ko an yo ben(baaba) amen, men salanaama ɓetu. neldu amen musiɗɗo amen on, men ɓetanee. Ko men reenooɓe mo
12|64|O maaki: "Hara mi hooloray on e fii makko, si wanaa no mi hoolornoo on non e neene-gooto makko on ko adii? Ko Alla woni moƴƴo reenoowo, ko Kanko ɓuri moƴƴude yurmeteeɓe ɓen
12|65|Nde ɓe udditunoo doŋlle maɓɓe ɗen, ɓe tawi coggeeli(njigguuji) maɓɓe ɗin ruttaama e maɓɓe. Ɓe wi'i: "Ko an yo ben amen, ko men ɗaɓɓata [kadi]? Ɗii ko coggeeli amen, ɗi ruttaama e amen. Meɗen jiggana yimɓe amen, men reena musiɗɗo amen on, men ɓeydora ɓetu ngelooba; ɗum ko ɓetu newiingu
12|66|O maaki: "Mi immindintaa(neldatah) mo e mooɗon haa ƴettanon mi ahadi ka Alla, wonnde on artiranay lam mo si wanaa hara on huɓinda". Ɓaawo ɓe ƴettanii mo ahadi maɓɓe ndin, o maaki: "Alla e dow ko wowluɗen kon, ko O deeno
12|67|O maaki: "Ko onon yo ɓiɗɓe am, wata on naatiroy e damal gootal, naatiree e dame seertuɗe. Mi dun-cantaa on e (muyɗe) Alla hay e huunde. Ñaawoore alanaa si wanaa Alla: Ko e Makko mi fawii, ko e makko kadi, yo fawo fawotooɓe ɓen
12|68|Nde ɓe naatirnoo nokku ka ben maɓɓe yamirnoo ɓe ɗon, ɗum wonaano no duncana ɓe [ko iwri] ka Alla si wanaa haaju wonunooɗo e fittaandu Yaaquuba mo o gasini. Kanko on, ko o jom-ganndal ngal Men anndini mo. Kono ko ɓuri ɗuuɗude e yimɓe ɓen ɓe anndaa
12|69|Nde ɓe naatunoo ka Yuusufa, o maɓɓi neene-gooto makko on e makko, o maaki: "Ko mi neene-gooto maa, wata a sunor ko ɓe huuwaynoo
12|70|Tuma nde o hebilannoo ɓe doŋlle maɓɓe ɗen, o waɗi etirgal ngal ka doŋngal neene-gooto makko on, refti ewnotooɗo eewnii: "Ko onon yo seteeɓe, Ko on wuyɓe
12|71|Ɓe fewtiti e maɓɓe ɓe wi'i: "Ko honɗum hattiɗon
12|72|Ɓe wi'i: "Men hattike etirde laamɗo on. Hino woodani kala adduɗo ngal, doŋngal ngelooba, ko min woni fawtiiɗo ɗum
12|73|Ɓe wi'i: "Men woondirii Alla, gomɗii hiɗon anndi men araali bonnugol ka leydi, men laataaki kadi wuyɓe
12|74|Ɓe wi'i: "Ko wonata njoɓdi makko si tawii ko on fenooɓe
12|75|Ɓe wi'i: "Njoɓdi makko: ko kala mo: [ɗum] tawaa ka doŋngal mun, haray ko kanko [tigir] woni njoɓdi mun. Ko wano non men yoɓitirta tooñooɓe ɓen
12|76|[Yuusufu] fuɗɗori doŋle maɓɓe ɗen ado doŋngal neene-gooto makko on; refti o yaltiniri nde ka doŋngal neene-gooto makko on. Ko wano non men fewjirani Yuusufa, [tawde] o hattantaano nanngude neene-gooto makko on ka sariya laamɗo on, si wanaa hara ko Alla muuyi. Meɗen ɓantana darajaaji on mo Men muuyi. No e dow kala jom-ganndal ganndo [goo]
12|77|Ɓe wi'i: "Si o wujjii, haray neene-gooto makko wujjiino ko adii". Yuusufu mari ɗum ka wonkii makko, o feññinanaali ɓe ɗum. O maaki: "Ko onon ɓuri bonnde nokku! Ko Alla ɓuri anndude ko sifotoɗon
12|78|Ɓe wi'i: "Ko an yo laamɗo on, oo no mari baabiraawo nawyuɗo oggos; ƴettu gooto e amen lonto makko. Menen men yi'ii ma jeyaaɗo e moƴƴinooɓe ɓen
12|79|O maaki: "Moolaara Alla nde men nanngata si wanaa on mo men tawi doŋlle amen ɗen e juuɗe mun. Mene haray ontuma ko men tooñuɓe
12|80|Nde ɓe taƴinoo fii hettugol mo, ɓe martiti ko ɓe gunndondirɓe. Mawɗo maɓɓe on wi'i: "E on anndaa wonnde ben mon ƴettodii e mo'on ahadi ka Alla, e aranun tuma welsindinoɗon e Yuusufa? Mi seerataa leydi ndin haa ben am duŋanoo lam maa O ñaawana lam [hettugol mo], ko Kanko ɓuri moƴƴude e ñaawooɓe ɓen
12|81|Ruttee ka ben mon wi'on: "Ko an yo ben amen, ɓiɗɗo maa on wujjii. Men seedaaki si wanaa ko men anndi, men wonaali reenuɓe ko wirnii
12|82|Lanndo (yimɓe) saare nden nde men wonunoo e mun, e seteeɓe ɓen ɓe men hawrondirnoo e mun. Pellet ko men goonguɓe
12|83|[Yaaquuba] maaki: "Wonkiiji mon ɗin cuɗanii on fiyaake! Ko muñal labangal. Hino hasii ka Alla artiranta mi ɓe, ɓe denndaangal. Ko Kanko woni Annduɗo, Ñeeñuɗo
12|84|O ɗuurnii ɓe o maaki: "Ee suno am e fii Yuusufa!" Gite makko ɗen rawniri suno. Ko o suuɗɗo suno
12|85|Ɓe wi'i: "Men woodirii Alla! A seerataa hiɗa janntoo fii Yuusufa, haa wonaa horsuɗo maa wonaa jeyaaɗo e halkiiɓe ɓen
12|86|O maaki: "Anndee ko e Alla mi wullitotoo annde am e sunaare am. Miɗo anndi ka Alla ko on anndaa
12|87|Ko onon yo ɓiɗɓe am, yehee tefon fii Yuusufa e neene-gooto makko on. Wata on taƴo e yurmeende Alla. Ko fii, taƴotaako e yurmeende Alla si wanaa yimɓe yedduɓe ɓen
12|88|Nde ɓe naatunoo ka makko [kanko Yuusufa], ɓe wi'i: "Ko an yo laamɗo, lorra heɓii men memen e ɓeynguure amen; men ardii e sil'a jaasuɗo. Hunnan men ɓetu ngun, sakko-ɗaa e amen. Pellet, Alla yoɓay sakkotooɓe ɓen
12|89|O maaki: "Enee, on annditii ko waɗunoɗon Yuusufa e neene-gooto makko on kon tuma nde wonunoɗon majjuɓe
12|90|Ɓe wi'i: "Kere ko an woni Yuusufa?" O maaki: "Ko min woni Yuusufa. Oo ɗoo ko miñam. Gomɗii Alla moƴƴike e amen. Ko fii, mo gomɗii o muññike, pellet, Alla yeebataa njoɓdi moƴƴinooɓe ɓen
12|91|Ɓe wi'i: "Men woondiri Alla, Alla ɓurnii ma e amen, men woniino woopuɓe
12|92|O maaki: "Feloore alaa e hoore-mon hannde! Yo Alla yawtan on. Ko Kano woni Moƴƴo Yurmeteeɗo
12|93|Yahdee e oo dolokke am ɗoo, werloɗon mo ka yeeso baaben am: o wattinay yi'oowo. Addanon lam ɓeynguure mon nden ɓe denndaangal
12|94|Nde seteeɓe ɓen seerti [yalti Misra]ben maɓɓe maaki: "Min miɗo heɓa balangol Yuusufa, sinno wanaa fii yo on ɗaytinam
12|95|Ɓe wi'i: "Men woondirii Alla, an hiɗa e majjere maaɗa ɓooyunde nden
12|96|Nde wewlinoowo on arunoo, o werlii [dolokke] on ka yeeso makko, o wonti yi'oowo. O maaki: "E mi wi'anaano on miɗo anndi ka Alla ko on anndaa
12|97|Ɓe wi'i: "Ko an yo ben amen, insinano men junuubi amen. Menen men woniino woopuɓe
12|98|O maaki: "Armami insinano on Joomi am. Ko Kanko woni Haforoowo, Hinnotooɗo
12|99|Nde ɓe naatunoo ka Yuusufa, o weerni ka makko [ɗon] mawɓe makko ɓen ɗiɗo, o maaki: "Naatiree Misra, si Alla muuyii, ko on hooliiɓe
12|100|O towniri mawɓe makko ɓen ɗiɗo ka belorki(danki), ɓe naayirani mo sujjugol. O maaki:"Ko onon yo baaba'en, ko ɗum ɗoo woni firo koyɗol am ngol oya tuma, gomɗii Joomi am waɗii ngol goonga. Gomɗii O moƴƴike e am tuma O yaltinnoo lam ka kaso, O itti on ka ladde, ɓaawo nde seytaane bonnii hakkunde am e ben-gootooɓe am ɓen. Pellet, Joomi am ko newaniiɗo ko O muuyi kon. Ko Kanko woni Annduɗo, Ñeeñuɗo
12|101|Joomi am, gomɗii A yeɗii lam laamu, A anndinii lam kadi firo koyɗi. [An] Taguɗo kammuuli ɗin e leydi ndin, ko An woni giɗo am aduna e laakara. Ƴettitam ko mi juulɗo, waɗitdaa lam e moƴƴuɓe ɓen
12|102|Ɗum ko jeyaaɗum e kumpite wirniiɗe, Meɗen wahayini ɗe e maaɗa. A tawanooka e maɓɓe tuma nde ɓe eɓɓunoo fiyaaku maɓɓe on hiɓe fewja
12|103|Ko ɓuri ɗuuɗude e yimɓe ɓen, hay si a rerɗi, (ɓe) wonaali gomɗinooɓe
12|104|A ɗaɓɓiraali ɓe e ɗum njoɓdi. Nde wonaali si wanaa waaju wonannde winndere nden
12|105|Ɗuuɗii e Aayeeje ka kammuuli e ka leydi, hiɓe rewa e majje hara ko ɓe ɗuurniiɓe ɗe
12|106|Ko ɓuri ɗuuɗude e maɓɓe gomɗintaa Alla, si wanaa hara ko ɓe sirkuɓe
12|107|E ɓe hooli nde hippooje arata ɓe e lepte Alla ɗen maa darngal ngal ardira ɓe juhal, hara kamɓe ɓe so'aa
12|108|Maaku: "Ko ngo'ol woni laawol am, miɗo noddira e Alla dow hujja, min e ɓen jokkuɓe lam. Senayee woodanii Alla! Mi wonaali jeyaaɗo e sirkooɓe ɓen
12|109|Men Nulaali ado maa si wanaa worɓe jeyaaɓe e yimɓe ca'e ɗen, Meɗen wahayina e maɓɓe. E ɓee [fennooɓe ma] yiilotaako ka leydi, ɓe ndaara ko honno battane ɓen adinooɓe ɓe wa'unoo? Pellet ko saare laakara nden ɓuri moƴƴannde ɓen huluɓe [Alla]. E on haqqiltaa
12|110|Haa si tawii Nulaaɓe ɓen taƴike, (heeferɓe ɓen) fellita wonnde kamɓe ɓe fennaama, ballal Amen ngal ara e maɓɓe; Men daɗnda on mo Men muuyi, lepte Amen ɗen ruttetaake gaayi e yimɓe bomɓe ɓen
12|111|Gomɗii wonii e fillayeeje maɓɓe ɗin tasakuyye wonannde joomiraaɓe haqqillaaji ɓen. Nde wonaali yewtere fefindaande. Ko woni, ko nde goonginnde ɗen adinooɗe nde, e fensitunde kala huunde, e peewal e yurmeende wonannde yimɓe gomɗimɓe ɓen
13|1|Alif, Laam, Miim, Raa. Ɗee ko Aayeeje Deftere nden; jippinaande nden e maaɗa immorde ka Joomi maa ko goonga; kono ko ɓuri ɗuuɗude e yimɓe ɓen ɓe gomɗintaa
13|2|Ko Alla woni ɓamtuɗo kammuuli ɗin doose ɗe on yi'ataa. Refti O fotondiri ka dow 'Arshi, O elti naange ngen e lewru ndun: kala majji no doga haa e lajal innaangal. Hino toppitoo fiyaakuuji ɗin, Himo fensita Aayeeje ɗen belajo'o on yananay hawroygol e Joomi mon. @Corrected
13|3|Ko Kanko woni fontuɗo leydi ndin, O waɗi e majji pelle e canɗi. E kala (noone) e dimɗe, O waɗi e majje noone ɗiɗi resindirayɗi. Himo suddira jemma on ñalorma on. Wonii e ɗum, maandeeji wonannde yimɓe miijitotooɓe
13|4|Hino ka leydi tummbe ɓadondirɗe, e gese 'inabu, e remuruuji, e tamarooje dukkinɗe e ɗe wonaa ɗukkinɗe, hiɗe yarniree ndiyam gootam, Meɗe ɓurna yoga majji dow yoga ka dakamme. Wonii e ɗum, maandeeji wonannde yimɓe haqqilooɓe
13|5|Si a ŋalɗay, haray ko konngol maɓɓe ngol jojji ŋalɗude: "Eyoo si men wontii mbulmbuldi, mene men wontay e tagu hesu?" Ko ɓen woni yedduɓe Joomi mun ɓen, ko ɓen tonngoytee ka daaɗe mun, ko ɓen kadi woni yimɓe Yiite; kamɓe ko ɓe luttooɓe e magge
13|6|Hiɓe hawjirane bone on ado moƴƴere nden. Gomɗii wulike ado maɓɓe [lepte] yeruuje majje. Pellet, Joomi maa ko Jom-haforanal wonannde yimɓe ɓen, e tooñe maɓɓe ɗen. Pellet kadi Joomi maa, ko sattuɗo lepte
13|7|Ɓen heefereɓe no wi'a: "Ko haɗno maande jippiniree e makko immorde ka Joomi makko?" Anndu ko an ko a jertinoowo, hino woodani yimɓe kala fewnoowo
13|8|Alla no anndi ko ronndotoo kala deyel, e ko renngaaji ɗin ustata e ko ɗi ɓeydata. Kala huunde ka Makko, ko eɓɓaa-ɗum
13|9|Annduɗo wirniiɗi e feeñuɗi, Mawɗo, Townitiiɗo
13|10|Hino fota [ka Makko anndugol] on suuɗuɗo konngol e mooɗon, e on feññinɗo ngol, on suuɗirayɗo jemma, e on yaltiniroowo ñalorma
13|11|Hino woodani mo lontondirooɓe yeeso makko e ɓaawo makko, hiɓe reenira mo yamiroore Alla. Pellet Alla waylataa ko woni e yimɓe, haa ɓe wayla ko woni kon e maɓɓe. Si Alla faandanike yimɓe bone, alaa yiltoowo mo. Alanaa ɓe gaanin Makko giɗo-heftoowo
13|12|Ko Kanko woni hollirayɗo on maƴe ɗen hulugol [ɗe] e tamƴinagol [toɓo]; O fuɗɗa ɗen duule tedduɗe
13|13|Digge ɗen no senina Mo yettugol Mo, e Malaa'ikaaɓe ɓen, immorde e kulol Makko. O wurta parñite ɗen, O meminira ɗe on Mo O muuyi. Kamɓe hiɓe wennja fii Alla, Kanko non ko O saɗtuɗo nanngal
13|14|Hino woodani Mo noddaandu goonga! Ɗin ɗi ɓe noddata ko woori Mo, ɗi jaabotaako ɓe e huunde; si wanaa wano fontuɗo newe mun e ndiyam fii yo ɗam yotto hunnduko makko, kono ɗam wonaali yottotoo-ɗam kon (hunnduko). Noddaandu heefereɓe ɓen wonaali si wanaa e majjere
13|15|Ko Alla woni ko sujjannta, denndaangal ko woni ka kammuuli e la leydi, ɗoftaare e waawneede, e ɗowdiiji maɓɓe, bimmbi e kiikiiɗe
13|16|Maaku: "Ko hommbo jeyi kammuuli ɗin e leydi ndin?" Maaku: "Ko Alla". Maaku: "E on jogiti gaanin Makko, heediiɗi ɗi waawanaa ko'e majji nafa wanaa lorra?" Maaku: "Hara bunɗo e yi'iiwo no fota? Kaa hara niɓe ɗen fotay e ndaygu ngu? Kaa ɓe waɗan Alla kafidiiɓe tagirɓe wano tagu Makko ngun, tagu ngun nanndani ɓe? Maaku: "Ko Alla woni taguɗo kala huunde, ko Kanko woni Bajjo, Fooluɗo
13|17|O jippinirii ka kammu ndiyam, ɗam ili e jooli emmbere majjam. Ilol ngol ronndii ngufo hummbu-ngo. No e kon ko ɓe huɓɓata yiite e mun fii ɗaɓɓu ɗaɓɓugol cuɗaari maa nafa-hoy, ngufo sugu mun. Ko wano nii Alla waɗirta misal goonga e fenannde. Si ko ngufo ngon, ngo yahray ɓeeɓugol, ammaa ko nafata yimɓe ɓen kon, ɗum ñiiɓa ka leydi. Ko wano nii Alla waɗirta mise ɗen
13|18|Hino woodani ɓen nootiiɓe Joomi mun moƴƴere. Ɓen ɓe nootaaki Mo, sinno woodaniino ɓe denndaangal ko woni kon ka leydi, e yeru mun wonndude e mu'un, ɓe soktorayno(soottorto) ɗum. Ɓen ɗon, no woodani ɓe bonɗum hasboore, jaaƴorde maɓɓe nden ko Jahannama. Nge bonii ndaɗɗundi
13|19|E ko on annduɗo wonnde ko jippinaa kon e maaɗa immorde ka Joomi maa ko goonga, wa'ata wa on ɓunɗo? Anndu ko waajitotoo, ko joomiraaɓe-haqqillaaji ɓen
13|20|ɓen hunnooɓe ahadi Alla ndin, ɓe firtataa ahodal(hoolaare)
13|21|e ɓen jokkooɓe kon ko Alla yamiri yo jokke, hiɓe hula Joomi maɓɓe, hiɓe hula bonnde hasboore
13|22|ɓen muññoriiɓe ɗaɓɓugol yarluyee Joomi maɓɓe, ɓe ñiiɓni julde, ɓe nafqii e kon ko Men arsiki ɓe, gunndoo e kene, hiɓe duñira moƴƴere nden bone on. Ɓen ɗon, no woodani ɓe battane galle
13|23|Aljannaaji ñiiɓal, hiɓe naata ɗi, e ɓen moƴƴuɓe e baabiraaɓe maɓɓe ɓen, e rewɓe maɓɓe ɓen, e geyngolji maɓɓe ɗin. Hara Malaa'ikaaɓe ɓen hino naatirana ɓe kala damal
13|24|Kisal wonii e mo'on, sabu muñal mon ngal. Battane galle ɗen moƴƴii
13|25|Ɓen (non) firtooɓe ahadi Alla ndin ɓaawo fiɓugol ndi, hiɓe taƴoo e ko Alla yamiri kon yo jokke, hiɓe bonna ka leydi, ɓe ɗon, hino woodani ɓe kuɗdi, hino woodani ɓe kadi bonɗum galle
13|26|Alla no yaññana arsike on Mo O muuyi, Himo ɓittina. Hiɓe weltora nguurndam aduna, nguurndam aduna non wonaali ka laakara, si wanaa dakamme-hoy
13|27|Ɓen yedduɓe no wi'a: "Ko haɗno Aaya jippinee e makko immorde ka Joomi makko?" Maaku: "Alla majjinay tun mo O muuyi, O fewna e Makko on tuubuɗo-ruttii
13|28|ɓen gomɗimɓe, ɓe ɓerɗe mun deeƴirta jantagol Alla. Anndee ko jantagol Alla ngol ɓerɗe ɗen deeƴirta
13|29|Ɓen gomɗimɓe ɓe golli golle moƴƴe, welo-welo woodaniiɓe e moƴƴude ruttorde
13|30|Ko wano nii Men nulir-maa e mofte - gomɗii mofte goo yawtiino ado majje - fii yo a janngan ɓe nden nde Men wahayini e maaɗa, kono hiɓe yedda Yurmeteeɗo On. Maaku: "Ko Kanko woni Joomi am. Reweteeɗo alaa si wanaa Kanko. Ko e Makko mi fawii, ko ka Makko kadi woni ruttorde am
13|31|Sinno janngeteende naɓirano pelle ɗen, maa leydi ndin seekiraa sabu mayre, maa nde wowliniraa maayɓe ɓen (harayno ko ndee ɗoo). Ko woni, ko Alla woodani fiyaaku on fow. E gomɗimɓe ɓen anndaali wonnde, sinno Alla muuyuno, O fewnayna denndaangal yimɓe ɓen? Masiibo seeraali no heɓira yedduɓe ɓen ko ɓe faggitii kon, maa [ngon masiibo] yana takko galle maɓɓe nden haa fodoore Alla nden ara. Pellet Alla firtataa fodoore
13|32|Gomɗii Nulaaɓe jalkitanoo ma ado maaɗa. Mi muññanii ɓen yedduɓe, refti Mi nanngi ɓe. Ko honno lepte Am ɗen wonirnoo
13|33|E hara ko On dariiɗo e kala wonkii ko ki faggitii kon [ɓuri hanndude e dewal?...] Ɓe waɗanii Alla kafidii- ɗi. Maaku: "Innee-ɗi" Kaa on humpitay Mo ko O anndaa ka leydi? Kaa ko ko [tun] e konngol? Ko woni, heeferɓe ɓen cuɗinanaa ma pewje maɓɓe ɗen, ɓe sakkaa(pala) e laawol ngol. Kala mo Alla majjini, fewnoowo alanaa mo
13|34|Hino woodani ɓe lepte ka nguurndam aduna. Pellet ko lepte laakara ɗen ɓuri sattude, alanaa ɓe daɗndoowo (ɓe) e Alla
13|35|Sugu Aljanna mo gomɗuɓe ɓen fodaa on: Canɗi no ila ley makko; ñaamɗi makko ɗin ko duumiiɗum, e ɗowdi makko ndin. Ɗum ko battane ɓen gomɗuɓe, battane heeferbe non ko Yiite
13|36|Ɓen ɓe Men okki Deftere nden, hiɓe weltora kon ko jippinaa e maaɗa. No e leƴƴi kon ɓen yeddooɓe yoga mayre. Maaku: "Anndee ko yamiraa-mi, ko nde reway-mi Alla hara mi sirkanaali Mo. Ko e Makko nodday-mi, ko ka Makko kadi woni ruttorde am
13|37|Ko wano nii Men jippiniri nde ñaawoore (e haala) aarabu. Pellet si a jokkii mbeleeɗe maɓɓe ɗen ɓaawo nde ganndal ari e maa, alanaa ma gaanin Alla immorde e giɗo, wanaa daɗndoowo
13|38|Gomɗii Men nulii Nulaaɓe ado maa, Men waɗani ɓe genndiraaɓe e geyngol. Haananaa Nulaaɗo nde o addata Aaya, si wanaa e sakkitoore Alla. Hino woodani kala lajal caati
13|39|Alla no meha ko O Muuyi O tabatina (ko O wela), ko ka Makko yumma defte ɗen woni
13|40|Si Men holliima yogo e ko Men fodi ɓe, maa Men hunnu maa (ado mun), anndu ko fawi maa ko yottingol, haasboore nde ko Menen fawtii
13|41|E ɓee yi'aali wonnde Meɗen ara e leydi ndin, Men ɗuytira ndi ka seraaji mayri? Alla no ñaawa, alaa wurtinoowo ñaawoore Makko nden, ko O yacciiɗo ñaawoore
13|42|Gomɗii ɓen adinooɓe ɓe fewjaniino (Annabaaɓe maɓɓe); ko Alla non pewje ɗen fow heeranii. Himo anndi kala wonkii faggitotoo. Arma heefereɓe ɓen annda ko hommbo battane galle (moƴƴe) woodani
13|43|Heeferɓe ɓen hino wi'a: "Wanaa a Nulaaɗo". Maaku: "Alla yonii seedee hakkunde am e mon, e ɓen jogitiiɓe ganndal Deftere nden
14|1|Alif, Laam, Raa. (Ndee ko) Deftere nde Men jippini e maaɗa, fii yo yaltinir yimɓe ɓen e niɓe faade e annoora, e duŋayee Joomi maɓɓe, haa e laawol Fooluɗo, Yettiniiɗo
14|2|Alla, On Mo woodani kala ko woni kammuuli e ka leydi. Bone woodani yedduɓe ɓen, immorde e lepte sattuɗe
14|3|Ɓen ɓurdinooɓe nguurndam aduna ɗam e dow laakara, ɓe faddoo e laawol Alla ngol, ɓe ɗaɓɓana ngol ooñorgal. Ɓen ɗow wonii e majjere woɗɗunde
14|4|Men nuliraali Nulaaɗo (woo), si wanaa e ɗemngal yimɓe makko ɓen, fii no o ɓannginirana ɓe. Alla no majjina on Mo muuyi, O fewna on Mo O muuyi. Ko Kanko woni Fooluɗo, Ñeeñuɗo
14|5|Gomɗii Men nulirii Muusaa Aayeeje Amen ɗen [wi'ugol Mo]: "Yaltin yimɓe maa ɓen e niɓe faade e annoora, anndintinaa ɓe ñalɗi Alla ɗin". Pellet hino e ɗum, tasakuyeeji kala munyoowo, yettoowo (neema)
14|6|(Janto) tuma nde Muusaa maakannoo yimɓe makko ɓen: "siftoree neema Alla on e mooɗon, tuma O daɗndunoo on e yimɓe Fir'awna ɓe no defaynoo on lepte bonɗe. Hiɓe hirsa ɓiɗɓe mon (worɓe) ɓe acca (ɓiɗɓe) mon rewɓe. Wonii e ɗum mo'on, jarrabuyee mawɗo immorde ka Joomi mon
14|7|e tuma nde Joomi maa anndinnoo: "Pellet si on yettii, ma Mi ɓeydan on. Si on yeddii non, pellet lepte am ɗen ko saɗtuɗe
14|8|Muusaa maaki: "Si on yeddii, onon e wonɓe ka leydi ɓen fow, [anndon] pellet Alla ko Galo Yettiniiɗo
14|9|E kumpite ɓen adinooɓe on araali on, yimɓe Nuuhu e Aadi, e Samuuda e ɓen wonunooɓe ɓaawo maɓ- ɓe, anndaa ɓe si wanaa Alla? Nulaaɓe maɓɓe ɓen addanii ɓe ɓanngannduyeeji, ɓe rutti juuɗe maɓɓe ɗen ka kunndule maɓɓe, ɓe wi'i: "Menen men yed- dii ko nulidaɗon e mun kon, menen, meɗen e sikkitii e ko noddoton men e mun sikkitiiɓe
14|10|Nulaaɓe maɓɓe ɓen maaki: "E hara sikke no e fii Alla, fuɗɗuɗo kammuuli ɗin e leydi ndin, himo nodda on fii yo O haforan on yoga e junuubi mon, himo nennana on haa e lajal innaangal?" Ɓe wi'i: "On wonaali si wanaa ɓanndinke yeru amen. Hiɗon faandii nde sakkotoɗon(falotodon) men e kon ko baabiraaɓe amen rewaynoo. Addanee men hujja ɓannguɗo
14|11|Nulaaɓe maɓɓe ɓen maakani ɓe: "[Ko goonga], men wonaali si wanaa ɓanndinke yeru mon, kono Alla no moƴƴoo e Mo O muuyi e jeyaaɓe Makko ɓen. Laatanaaki men nde men addana on hujja, si wanaa e duŋayee Alla. Ko e Alla gomɗimɓe ɓen fawotoo
14|12|Ko haɗata men nde fawotoo e Alla, gomɗii O fewnii men (e) laawi amen? Ma men muñño e kon ko lorroton men. Ko e Alla gomɗimɓe ɓen fawotoo
14|13|Ɓen yedduɓe (kadi) wi'ani Nulaaɓe mun ɓen: "Ma men yaltin on ka leydi amen, maa ruttoɗon e diina amen". Joomi maɓɓe wahayini e maɓɓe: "Ma men halku tooñuɓe ɓen
14|14|Ma Men hoɗnu on e leydi ndin ɓaawo maɓɓe. Ɗum ko wonannde on huluɗo daroyagol yeeso Am, o huli kammbaa Am on
14|15|Ɓe ɗaɓɓi uddital. Sooyi kala dunndaranke ƴagguɗo
14|16|Jahannama no yesso makko, himo yarniree ndiyam mbordi ƴiiƴiiri
14|17|himo wooɓa ɗam, e ɗeɓataa ɓennugol ɗam. Maayde nden ardana mo e kala nokku, kono o wonaali maayoowo. Hara no yeeso makko lepte sattuɗe
14|18|Ko woni sifa ɓen yedduɓe Joomi mun, kuuɗe maɓɓe ɗen, ko wano ndoondi ndi henndu tiiɗi e mun, e ñalaande wippoore. Ɓe hettoytaa huunde e ko ɓe faggitinoo. Ko ɗum woni majjere wonɗɗunde
14|19|E a yi'aali Alla tagirii kammuuli ɗin e leydi ndin goonga? Si O muuyii, O ittay on O adda tagu hesu
14|20|ɗum wonaali sattuɗum ka Alla
14|21|Ɓe feeñana Alla ɓe denndaangal. Lo'uɓe ɓen wi'ana townitinooɓe ɓen: "Menen men wonanno on jokkuɓe. Taw si on duncanay men e lepte Alla ɗen goɗɗum?" Ɓen wi'a: "Sinno Alla fewnuno men, men fewnayno on. Hino fota e amen, si en ɗenƴi maa si en muññi; daɗirde alanaa en
14|22|Seytaane wi'a, tuma fiyaaku on ñaawaa: "Pellet Alla fodiino on fodoore goonga; mi fodi on mi lunndii on. Alanaa lam e mo'on immorde e hujja, si wanaa mi nodii on, on jaabike lam. Wata on felam; felee ko'e mon. Wanaa mi faabotooɗo on; wanaa on faabotooɓe lam. Mi yeddii ko kafidunoɗon mi kon [e Alla] ado (hannde)". Pellet, tooñooɓe ɓen, hino woodani ɓe lepte muusuɗe
14|23|Gomɗimɓe golli moƴƴuɗi ɓen naatnaa e Aljannaaji, canɗi hino ila ley majji, ko ɓe duumorayɓe ton e duŋayee Joomi maɓɓe. Hiwraandu maɓɓe ndun ton ko: "Salaam" (Kisiyee). @Corrected
14|24|E a yi'aali ko honno Alla piyiri misal konngol laaɓungol, ko wano leggal welngal, binndeere maggal ko tabituɗi, calɗi maggal no ka weeyo
14|25|Hingal okkira dimɗe maggal on tuma kala, e duŋayee Joomi maggal. Alla no piyana yimɓe ɓen mise, belajo'o ɓe waajitoto
14|26|Ko woni kadi misal konngol soɓungol, ko wano leggal soɓungal, irtaangal ka hoore-leydi, ngal alanaa ɗum ñiiɓirde
14|27|Alla no tabintinira gomɗimɓe ɓen konngol tabitungol, ka nguurandam aduna e ka laakara. Alla no majjina tooñooɓe ɓen. Alla no waɗa ko O muuyi
14|28|E a tinaali ɓen waɗtitirɓe neemaaji Alla ɗin keeferaaku, ɓe weerni yimɓe ɓen galle halkaare
14|29|Jahannama, hiɓe naata nge, nge bonii ñiiɓirde
14|30|Ɓe waɗani Alla yerondiraaɗi fii yo ɓe majjin (yimɓe ɓen) e laawol Alla ngol. Maaku: "Dakmitee, pellet ruttorde mon nden ko ka Yiite
14|31|Maakan jeyaaɓe am gomɗimɓe ɓen, yo ɓe ñinnu julde ɓe wintoo e kon ko Men arsiki ɓe gunndoo e kene, ado nde arata ɓe ñalaande nde jgeeygu alaa e mun wanaa weldigal
14|32|Ko Alla woni taguɗo kammuuli ɗin e leydi, O jippiniri ka kammu ndiyam; O yaltiniri ɗam dimɗe arsike wonannde on. O eltirani on laaɗe ɗen, fii yo ɗe dogir ka maayo e duŋayee Makko. O eltani on kadi canɗi ɗin
14|33|O eltani on naange ngen e lewru ndun dogooji ɗiɗi. O eltani on jemma on e ñalorma on
14|34|O okki on e kala ko toriɗon Mo. Si on lintii neemaaji Alla ɗin, on moftataaɗi. Pellet neɗɗanke on ko hee- wuɗo tooñe, heewuɗo yeddugol
14|35|(Janto) kadi tuma nde Ibraahiima maakunoo: "Joomi am, waɗu ndee saare hooliinde, daɗndaa lam e ɓiɗɓe am ɓen nde men rewata sanamuuji
14|36|Joomi am, kannji (sanamuuji ɗin), ɗi majjinii ko ɗuuɗi e yimɓe ɓen. Kala jokkuɗo lam, on ɗon ko jeyidaaɗo e am. Kala non yedduɗo lam, haray An ko A Haforoowo, Hinnotooɗo
14|37|Joomi amen, min mi hoɗinii yoga e ɓiɗɓe am ɓen e aynde nde wonaa remotoonde, ka Suudu Maa Hormanteeru, - Joomi amen - fii yo ɓe ñinnu julde. Waɗu ɓerɗe yimɓe ɓen no yiiloo e maɓɓe, arsikaaɓe dimɗe, belajo'o ɓe yetta
14|38|Joomi amen, pellet, An hiɗa anndi ko men suuɗi e ko men feññini: hay huunde suuɗotaako Alla ka leydi wanaa ka kammu
14|39|Yettoore woodanii Alla, On yeɗuɗo lam e hoore mawngu, Ismaa'iila e Ishaaqa. Pellet, Joomi am ko nanoowo du'aa
14|40|Joomi am, waɗan ñinnoowo julde e ɓeynugol am ngol. Joomi amen, jaɓu toraare am nden
14|41|Joomi amen, haforanam min e jibimɓe lam ɓen e gomɗimɓe ɓen, ñalnde ñaawoore nden dorotoo
14|42|Wata sikku Alla ko welsindiiɗo e ko tooñooɓe ɓen huuwata. Anndu ko O nenniranta ɓe, ko haa e ñalaande nde gite saafotoo e mun
14|43|Ko ɓe heñiiɓe, ŋallimɓe ko'e maɓɓe, ndaarɗe maɓɓe ɗen yiltotaako e maɓɓe, ɓerɗe maɓɓe ɗen ko yeewuɗe
14|44|Jertniri yimɓe ɓen ñalaande nde lepte ɗen arata ɓe, tooñuɓe ɓen wi'a: "Joomi amen, nennan men haa lajal ɓaɗiingal, men nootoo noddaanndu Maa, men jokka Nulaaɓe ɓen". E on laatanooki on woondiino ado (hannde) alanaa on iwugol (ton)
14|45|Hoɗuɗon e koɗooli ɓen tooñuɓe ko'e mun. Ɓanngani on ko honno Men huuwunoo ɓe, Men piyani on mise
14|46|Gomɗii ɓe fewjii feere maɓɓe nden. Ko ka Alla feere maɓɓe nden woni, hay si feere maɓɓe nden ittayno pelle ɗen
14|47|Wata a sikku Alla ko lunndotooɗo fodoore Makko (nde O fodi) Nulaaɓe Makko ɓen. Pellet, Alla ko Fooluɗo, Jom yottagol
14|48|ñalnde leydi ndin waɗtitirtee leydi goo, e kammuuli ɗin, ɓe feeñana Alla, Bajjo On, Fooluɗo On
14|49|A yi'ay bomɓe ɓen nden ñalnde, ko jokkindiraaɓe e kolombooje
14|50|Dolokkaaji maɓɓe ɗin ko mbullam feewnira, Yiite ngen no sudda geece maɓɓe ɗen
14|51|Fii yo Alla yoɓitu kala wonkii ko ko faggitii. Pellet, Alla ko yaawuɗo hasboore
14|52|Ndee (Alqur'aanaare) ko yottinoore yimɓe ɓen fii yo ɓe waajitornde, e yoɓe anndu kadi, wonnde Kanko ko O reweteeɗo Gooto, e fii yo joomiraaɓe haqqillaaji ɓen waajitor
15|1|Alif, laam, raa. Ɗen ko Aayeeje Deftere e janngeteende ɓannginnde
15|2|Na waawi Heeferɓe ɓen yeloyto sinno ɓe laatino juulɓe
15|3|Accu ɓe, ɓe ñaama ɓe dakmitoo, yela soklina ɓe; arma ɓe anndoya
15|4|Men halkaali saare woo, si wanaa hara no woodani nde happu anndaaɗo
15|5|Mofte woo adotaako lajal mun, ɓe nennantaake kadi
15|6|Ɓe wi'i: "Ko an yo mo Deftere nden jippinaa e mun, an ko a feetuɗo
15|7|Ko haɗno addanaa men Malaa'ikaaɓe, si a laatike goonguɗo
15|8|Men jippinirtaa Malaa'ika si wanaa fii goonga; ɓe wonataa ontuma, nennanteeɓe
15|9|Menen Men jippinii Deftere nden, Menen kadi ko Men reenooɓe nde
15|10|Gomɗii Men nuliino ado maa, e leñi adinooɓe
15|11|Nulaaɗo (woo) araali e maɓɓe si wanaa ɓe jalkitay mo
15|12|Ko wano nii Men naadiri ɗum e ɓerɗe bonɓe ɓen
15|13|Ɓe gomɗintaa nde, gomɗii sunna aramɓe ɓen yawtiino
15|14|Hay si Men udditanno ɓe damal ka kammu, ɓe waɗtini hiɓe ƴawra heen
15|15|ɓe wi'ayno: "Anndee gite amen ɗen hippa. Wurin ko men yimɓe mbilɗaaɓe
15|16|Gomɗii Men waɗii ka kammu koode, Men cuɗirani ɗe ndaarooɓe
15|17|Men reeni mbo e kala seytaane riiwaaɗo
15|18|Si wanaa on wujjuɗo nanɗe, o jokkintina hoodere-fiɗaynnde jalɓunde
15|19|Leydi ndin, Men weerti ndi Men werlii e mayri pelle, Men fuɗini e mayri kala huunde eɓɓaande
15|20|Men waɗani on e mayri wuurirɗe, e ɓen ɓe on laatanooki arsikooɓe ɗum
15|21|Huunde alaa si wanaa marga mun ko ka Amen, Men jippintaa ɗum si wanaa e eɓɓoore anndaande
15|22|Men wurti keneeli ɗin hawrondirooji e duule; Men jippiniri ka kammu ndiyam Men yarniri on ɗam, wonaa onon mari ɗam
15|23|Ko Menen kadi woni ko wuurnata Men wara, ko Menen woni ronooɓe ɓen
15|24|Gomɗii Men anndii adiiɓe e mon ɓen Gomɗii Men anndii sakkitiiɓe ɓen
15|25|Pellet, Joomi maa, ko Kanko mooɓoyta ɓe. Kanko ko O Ñeeño, Annduɗo
15|26|Gomɗii Men tagii neɗɗanke on e senƴayngal, e (cenlatngal) loopal-ɓalewal ɓowrungal
15|27|E jinnaaji ɗin, Men tagir ndu ko adii, e yiite ooyunge
15|28|Janto tuma nde Joomi maa daalannoo Malaa'ika'en: "Min ko Mi tagiroowo ɓanndinke immorde e senƴayngal, e loopal-ɓalewal ɓowrungal
15|29|si Mi fotndiii mo, Mi wuttii e makko ruuhu Am on, haray suuyanee mo ko on sujjuɓe
15|30|Malaa'ika'en fow sujji ɓe denndaangal
15|31|si wanaa ibuliisa, o salii tawdeede e sujjooɓe ɓen
15|32|O daali: "Ko an yo Ibuliisa, e ko heɓu maa a laatodaaki e sujjuɓe ɓen
15|33|O wi'i: "Mi wonatah sujjanoowo ɓanndinke mo Taguɗaa immorde e senƴayngal, e loopal-ɓalewal ɓowrungal
15|34|O daali: "Yaltu ton, an on ko a riiwaaɗo
15|35|pellet, kuddi fawike e ma haa ñalnde njoɓdi diina
15|36|O wi'i : "Joomi am, nennitanam haa ñalnde ndeɓe immintintee
15|37|O daali:"An,ko a jeyaaɗo e nennitanteeɓe ɓen
15|38|haa e ñalaande happu anndaaɗo
15|39|O wi'i: "Joomi am, sabu ko bewinɗaa mi kon, ma mi cuɗinan ɓe ka leydi, ma mi bewnu ɓe fow maɓɓe
15|40|si wanaa jeyaaɓe Maa, laɓɓinaaɓe ɓen e maɓɓe
15|41|O daali: "Ngol ɗoo ko laawol ka Am focciingol
15|42|Pellet, jeyaaɓe Am ɓen, a alanaa ɓe cemmbe, si wanaa ɓen bewɓe jokkuɓe ma
15|43|Pellet Jahannama on wonii fodoore maɓɓe ɓe fow
15|44|Hinge mari dame jeeɗiɗi; damal kala e majje no mari geɓal senndaangal
15|45|Pellet, gomɗuɓe ɓen wonii e aljannaaji e ɓulli
15|46|Naatiree ɗi e kisial, ko on hooliiɓe
15|47|Men ɗoofi kala ko woni e ɓerɗe maɓɓe e konnaagu(cokotaagal): ɓe wonti musiɗɓe fewtondirɓe e danɗe
15|48|Tampere heɓataa ɓe ton, ɓe wonah kadi yaltintee ɓe ton
15|49|Yeetito jeyaaɓe Am ɓen, ko Min woni Haforoowo, Hinnotooɗo On
15|50|e wonnde lepte Am ɗen, ko ɗen woni lepte muusuɗe ɗen
15|51|Yeetito ɓe kadi fii hoɓɓe Ibraahiima ɓen
15|52|Tuma ɓe naatunoo ka makko ɓe wi'i: "Salaam (Kisiyee mon)". O maaki: "Menen ko men ɗenƴii ɓe on
15|53|Ɓe wi'i: "Wata a faay, menen meɗen wewlinire [ɓiɗɗo] gorko ganndo
15|54|O maaki: "E on wewliniray lam [ɗum] e hoore ko mi nawyi kon? E ko wewlinirton mi
15|55|Ɓe wi'i: "Men wewlinirii ma goonga, wata a jeye e taƴiiɓe ɓen
15|56|O maaki: "Ko hommbo taƴotoo e yurmeende Joomi mun nden, si wanaa majjuɓe ɓen
15|57|O maaki: "Ko woni fii mon, onon ɓee imminaaɓe
15|58|Ɓe wi'i: "Menen men nulaa ko e yimɓe bomɓe
15|59|si wanaa ɓeynguure Luuti nden, pellet ko men daɗndooɓe ɓe denndaangal
15|60|si wanaa debbo makko on". Men hoddirii on ɗon ko jeyaaɗo e halketeeɓe ɓen
15|61|Nde imminaaɓe ɓen aruno ka ɓeynguure Luuti
15|62|O maaki: "Onon ko on yimɓe faaytaa ɓe
15|63|Ɓe wi'i: "Wurin men addanii ma ko ɓe wonunoo e sikkitaade kon
15|64|Men addanii ma goonga kan, pellet ko men goonguɓe
15|65|Yahdu e ɓeynguure maa nden ka taƴitannde jem- ma, jokkaa ɓaawo maɓɓe; hara gooto e mo'on yeƴƴitaaki, rewon ka yamiraɗon
15|66|Men anndini mo on fiyaaku: wonnde wattannde ɓee ɗoo, ko taƴeteeɗum ka subaka
15|67|Yimɓe saare nden ari hiɓe wewla
15|68|O maaki: "Ɓee ɗoo ko hoɓɓe am, wata on wirtam
15|69|Hulee Alla, wata on hoynam
15|70|Ɓe wi'i: "E men haɗaali ma [weernugol] tagoore nden
15|71|O maaki: "Ɓee ɗoo ko jiwɓe am, si wonii ko on waɗooɓe [goɗɗum]
15|72|Mi woondirii nguurndam maa! Ɓe wonii e siwrugol maɓɓe hiɓe wemmbii
15|73|Haacaango ngon nanngiri ɓe ka puɗal
15|74|Men waɗtiniri dow mayre on ley mayre, Men saaƴini(toɓri) e maɓɓe kaaƴe iwruɗe e loope juɗaaɗe
15|75|Wonii e ɗum, maandeeji wonannde ɓen teskotooɓe
15|76|Pellet, ɗen [ca'e] no e jurol(bolol) ñiiɓungol
15|77|Wonii e ɗum, maande wonannde ɓen gomɗimɓe
15|78|Gomɗii yimɓe fitaare(sutu) ɓen [kadi] ko tooñuɓe
15|79|Men yoɓtii e maɓɓe. Pellet ɗen [ca'e] ɗiɗi wonii e laawol ɓanngungol
15|80|Gomɗi yimɓe (aynde) Hijiri nden fennii Nulaaɓe ɓen
15|81|Men addani ɓe aayeeje Amen ɗen, ɓe laatii ɗuurniiɓe ɗe
15|82|Hari hiɓe lesoynoo e pelle ɗen cuuɗi, ko ɓe hooliiɓe
15|83|Haacaango ngon nanngiri ɓe ka subaka
15|84|Nafaaniɓe kon ko ɓe laatinoo hiɓe faggitoo
15|85|Men tagiraali kammuuli ɗin e leydi ndin, e ko woni hakkunde majji kon, si wanaa e goonga. Pellet, darngal ngal ko arayngal! yaafora jaafaggol labaangol
15|86|Tabitii ko Joomi maa woni Taguɗo, Annduɗo
15|87|Gomɗii Men okkii ma jeeɗiɗi ummorde ɗimmitaa-ngol, e Alqur'aanaare mawnde nden
15|88|Wata a ɓamtu gite maa ɗen e neemaaji ɗi Men dakmiti ɓe e mum en, wata a sunu e maɓɓe, lesɗin becce maa ɗen gomɗimɓe ɓen
15|89|Maaku: "Min ko mi jertinoowo ɓannginoowo
15|90|Wano Men jippinirnoo e senndooɓe [defte Alla] ɓen [lepte]
15|91|Ɓen waɗuɓe Alqur'aanaare nden geɓe-geɓe
15|92|Mi woondirii Joomi maa! Ma Men lanndoyo ɓe fow maɓɓe
15|93|fii ko ɓe wonunoo e huuwude
15|94|Feññin ko yamira-ɗaa kon, ɗuurno-ɗaa sirkooɓe ɓen
15|95|Menen Men yonii ma e ɓen jalkitooɓe
15|96|ɓen waɗdooɓe e Alla reweteeɗo goo. Aray ka ɓe annda
15|97|Gomɗii Meɗen anndi wonnde bernde maa nde na ɓiɗtora ko ɓe wowlata kon
15|98|Subbhinor yettugol Joomi maa, laato-daa e sujjooɓe ɓen
15|99|rewaa Joomi haa yananeede (maayde) ara e maa
16|1|Yamiroore Alla nden ɓadike, wata on hawjan nde. Senayee woodanii Mo! O toowii e ko ɓe sirkata
16|2|Himo jippinira Malaa'ikaaɓe ɓen e wayhu on e yamiroore Makko, dow mo O muuyi e jeyaaɓe Makko ɓen, wonnde : "Jertinree wiide reweteeɗo alaa si wanaa Min. Hulee Lam
16|3|O tagiri kammuuli ɗin e leydi ndin goonga. O toowii e ko ɓe sirkoobe sirkata ko
16|4|O tagiri neɗɗanke iwde e toɓɓere (maniiyu); jaka yoo kanko ko wennjoowo ɓannguɗo
16|5|Neemoraaɗi ɗin, O tagani on ɗi; no e majji nguli nugguki e nafaaji. Ko e majji kadi ñaamoton
16|6|Hino woodani on e majji cuɗaari, tuma njofnoton ɗi e tuma oornoton ɗi
16|7|Hiɗi ronndoo donle mon naɓa e leydi ndi on yotto- tanooko si wanaa e tampere pittaali. Pellet, Joomi mon ko O Yurmeteeɗo Hinnotooɗo
16|8|E pucci, e mbam-pucci, e mbabbi, fii yo on waɗɗo ɗi, e cuɗaari. Himo taga kadi ko on anndaa
16|9|Ko Alla woodani ɓanngingol laawol focciingol ngol, no e majji ngol feewaani. Si O muuyuno, O fewnay on denndaangal
16|10|Ko Kanko woni jippinirɗo ndiyam ka kammu, hino woodani on e majjam njaram, leɗɗe no (yalta) e majjam, ko e majjam kadi oornoton
16|11|Himo fuɗnirana on ɗam aawruuji, nebbanteeje, e tamarooje, e inabuuje, e kala dimɗe. Wonii e ɗum, tasakuyee wonannde yimɓe miijitotooɓe
16|12|O eltani on jemma on e ñaloma on; naange ngen e lewru ndun. Koode ɗen kadi ko eltiraaɗe yamiroore Makko. Wonii e ɗum, tasakuyeeji wonannde yimɓe haqqilooɓe
16|13|E ko O tagani on kon ka leydi sertuɗum nooneeji. Wonii e ɗum, tasakuyee wonannde yimɓe waajitorayɓe
16|14|Ko Kanko woni eltanɗo on maayo ngon fii yo on ñaamu e maggo teewu keccu, yaltinon e maggo cuɗaari ndi ɓornotoɗon. A yi'ay laaɗe no feƴƴa e maggo, e fii yo on ɗaɓɓu e ɓural Makko ngal, belajo'o, on yettay [Mo]
16|15|O tuti penle ka leydi fii wata ɗe dillidu e mo'on, e canɗi, e ɗate, belajo'o on feeway
16|16|e maandeeji [laawi]. Koode ɗen hiɓe ɗowora ɗe
16|17|E hara tagoowo on wa'ay wa on tagataa? E on waajitotaako
16|18|Si on lintii neemaaji Alla ɗin, on moftataa ɗi. Pellet, Alla ko Haforoowo, Hinnotooɗo
16|19|Alla no anndi ko suuɗoton e ko feññinton
16|20|Ɗin ɗi ɓe rewata gaanin Alla, ɗi tagataa hay huunde, kannji tigi ko ɗi tageteeɗi
16|21|Koɗi maayuɗi ɗi wuuraa, ɓe so'aa-anndude nde ɓe immintintee
16|22|Reweteeɗo mon on ko Reweteeɗo gooto. Ɓen ɓe gomɗinaa laakara, ɓerɗe maɓɓe ɗen ko yedduɗe, ɓen ko townitiiɓe
16|23|Sikke alaa wonnde Alla no anndi ko ɓe suuɗata e ko ɓe feññinta. Kanko O yiɗaa townitiiɓe ɓen
16|24|Si ɓe wi'anaama : "Ko honɗum Joomi mon jippini?" Ɓe wi'a: "Ko tinndi adinooɓe
16|25|Fii yo ɓe ronndo bakkaatuuji maɓɓe ɗin fow Ñalnde Darngal, e bakkaatuuji ɓen ɓe majjinirta ko aldaa e ganndal; anndee bonii ko ɓe ronndoytoo
16|26|Gomɗii ɓen adinooɓe ɓe fewjiino, Alla yirbiniri mahdeele maɓɓe ɗen ka doose. Kippoodi ndin yanti e maɓɓe, lepte ɗen ardirani ɓe nokku ka ɓe so'aa-aanndude
16|27|Refti Ñalnde Darngal, O hoynoyayɓe, O wi'anaɓe: Ko honto kafidaaɗi am ɗin ɗi haɓiraynoɗon fii mun?" Ɓen okkaaɓe ganndal wi'a: "Koyeera on hannde e bone on wonii e heeferɓe ɓen
16|28|Ɓen ɓen Malaa'ikaaɓe ɓen hunnata, tooñuɓe ko'e-mun, ɓe werloo jebbilraare, (ɓe wi'a): "Men wonaa- no gollatnooɓe ko boni!" -"Wonaa non woniri, pellet Alla ko annduɗo ko huuwaynoɗon
16|29|Naatiree dame Jahannama ɗen luttugol ton. Nge bonii ñaaƴorde wonande townitiiɓe ɓen
16|30|Wi'anee ɓen gomɗuɓe: "Ko honɗum Joomi mon jippini?" Ɓe wi'a: "Ko moƴƴere". Hino woodani ɓen moƴƴimɓe aduna ɗoo moƴƴere; pellet ko saare laakara nden ɓuri moƴƴude. Nde moƴƴii saare gomɗuɓe ɓen
16|31|Aljannaaji duumal, hiɓe naati ɗi, canɗi no ila ley majji. Hino woodani ɓe ton kala ko ɓe faaletee; ko wano nii Alla yoɓirta gomɗuɓe ɓen. @Corrected
16|32|Ɓen ɓe Malaa'ikaaɓe ɓen warta hara ko ɓe laaɓuɓe- ɓe wi'an [ɓen]: "Kisiyee wonii e mon! Naatiree Aljanna on, sabu ko gollaynoɗon kon
16|33|Hara [ɓee sirkooɓe fenna] hino habbitii si wanaa nde Malaa'ikaaɓe ɓen arata e maɓɓe, maa yami- roore Joomi maa nden ara? Ko wano non ɓen adinooɓe ɓe waɗirnoo. Alla tooñaali ɓe; si ko woni, ko ko'e maɓɓe ɓe wonunoo e tooñuɓe
16|34|Boneeji ɗi ɓe huuwi ɗin memi ɓen, kon ko ɓe jalkitaynoo jippii e maɓɓe
16|35|Ɓen sirkuɓe wi'i: "Sinno Alla muuyuno, men rewataano gaanin Makko hay huunde, wanaa menen wanaa baabiraaɓe amen; men harmintaa- no gaanin Makko hay huunde". Ko wano non adi- nooɓe ɓen gerdunoo. Taw si no fawiiii Nulaaɓe ɓen si wanaa yottingol ɓanngina
16|36|Gomɗii Men imminii e kala mofte Nulaaɗo, wonnde rewee Alla, woɗɗitoɗon bewnayɗi ɗin. Hino e maɓɓe on Mo Alla fewni, hino e maɓɓe kadi on mo majjere nden jojji e mun. Yiilee ka leydi, ndaaron ko honno battane fennooɓe ɓen wa'unoo
16|37|Si a rerɗii e peewal maɓɓe, [anndu] pellet, Alla fewnataa on Mo o majjini, alanaa ɓe kadi wallooɓe
16|38|Ɓe woondirii Alla haɗtirde goondooje maɓɓe: "Alla immintintaa on maayuɗo". Wanaa non! Ɗum ko fodoore goonga ka Makko, ko woni tun, ko ɓuri ɗuuɗude e yimɓe ɓe anndaa
16|39|(O immintiniroyay ɓe) fii yo O ɓannginan ɓe ko ɓe luutondiraynoo e mun, e fii yo ɓen yedduɓe anndu wonnde hari ko ɓe fenooɓe
16|40|Anndee daalol Amen wonannde huunde, si Men faandike nde, Men wi'anay nde tun: "Laato", nde laatoo
16|41|Ɓen ferunooɓe fii Alla, ɓaawo ɓe tooñaama, ma Men hoɗnu ɓe ka aduna (e weerde) moƴƴere. Pellet, ko njoɓdi laakara ndin ɓuri mawnude, si tawno hiɓe anndi
16|42|Ɓen muññiiɓe, e tuugii e Joomi maɓɓe
16|43|Men Nulaali ado maaɗa si wanaa worɓe, Men wahayina e maɓɓe. Lanndee yimɓe defte ɓen si wonii on anndaa. @Corrected
16|44|(Men nulirii ɓe) ɓanngudi e defte. Men jippini e maaɗa janngeteende nden, fii yo a ɓannginan yimɓe ɓen kon ko jippinaa e maɓɓe, belajo'o kamɓe ɓe miijitoto
16|45|E hara ɓen fewjuɓe boneeji ɗin hooli wonnde Alla munnirtaa ɓe leydi ndin, maa lepte ɗen ardirana ɓe nokku mo ɓe so'aa-anndude
16|46|maa O nanngira ɓe yahdu maɓɓe, ɓe wonaali laawotooɓe
16|47|Maa O nanngira ɓe e hoore kulol. Anndu Joomi mon ko Yurmeteeɗo, Hinnotooɗo
16|48|E ɓee yi'aali ko Alla tagi kon e huunde nde ɗowɗe mun yiiltondirta ñaamo e nano, sujjangol Alla, hara ko ɗi yannkiniiɗi
16|49|Ko Alla woni ko sujjanta kala ko woni ka kammuuli e ka leydi, immorde e ruugayngel, e Malaa'ikaaɓe ɓen, kamɓe ɓe townitotaako. @Corrected
16|50|Hiɓe hulira Joomi maɓɓe, senngo dow maɓɓe, hiɓe waɗa ko ɓe yamiraa. @Corrected
16|51|Alla daali: "Wata on jogito reweteeɓe ɗiɗo. Anndee Kanko ko O reweteeɗo gooto. Ko Min woni ko huloton
16|52|Ko Kanko woodani kala ko woni ka kammuuli e ka leydi; ko Kanko ɗoftagol duumiingol tabitani. E ko ko woori Alla huloton
16|53|Kala ko heɓuɗon e neema ko immorde ka Alla. Refti si lorra memii on, ko Ka Makko wullitotoɗon
16|54|Refti si O huncanii on lorra kan, e jaka fedde goo e mo'on, ko sirkanooɓe Joomi mun
16|55|Fii yo ɓe yeddu ko Men okki ɓe kon. Awa dakmitee, arma anndon
16|56|Hiɓe waɗana huunde nde ɓe anndaa geɓal e kon ko Men arsiki ɓe. Wallaahi! On lannditete e kon ko fefindotonoɗon
16|57|Hiɓe waɗana Alla ɓiɗɓe rewɓe. Senayee woodanii Mo Hiɓe (waɗana) ko'e maɓɓe ko ɓe wooɗitii
16|58|Si gooto e maɓɓe wewliniraama ɓiɗɗo debbo, yeeso makko ngon waɗtina wayliingo ɓalewo e, hara ko o suuɗ-suno
16|59|Himo suuɗora yimɓe ɓen, sabu bone mo o wewliniraa on. E o jogitoray mo e hoore koyeera kaa o uway mo ka leydi? Annde bonii ko ɓe ñaawata
16|60|Hino woodani ɓen ɓe gomɗinaa laakara sifa bonɗo on. Ko Alla woodani sifa toowuɗo on. Ko Kanko kadi woni Fooluɗo, Ñeeñuɗo
16|61|Si tawno Alla nanngitirayno yimɓe ɓen sabu tooñe maɓɓe ɗen, O ccataano e dow mayri ruugayngel. Ko woni tun, Himo nennitana ɓe haa e lajal annda- ngal. Si lajal maɓɓe ngal arii, ɓe nennantaake yonta ɓe adintinantaake
16|62|Hiɓe waɗana Alla ko ɓe añanta [ko'e-maɓɓe]. Ɗemɗe maɓɓe no sifoo fenaande, wonnde no woodani ɓe moƴƴere. Sikke alaa wonnde no woodani ɓe Yiite, e wonnde ko ɓe ɗaliiɓe
16|63|Wallaahi! Gomɗii Men nulii e mofte adinooɓe ma, seytaane cuɗani ɓe golle maɓɓe ɗen. Ko kanko woni giɗo maɓɓe hannde, hino woodani ɓe lepte muusuɗe
16|64|Men jippiniraali Deftere nden e maaɗa si wanaa fii yo a ɓannginan ɓe kon ko ɓe luutondiri e mun, kadi ko nde peewal, e yurmeende wonannde yimɓe gomɗimɓe ɓen
16|65|Alla jippinirii ka kammu ndiyam, O wuurnitiri ɗam leydi ndin ɓaawo ndi yoorude. Wonii e ɗum, maande wonannde yimɓe nanooɓe
16|66|Hino woodani on e neemoraaɗi ɗin tasakuyee: Meɗen yarna on e ko woni e deedi majji, - hakkunde coowo e ƴiiƴam - ɓiraaɗam laaɓuɗam, welɗam fii yarooɓe
16|67|E dimɗe tamarooji e inabuuje, hiɗon jogitora ɗam siwran e arsike moƴƴo. Wonii e ɗum, maande wonannde yimɓe haqqilooɓe
16|68|Joomi maa wahayini e ñaakii ngii, wonnde : "Jaggu ka pelle cuuɗi, e leɗɗe ɗen, e kon ko ɓe saññata
16|69|Refti ñaamaa e kala dimɗe ɗen, naaton e ɗate Joomi mon newinaaɗe. Hino yalta e deedi majji [kannji ñaaki ɗin], njaram seruɗam nooneeji mun, no e majjam cellal wonannde yimɓe ɓen. Wonii e ɗum, maande wonannde yimɓe miijitotooɓe
16|70|Alla tagii on, refti O hunnay on. Hino e mooɗon on rutteteeɗo e jaasuɗum nguurndam, fii wata o anndu huunde ɓaawo ganndal [makko aranal]. Pellet, Alla ko Annduɗo, Hattanɗo
16|71|Alla ɓurnii yoga mon e dow yoga ka arsike. Ɓurnaaɓe ɓen wonaali ruttirooɓe arsike maɓɓe on e ɓen ɓe jeytiri ñaame maɓɓe ɗen haa ɓe fota e mayri. E ko neema Alla on ɓe yeddata
16|72|Alla waɗiranii on e wonkiiji mon ɗin resondirɓe, O waɗirani on e resondiraaɓe mon ɓen ɓiɗɓe e taaniraaɓe, O arsiki on immorde e laaɓuɗi. E ko meere nden ɓe gomɗinta? E ko neema Alla on kamɓe ɓe yeddata
16|73|Hiɓe rewa gaanin Makko, huunde nde waawanaa ɓe (addude) arsike ka kammuuli e ka leydi hay huunde, ɗi hattanaaka [ɗum]
16|74|Wata on waɗan Alla yerodniraaɗi. Pellet, Alla ko annduɗo, onon on anndaa
16|75|Alla piyii misal maccuɗo jeyaaɗo, mo waawaa hay huunde, e on mo Men arsiki immorde e Amen arsike moƴƴo, hara on wintoo e ɗum gunndoo e kene. Hara ɓen no fota? Yettooree woodanii Alla! Ko woni, ko ɓuri ɗuuɗude e maɓɓe anndaa
16|76|Alla piyi kadi misal worɓe ɗiɗo: goɗɗo e maɓɓe ko mbobo, o waawaa hay huunde, kanko ko o donngal e hoore jeyɗo mo on; nokku kala ka on fewtiniri mo, o addataa moƴƴere; hara on ɗon fotay e on yamiroowo nunɗal, hara himo e laawol focciingol
16|77|Ko Alla woodani wirniiɗi kammmuuli ɗin e leydi ndin. Fiyaaku Darngal ngal wonaali si wanaa yeru kinƴan yiitere maa hara ko kañun ɓuri ɓaɗtaade. Pellet, Alla ko hattanɗo kala huunde
16|78|Alla yaltinii on ka deedi neeniraaɓe mon, on anndaa huunde, O waɗani on nanɗe, e giiɗe e ɓerɗe, belajo'o, on yettay [Mo]
16|79|E ɓe yi'aali colli ɗin ko ɗi eltaaɗi ka weeyo kammu (wonnde) jogitaaki ɗi si wanaa Alla? Wonii e ɗum, maandeeji wonannde yimɓe gomɗinooɓe ɓen
16|80|Alla waɗanii on e cuuɗi mon ɗin hoɗo, O waɗani on e guri neemoraaɗi ɗin tillisaaji ɗi taggoton ñalnde eggoton e ñalnde hoɗtoton. No e leeɓi (baali) ɗin, e leeɓi (gelooɗi) ɗin e leeɓi (dammi) ɗin ndaɗɗudi [suudu] e dakmitorɗi haa e saanga
16|81|Alla waɗanii on e ko O tagi kon ɗowɗe. O waɗani on e pelle ɗen suuɗorɗe. O waɗani on conci daɗndayɗi on nguleendi, e conci daɗndayɗi on e hare mon. Ko wano nii O timminirta neemaaji Makko ɗin e dow mon, belajo'o on jebbiloto
16|82|Si ɓe huccitii, anndu ko fawi maa, ko yottingol ɓanngina
16|83|Hiɓe anndi neemaaji Alla ɗin; refti ɓe yedda ɗi. Ko ɓuri ɗuuɗude e maɓɓe ko heeferɓe
16|84|(Janto) kadi ñalnde Men immintinoyta e kala mofte seedeejo, refti ɓen yedduɓe sakkitoyantaake (ngantinagol), wanaa kamɓe woni ko ɗaɓɓiroytee ruttitagol [e yarluyee Joomi maɓɓe]
16|85|Si tooñuɓe ɓen yi'ii lepte ɗen, ɓe hoynantaake, lette wanaa ɓe nennitanteeɓe
16|86|Si sirkooɓe ɓen yi*i kafidaaɓe maɓɓe ɓen, ɓe wi'a: "Joomi amen, ko ɗii woni kafidaaɗi amen ɗi men rewaynoo gaanin Maa". [Kafidaaɗi maɓɓe] ɗin yilta e maɓɓe konngol ngol: "Onon ko on fenooɓe
16|87|Ɓe werloo e Alla nden ñalnde jebbilaare, kon ko fefindotonoo majjira ɓe
16|88|Ɓen yedduɓe ɓe faddii e laawol Alla ngol, Men ɓeydiranii ɓe lepte e hoore lepte, sabu ko ɓe bonniraynoo kon
16|89|(Janto kadi) ñalnde Men immintinoyta e kala mofte ko seeditoo e maɓɓe, jeyaaɗo e maɓɓe, Men adda maa [an Muhammadu] ko seeditoo e ɓee ɗoo. Men jippini e maaɗa Deftere nden, ko nde ɓannginoore kala huunde, e peewal, e yurmeende, e welo-welo wonannde juulɓe ɓen
16|90|Tabitii Alla yamirii nunɗal, e moƴƴingol, e moƴƴagol e joomiraaɓe ɓadondiral. Himo haɗa gaay e pan-kare, e ko añinii, e bewre. Himo waajoo on, belajo'o, on waajitoray
16|91|Hunnee ahadi Alla ndin si on ahodaama, wata on firtu goondooje ɗen ɓaawo ɗe tenntineede, gomɗii on waɗii Alla seedaniiɗo [on e hunnugol ngol]. Pellet, ko annduɗo ko golloton
16|92|Wata on wonu wa on (debbo) firtunooɗo mottawol mun ɓaawo doole firtude, hiɗon jogitora goondooje mon ɗen janfondiro hakkunde mon, nde mofte [mon ɗen] wonata ɓurde tonaade e dii mofte goo. Anndee Alla no jarribora on ɗum. Ma O ɓanngina- na on Ñalnde Darngal, kon ko luutondiraynoɗon e mun
16|93|Sinno Alla muuyuno, O waɗayno on mofte goote. Kono, Himo majjina on Mo O muuyi, O fewna on Mo O muuyi. Ma on lannditoye e kon ko gollaynoɗon
16|94|Wata on jogitor goondooje mon janfondiro hakkunde mon, sakko koyngal [mon] mortotoo (fergito) ɓaawo ngal tabitude, meeɗiron bone sabu ko sakkiɗon kon e laawol Alla ngol. Hino woodani on lepte mawɗe
16|95|Wata on waɗtitir ahadi Alla ndin coggu fanɗungu. Anndee ko ko woni ka Alla kon ɓuri moƴƴannde on, si tawno hiɗon anndi
16|96|Ko marɗon kon re'ay (lanna), ko woni ka Alla kon ko heddotooɗum. Ma Men warjor ɓen muññiiɓe njoɓdi maɓɓe ndin ko ɓuri moƴƴude e ko ɓe gollaynoo kon
16|97|Kala golluɗo moƴƴere, woni gorko maa debbo, hara ko o gomɗinɗo, Ma Men wuurnu mo nguur- ndam laaɓuɗam. Ma Men warjor ɓe njoɓdi maɓɓe ndin, ko ɓuri moƴƴude e ko ɓe gollaynoo kon
16|98|Si a janngay Alqur'aana, moolor Alla seytaane raɗaaɗo on
16|99|Kanko on, mbawdi(cemmbe) alanaa mo e ɓen gomɗimɓe, ɓe fawii e hoore Joomi maɓɓe
16|100|Anndee mbawdi makko ndin, ko hoore ɓen welduɓe e makko woni, e ɓen sirkirooɓe sabu makko
16|101|Si Men lontinii Aaya lonto Aaya goo - Ko Alla ɓuri anndude ko O jippinta - Ɓe wi'a: "An on ko a fefindiiɗo". Si ko woni, ko ɓuri ɗuuɗude e maɓɓe anndaa
16|102|Maaku: "Ko jippini ndee, ko [Jibriilu] Fittaanndu Laaɓundu ndun, immorde ka Joomi maa, fii yo o tabintin ɓen gomɗimɓe, e [fii yo nde wonu] peewal, e welo-welo wonannde juulɓe ɓen
16|103|Gomɗii Men Meɗen anndi wonnde hiɓe wi'a: "Ko neɗɗanke woni mo anndinnde (Alqur'aana)". Ɗemngal ngal ɓe ooñotoo e mun ngal ko ajami, ndee ɗoo non ka ɗemngal Aarabu ɓanngungal
16|104|Pellet, ɓen ɓe gomɗinaali Aayeeje Alla ɗen, Alla fewnataa ɓe. Hino woodani ɓe lepte muusuɗe
16|105|Anndee ko fefindotoo fenaande, ko ɓen ɓe gomɗi- aa Aayee Alla ɗen; ko kamɓe woni fenooɓe ɓen
16|106|Kala yedduɗo Alla ɓaawo gomɗinal makko ngal - si wanaa on waawnaaɗo hara ɓernde makko nden ko deeƴirnde gomɗinal , kono, ɓen yaññamɓe ɓerɗe mun keeferaaku, hino fawii ɓe tikkere immorde Alla, hino woodani ɓe kadi lepte mawɗe
16|107|Ngol [murtugol maɓɓe], ko tawde ɓe suɓike nguurndam aduna e dow laakara, e wonnde Alla kan, O fewnataa yimɓe yedduɓe ɓen
16|108|Ko ɓen woni ɓe Alla noti e ɓerɗe mun, e nanɗe mun e gite mun. Ko ɓen woni welsindiiɓe ɓen
16|109|Sikke alaaa wonnde ɓen ɗon ka laakara, ko kamɓe woni sooyuɓe ɓen
16|110|Refti pellet Joomi maa, wonannde ɓen ferunooɓe ɓaawo nde ɓe tampinaama, hooti ɓe tiiɗnii ɓe muññii, pellet Joomi maa, ɓaawo ɗum, Ko O Haforoowo, Hinnotooɗo
16|111|(Janto) tuma ñalnde kala wonkii arata, hara hiki wennja fii hoore-makki, wonkii kala yoɓee ko ki golli kon, kamɓe ɓe tooñetaake
16|112|Alla piyii misal hoɗo: hoɗo hoolinoongo, deeƴungo; arsike maggo no ardirana ngo nokku kala e yaaj- jeende. Ɓe yeddi neemaaji Alla ɗin, Alla meeɗiniri ɓe koltu heege e kulol, sabu ko ɓe huuwaynoo kon
16|113|Gomɗii arii e maɓɓe Nulaaɗo jeyaaɗo e maɓɓe, ɓe fenni mo. Lepte ɗen nanngi ɓe, tawi ko ɓe tooñuɓe
16|114|Ñaamee e kon ko Alla arsike on dagiiɗi laaɓuɗi, yetton neemaaji Alla ɗin, si wonii ko Kanko rewoton
16|115|Anndee ko O Harminani on, ko jiiba, e ƴiiƴam (rufaaɗam), e teewu kose, e [huunde hirsiraande] daginiraande ko woori Allah. Kala on duñaaɗo [e ñaamugol ɗum] hara wanaa ɓewɗo wanaa jaggi- tuɗo,Anndee pellet, Allah ko Ya'fotooɗo Hinnotooɗo
16|116|Wata on wi'u ko ɗemɗe mon sifotoo e penaale: "Ɗum ɗoo no dagii, ɗum ɗoo no harmi", fii no fefindoron e hoore Alla fenaande. Pellet, ɓen fefindotooɓe fenaande e hoore Alla, ɓe maletaake
16|117|Ko dakamme fanɗuɗo, hino woodani ɓe lepte muusuɗe
16|118|E hoore Alyahuudaaɓe ɓen (kan), Men harminno ko Men fillani maa kon ko adii. Men tooñaano ɓe; ko woni, ko ko'e-maɓɓe ɓe wonunoo e tooñude
16|119|Refti pellel, Joomi maa, wonannde ɓen huuwirɓe bone on majjere, refti ɓe tuubi ɓaawo ɗum ɓe moƴƴini, pellet Joomi maa, ɓaawo ɗum, ko Haforoowo, Hinnotooɗo
16|120|Pellet, Ibraahiima woniino ɗowro hoykinaniiɗo Alla, ooñiiɗo [e ɗiya diinaaji], o wonaali jeyaaɗo e sirkooɓe ɓen
16|121|Yettaynooɗo nemaaji Makko ɗin. [Alla] suɓike mo, O fewni mo e laawol focciingol
16|122|Men okki mo ka aduna moƴƴere. Kanko on ka laakara, ko o jeyaaɗo e moƴƴuɓe ɓen
16|123|Refi Men wahayini e maaɗa, wonnde: " Jokku diina Ibraahiima ka naayaaki e diinaaji mehre o jeyanooka e sirkooɓe ɓen
16|124|Anndee [mawningol fii] aseweere nden ko waɗanaa, ko ɓen luutondirɓe e mayre. Pellet, Joomi maa, ko ñaawoyoowo hakkunde maɓɓe Ñalnde Darngal, e kon ko ɓe luutondiraynoo fii mun
16|125|Noddir e diina Joomi maa kan ñeeñal e waaju moƴƴu. Wennjiraa ɓe e noone ɓurɗo moƴƴude. Pellet, Joomi maa, ko Kanko ɓuri anndude on majjuɗo e laawol Makko ngol, ko Kanko kadi ɓuri anndi feewuɓe ɓen
16|126|Si on yagginay, haray yagginiree yeru no waɗiranoɗon non. Ko si on muññike, pellet ko ɗum ɓuri moƴƴannde muññiiɓe ɓen
16|127|Muñño! Muñal maa ngal ko sabu Alla tan. Wata a suno fii maɓɓe. Wata wonu ɓittorɗo e kon ko ɓe fewjata
16|128|Pellet, Alla no wonndi e ɓen huluɓe [Mo] e ɓen moƴƴinooɓe
17|1|Senayee wondanii On Royruɗo Jeyaaɗo Makko on jemma, iwde ka juulirde hormante haa ka juulirde woɗɗitiinde, nden nde Men Barkini banŋe mun,fii yo Men Hollu mo immorde e Aayeeje Amen. Pellet, Ko Kanko woni Nanoowo, Yi’oowo. @Corrected
17|2|Men Jonniino Muusaa Deftere nden, Men Waɗi nde peewal, wonannde ɓiɗɓe Israa’iila ɓen, wonnde : "Wata on jogito gaanin Am hooloraaɗo
17|3|[Ko onon yo] ɓiɗɓe ɓen ɓe Men waɗɗinnoo wonndude e Nuuhu.Pellet, o laatino jeyaaɗo yettoowo
17|4|Men wahyiniino e ɓiɗɓe Israa’iila ɓen ka Deftere [wonnde] : "On bonnayay ka leydi laabi ɗiɗi, on townitoyto kadi townitaare mawnunde
17|5|Si fodoore gootel e ɗin ɗiɗi arii, Men wurtay e mon jeyaaɓe Amen, marɓe doole tiiɗuɗe, ɓe yiiloo hakkunde galleeji ɗin. Ɗum wonii fodoore huuwoyteende =golloteende
17|6|Refti Men ruttitanani on doole ɗen e hoore maɓɓe; Men Ɓeydi on jawle e ɓiɗɓe,Men Waɗa on gorol ɓurngol ɗuuɗude
17|7|Si on moƴƴinii, ko ko'e mon moƴƴinanɗon ; si on bonnii kadi, ko ko’e mon [bonnannɗon]. Si fodoore sakkitiinde nden arii, ko fii yo ɓe hoynu geece mon ɗen, e fii yo no ɓe naatiraa ka juulirde wano ɓe naatirnoo e mayre ka laawol aranol, e fii yo ɓe muncu yeru woo ko ɓe townani muncudee
17|8|Hino jortaa ka Joomi mon yurmee on.Si on fillitike (non),Men fillitoo. Men waɗanii yedduɓe ɓen Jahannama on tonngorde
17|9|Pellet, ndee Alqur’aanaare no fewnay e ko ɓuri e nunɗude,hinde wewlinira=weltanira gomɗimɓe,ɓen gollooɓe moƴƴuɗi ɗin, wonnde, no woodani ɓe njoɓdi mawndi
17|10|E wonnde pellet, ɓen ɓe gomɗinaa laakara on, Men maranii ɓe lepte muusuɗe
17|11|Neɗɗo no toroo bone, wano o tororta non moƴƴere,neɗɗanke on wonii ko heñiiɗo
17|12|Men waɗii jemma on e ñalorma on Aayeeje ɗiɗi, Men monti Aaya jemma on, Men waɗi Aaya ñalorma on hentiiɗo, fii yo on ɗaɓɓu ɓural immorde ka Joomi mon, e fii yo on anndu limoore duuɓi, e hasboore. Kala huunde, Men fensitirii nde fensitudee
17|13|Kala neɗɗanke, Men waɗɗinii mo talkuru makko ndun ka daande makko. Men yaltinanoyay mo Ñalnde Darngal, deftere, o hawra e mayre ko nde fontaande
17|14|Janngu deftere maa nden, hoore-maa yonante hannde hasboowo
17|15|Mo feewii, haray pellet, ko hoore-makko o feewani ; mo majii kadi, haray pellet, ko o majji kon yantay e hoore-makko. Wonkii ronndotaako bone wokki goo. Men wonaali leptooɓe, haa Men immina Nulaaɗo
17|16|Si Men faandike halkude saare, Men yamiray neeminaaɓe mayre ɓen, ɓe faasinqinoo e mayre, konngol (lepte) ngol jojja e mayre, Men munca nde muncudee
17|17|Heewii gire ɗe Men halki ɓaawo Nuuhu! Joomi maa Yonii Humpitiiɗo, Yi’oowo junuubi=bakkatuuji jeyaaɓe Makko ɓen
17|18|On tawɗo no faandii yaccinaneede=yaawnaneede, Men yaccinanay mo ton huunde ko Men muuyi, wonannde on mo Men yiɗi, refti Men waɗana mo Jahannama, o naatoya nge ko o ŋiñaaɗo, pottinaaɗo [yurmeende]
17|19|On faalaaɗo laakara, o gollani ngal golle maggal, hara kanko ko o gomɗinɗo ;ɓen ɗon, golle maɓɓe ɗen wonii jaarnaaɗe
17|20|Kala (maɓɓe),Meɗen ɓeydana ; ɓee ɗoo e ɓee ɗoo, immorde e dokkal Joomi maa. Dokkal Joomi maa ngal wonaali haɗaa ngal
17|21|Ndaarii no Men ɓurniri yoga maɓɓe e dow yoga, ko laakara on ɓuri mawnude darjaaji,ɓuri mawnude kadi ɓural
17|22|Wata a waɗidan Alla reweteeɗo goo ; jooɗoyoɗaa ko a ŋiñaaɗo woppaaɗo
17|23|Joomi maa yamirii :"Wata on rewu ko wanaa Kanko, jibimɓe ɓen,moƴƴagol [e maɓɓe]:si nayewu goɗɗo e maɓɓe yottike ma,maa ɗum ɓe ɗiɗo non;wata a wi’an ɓe "bis=uf!" wata a wikko ɓe =wota a furo,wowlan ɓe konngol teddungol
17|24|Yankinanoɗaa ɓe yurmeɗaa ɓe, wi’aa: « Joomi an, yurme ɓe’e, wano ɓe ne’irnoo lan non hari ko mi tosokun »
17|25|Joomi mo'on no Anndi ko woni ka nder wonkiiji mon, si tawii on wonuno moƴƴuɓe ; pellet Kanko O wonanii ruttotooɓe ɓen Surroowo
17|26|Jonnu jom ɓadondiral haqqee makko on, e ɓilliiɗo, e seteejo haqqee makko on ; wata a funsu funsudee
17|27|Pellet funsooɓe ɓen, ko siɗɓe seytanuuji ɗin ; seytaane non wonii yedduɗo Joomi mun
17|28|Si a ɗurnike ɓe fii ɗaɓɓugol yurmeende immorde ka Joomi maa, nde jortiɗaa ɗum, wi'an ɓe konngol newiingol
17|29|Wata a waɗu junngo maa ngon ko lmbaango, ka daande maa ; wata a fontu ngo kadi kala fontugol, haa jooɗoɗaa ko a felniiɗo, ninsuɗo
17|30|Pellet Joomi maa, no yanñana arsike, on Mo O muuyi. O ɓittina. Pellet Kanko O wonii Humpitiiɗo, Yi’oowo jeyaaɓe Makko
17|31|Wota on warir ɓiɓɓe mon ɓen kulol ɓilla=baasal, ko Menen arsikata ɓe, wonndude e mon ; pellet warugol ɓe ngol, wonii goopol manngol
17|32|Wota on ɓatto jeeno ngon=fijrde nde, pellet ɗun wonii pankare e laawol bonungol
17|33|Wata on waru wonkii, ki Allah harmini kin [warugol], si wonaa sabu hakkee. Mo tooñaama waraama, Men waɗanii heftuɓe e makko ɓen doole wota non o fantin ka warugol. Pellet Kanko o wonii wallaaɗo
17|34|Wata on ɓatto jawle Alyatiim, si wonaa ɓattagol ɓurngol moƴƴude, haa sagatalaaku makko timma ; humnee aadi ndin; pellet, aadi ndin wonii lannditoytee ndi
17|35|Hunnee ɓetu ngun si on etay, manndikiron manndakke=peeson peese feewuɗe, ko ɗun moƴƴi, ko kañun ɓuri moƴƴude battane
17|36|Wata a naatu e ko a anndaa fii mun. Pellet nanɗe ɗen, e giiɗe ɗen e ɓernde nden, ɗiiɗoo fow wonii lannditoyteeɗi ka Makko
17|37|Wata a yaaru ka leydi ñaaƴa bunnga, ko fii pellet an a yulataa leydi ndin, a yottotaako pelle ɗen junndi=njuuteendi
17|38|ɗin fow, bone majji on wonii añaaɗun ka Joomi maa
17|39|Ɗun, ko goɗɗun e ko Joomi maaɗa wahayini faade e maa, immorde e Ñeeñal wata a waɗu reweteeɗo goo wonndude e Alla, sakko werleɗaa ka nder jahannama ko a felaaɗo raɗaaɗo
17|40|E hara Joomi mon suɓani on ɓiɓɓe worɓe, O jogitoo immorde e malaa'ikaɓe ɓen rewɓe? Pellet, onon hiɗin wowlude konngol mawnungol
17|41|Gomɗii Men fensitii e nder ndee Alqur'aanaare fii yo ɓe waajitor, ɗum ɓeydaali ɓe si wonaa woɗɗitagol
17|42|Maaku : « Si tawno no wonndi e makko, reweteeɗi wano ɓe wi’iri non awa ɗi ɗaɓɓayno laawol ummaade Jom Arsi o." @Corrected
17|43|Senayee wonanii Mo, O Toowii gaayi e ko ɓe wi'ata Toowal Mawnungal
17|44|No subunhinannde Mo kammuuli ɗin jeeɗiɗi e leydi ndin e ɓen wonuɓe e majji, alaa e hay e huunde si wanaa hinde Subunhinaade sabu Yettugol Mo, kono on faamataa subunhinaali maɓɓe ɗin, pellet, Kanko O wonii Munñiiɗo Surroowo
17|45|Si a janngii Alqur'aanaare nden Men waɗay hakkonde maa e ɓen ɓe gomɗinaa laahara on heedo suuɗiingo
17|46|Men waɗi e dow ɓerɗe maɓɓe ɗen cokooɗe fii wata ɓe faamu nde [Alqur'aanaare nden] e ka noppi maɓɓe kadi teddeele, si a jantike Joomi maaɗa ka nder Alqur'aanaare Kanko Tun ɓe huccinay ɓabbe maɓɓe ɗen ko ɓe dogooɓe
17|47|Ko Menen Anndi ko ɓe heɗotoo kon, tuma ɓe heɗotoo faade e maaɗa [yo Nulaaɗo], e tuma ɓe sowndondirta=ndeeydata, tuma nde tooñooɓe ɓen wi'ata: «On jokkaali si wanaa gorko mbilɗaaɗo=bilaado»
17|48|Ndaarii [yo Nulaaɗo] ko honno ɓe piyiranay maa mise=yeruuji, ɓe majjii ɓe hattantaake [heɓude] laawol
17|49|Ɓe wi'i: «E hara si men wonii ƴi'e e mbuɗu, haray ko men immintinoyteeɓe tagu hesu?»
17|50|Maaku: [yo Nulaaɗo] «Wonee kaaƴe maa jamɗe»
17|51|Maaɗun tagu tawayngu no mawni ka ɓerɗe mon, aray ɓe wi'a: 'Ko hommbo ruttata men?" Maaku: "Ko On Taguɗo on ka laawol aranol". Aray ɓe dimmba ko'e maɓɓe ɗen faande e maa, ɓe wi'a: "Ɗun ko honnde tuma", Maaku: 'No tijjaa nde tawata ɓadike
17|52|Ñannde O noddata on nootoɗon yetton Mo sikkon on ñiiɓaano [ka leydi] si wanaa seeɗa
17|53|Maakan jeyaaɓe an ɓen: "Yo ɓe wowlu nden huunde ɓurnde moƴƴude, pellet, Seytaane o bonnay hakkunde maɓɓe, pellet, Seytaane wonanii neɗɗanke gaño ɓannguɗo
17|54|Joomi mon ko O Annduɗo fii mon, si O yiɗii O hinnoo on, maaɗun si O yiɗii O lepta on. Men nulaali ma e dow maɓɓe fawtiiɗo
17|55|Ko Joomi maa Annde fii ɓen womɓe ka kammuuli e ka leydi, pellet, Men ɓurnii woɓɓe e Annabaaɓe ɓen e dow woɓɓe, Men Jonni Daawuuda Jabuura
17|56|Maaku: "Noddee ɓen ɓe aaƴiɗon [ko reweteeɓe] gaanin Makko, ɓe maraa huncugol lorra kan gaayi mo'on wonaa waylugol kadi
17|57|Ɓen, ɓe ɓe woni noddude, hiɓe ɗaɓɓude ɗoworgal faade e Joomi maɓɓe, ko hommbo e maɓɓe ɓuri ɓadaade, hiɓe jortii Hinnayee Makko on hiɓe huli lepte Makko ɗen, pellet, lepte Joomi maa ɗen ɗe laatike ko rentaaɗe
17|58|Alaa e saare si wanaa Menen ko Men halkayɓe nde ko adii ñalde darngal, maa ko Men leptayɓe nde lepte sattuɗe, ɗun ɗon wonii ko winndaa ɗun ka Deftere
17|59|Haɗaali Men nde Men nula Aayeeje ɗen, si wanaa sabu fenniino ɗe adiiɓe ɓen, Men okki Samuuda Naaqaawa mban yi'teemba ɓe tooñi mba, Men nuliraali Aayeeje ɗen si wonaa hulɓinirɗe
17|60|[Janto] Tuma nde Men wi'anno maa: "Pellet, Joomi maa O huɓindike yimɓe ɓen, Men waɗiraali nden yi'annde nde Men hollumaa si wanaa fitina wonannde yimɓe ɓen e lekki huɗaaki ki ka Alqur'aana, Meɗen hulɓina ɓe kono ɓeydataa ɓe si wanaa bewre mawnde
17|61|Nde Men Daalannoo Malaa'ikaaɓe ɓen sujjanee Aadama, ɓe sujji si wanaa Ibliisa o wi'i: "Hara mi sujjanay on mo taguƊaa e loopal
17|62|O wi'i: "A yi'ii oo mo teddinƊaa e dow an, pellet, si A nennanii lan haa ñalde darngal mi bonnay ɓiɓɓe makko ɓen si wanaa seeɗaaɓe
17|63|[Alla] Daali: "Yahu, kala jokkuɗo ma e maɓɓe pellet, ko jahannama woni njoddi mon, njoddi yonoori
17|64|Dillinir on mo hattanaɗaa e maɓɓe hito maa ngon, pooɗu e dow maɓɓe pucci maa e seppooɓe maa, ka fidu e maɓɓe ka jawle e ka ɓiɓɓe foduɓe, [kono] Seytaane fodaali ɓe si wanaa hodo
17|65|Pellet, Jeyaaɓe An ɓen a maraa doole e hoore maɓɓe, Joomi maa yonii Hooloraaɗo
17|66|Ko Joomi mon woni sogganayɗo on laaɗe ɗen ka maayo, fii yo on ɗaɓɓu immorde e ɓural Makko ngal, pellet, Kanko ko O Yurmeteeɗo on
17|67|Si lorra kan heɓii on ka maayo, majjay ɓen ɓe noddayno ɗon, si wonaa Kanko [Alla] nde O danndi on ka njorndi ɗurnoɗon, neɗɗanke on wonii te o seeraani wonde heewuɗo yeddugol
17|68|Enee, on hooli O mutintaa on ka banŋe njorndi maaɗun O nula e mon damagariire [toɓo koccu], refti hara heɓantaake on fawtiiɗo
17|69|Kaa on hooli O ruttaraa on e maggo laawol goo O accita e dow mon bippooru immorde e keneeli O yoolira on sabu ko yeddunoɗon kon, refti on heɓantaake jokkitirayɗo e dow amen cukkoowo
17|70|Gomɗii, Men teddinii ɓiɗɓe Aadama ɓen, Men ronndike ɓe ka njorndi e ka maayo Men arsiki ɓe immorde e laaɓuɗi Men ɓurni ɓe e dow ko heewi e ɓen ɓe Men tagi ɓurnudee
17|71|Ñannde Men noddiroyta kala yimɓe yeesoojo maɓɓe on,kala on jonnitiroyaaɗo deftere makko nden ka ñaamo makko ɓen ɗon ɓe janngay deftere maɓɓe nden ɓe tooñirtaake hay yeru gaarayol hun tamaro
17|72|Kala on wonuɗo e [ngurndan aduna] ko o bunɗo, haray kanko, ko ka laahara o ɓurata wumude e majjude laawol
17|73|Fii kala ɓe eɓɓii nde ɓe fitinaymaa gaayi nden huunde nde Men wahayini e maaɗa fii yo a fefindo e Amen ko wonaa ɗun [ko Men tellini e maa] ontuma ɓe jogitoto ma sehlaajo
17|74|Si tawiino Men tabintinaanoma, gomɗii hari a do'ii ooñaade e maɓɓe huunde seeɗaare
17|75|Ontuma Men meeɗinteno cowale [lepte] ka ngurndan e cowale [lepte] ka mayde refti heɓantaake ma ballo e hoore Amen
17|76|Fii kala ɓe eɓɓiino dillinngol ma ka leydi fii yo ɓe yaltine e mayri, ontuma ɓe ñiiɓataano ɓatte maa si wanaa seeɗa
17|77|Ɗun ko Sunna ɓen ɓe Men nuli ko adimaa immorde e Nulaaɓe Amen, a heɓantaa Sunna Amen on mbattiigu
17|78|Ñinnu julde nden ka mortagol naange ngen haa ka niwre jemma, Julde subaha nden, pellet, Julde subaha nden wonii seedeteende
17|79|Ka jemma tinno e makko ko ɓeydaari maaɗa, no jortaa nde Joomi maaɗa immintinay maa e darorde yettiniinde
17|80|Maaku: "Jooma, naadiran naatirgal goonga yaltiniraa mi yaltirgal goonga, waɗanaa mi immorde ka Maaɗa doole ballal
17|81|Maaku: "goonga kan arii meere nden fuuyii, pellet, meere nden wonii fuuyoore
17|82|Meɗen tellina ka Alqur'aana huunde nde konde cellal e yurmeende wonnande gomɗinɓe ɓen, ɓeydataa tooñooɓe ɓen si wanaa hayrere
17|83|Si Men neeminii e neɗɗanke on o ɗuurnoo o townaa balaaje makko, si bone heɓii mo o wona hattuɗo e taƴiiɗo
17|84|Maaku: "Mo kala yo gollu e laawol mun, ko Joomi mon woni Annduɗo on ɓurɗo feewude laawol
17|85|Hiɓe lanndo maa fii fittaandu, maaku: "Fittaandu ndun ko e fiyaake Joomi an, on okkaaka e ganndal si wanaa seeɗaé
17|86|Mi woondii, si Meɗen yiɗunoo Men naɓayno nden huunde nde Men wahyini faade e Maaɗa, refti heɓantaake ma fawtiiɗo ɗun e hoore Amen
17|87|Ko woni tun, ko Hinnayee immorde ka Joomi maa, pellet, ɓural Makko ngal e dow maa wonii mawnungal
17|88|Maaku: "Mi woondii, si yimɓe ɓen e jinnaaji ɗin hawtitii fii yo ɓe addu yeru ndee Alqur'aanaare, ɓe addataa yeru mayre, hay si wonii woɓɓe maɓɓe ko wallindrayɓe e woɓɓe
17|89|Gomɗii Men ɓannginanii yimɓe ɓen e ndee Alqur'aanaare immorde e kala misal, ɓurɓe ɗuuɗude e yimɓe ɓen salii, si wanaa yeddugol
17|90|Ɓe wi'i: "Men gomɗintaa ma, haa ɓullitanaa men ka leydi ɓunndu
17|91|Maaɗun laatano maa ngesa immorde e tamorooje e inabuuje ɓullitaa canɗi ɗin hakkunde majje ɓullitugol
17|92|Maaɗun liɓaa kammu ngun e hoore amen wano aaƴorɗaa non kunte, maaɗun addaa Alla e Maalaa'ikaaɓe ɓen [men] tiindondira
