17|93|Maaɗun laatano maa suudu immorde e cuɗaaje [kanŋe], maaɗun ƴawaa ka kammu, men gomɗintaa ƴawugol maaɗa ngol haa jippinaa e amen deftere men jannga nde. Maaku: "Senaade Jom an, hara mi wonu, ko wonaa ɓanndinke Nulaaɗo
17|94|Haɗaali yimɓe ɓen nde ɓe gomɗinta tuma nde peewalngal arunoo ɓe, si wanaa fii ɓe wi'ii: "E hara Alla nulay ɓanndinke Nulaaɗo
17|95|Maaku: "Si tawiino laatinoke ka leydi Malaa'ikaaɓe hiɓe yaha ko ɓe deewuɓe, Men jippinayno e maɓɓe immorde ka kammu Malaa'ikaajo Nulaaɗo
17|96|Maaku: "Alla yonii Seediiɗo hakkunde an e mon, pellet Kanko O wonii Humpitiiɗo Reenuɗo jeyaaɓe Makko ɓen
17|97|On mo Alla fewni ko on woni feewuɗo, ɓe O majjini ɓen a heɓantaaɓe wallooɓe ko woori Mo. Men mooɓay ɓe ñalde darngal e dow geece maɓɓe ɗen ko ɓe wumuɓe e mbobiɗu= fahdube ɓe e faaɗuɓe, werde maɓɓe nden ko jahannama tuma kala nge rocci Men ɓeydana ɓe huɓɓunge
17|98|Ɗun ko njoddi maɓɓe, sabu kamɓe ɓe yeddii Aayeeje Amen ɗen, ɓe wi'i: "E hay si men wonii ƴi'e e mbuɗu e hara menen ko men immintinteeɓe tagu hesu
17|99|Enee, ɓee yi'aali, wonnde Alla On Taguɗo kammuuli ɗin e leydi ndin ko O Hattanɗo nde O tagata yeru maɓɓe, O waɗani ɓe lajal [caate] sikke alaa e maggal. Tooñooɓe ɓen salii si wanaa yeddugol
17|100|Maaku: "Sinndo onon hiɗon marunoo ngaluuji Hinnayee Joomi an on, ontuma, on jogitotono kulol nafkugol, neɗɗanke on wonii nguddo
17|101|Gomɗii Men okkiino Muusaa Aayeeje jeenay ɓannguɗe, lanndii ɓiɓɓe Israa'iila ɓen tuma nde o arunoo ɓe Fir'awna wi'ani mo: "Min dey miɗo sikkumaa ko an yo Muusaa ko a mbilɗaaɗo
17|102|Maaku: "Goɗii hiɗa anndi jippinaali ɗee si wanaa Jeyɗo kammuuli ɗin e leydi ndin Aayeeje [yi'eteeɗi]. Min dey miɗo sikkumaa ko an yo Fir'awna ko a halkiiɗo
17|103|O faalaa nde o dillinta ɓe ka leydi Men yooli mo e ɓen wonnduɓe e makko ɓe denndaangal
17|104|Men Daalani ɓaawo makko ɓiɓɓe Israa'iila ɓen: "Hoɗee ka leydi, si fodoore sakkitiinde nden arii, Men adday on ko on muuɓiiɓe=fiiliibe
17|105|Ko sabu Goonga Men telliniri nde, ko sabu Goonga nde tellii, Men nuliraali ma si wanaa [ko a] wewlinoowo=beltinoowo e jertinoowo
17|106|E Qur'aanaare Men ɓanngini nde fii yo a janngannde yimɓe ɓen e dow deeƴere, Men jippini nde jipinnde
17|107|Maaku: "Gomɗinee nde, maaɗun wata on gomɗin, pellet, ɓen okkaaɓe ganndal ko adii nde si [nde] janngaama e taweende maɓɓe ɓe suuyiray wokkuɗe ko ɓe sujjooɓe
17|108|Ɓe wi'a:Senaade woodanii Joomi amen,nde wonnoo Fodoore Joomi amen nden ko waɗoore
17|109|Hiɓe suuyira wokkuɗe ɓe wulla [Alqur'aana on] ɓayda ɓe yankinaare
17|110|Maaku: "Noddiree Mo Alla maa noddiro Mo Hinnorante, kala no noddirɗon Mo, ko Kanko Inɗe Moƴƴe ɗen heeranii, wata a fenñin julde maaɗa nden wata a suudu nde ɗaɓɓu hakkunde ɗun laawol
17|111|Maaku: Yettoore nden woodanii Alla On Mo jogitaaki ɓiɗɗo laatanaaki Mo kafidaaɗo e Laamu laatanaaki Mo tedduɗo mo O huykinantoo, Mawnin Mo Mawninndee
18|1|Yettoore woodanii Alla, On Tippinɗo e dow Jeyaaɗo Makko on Deftere nden O waɗanaali nde ooñaare
18|2|Feewunde fii yo o [Nulaaɗo on] hulɓinir lepte sattuɗe immorde ka Makko o weltinira gomɗinɓe ɓen, ɓen ɓe no golla Moƴƴuɗi ɗin wonnde no woodani ɓe Njoddi Moƴƴiri
18|3|Ko ɓe ñiiɓooɓe e nder makko [Neema on] poomaa
18|4|O rentina ɓen wi"uɓe: "Alla jogitike ɓiɗɗo
18|5|Ganndal alanaaɓe e mun, wanaa baabiraaɓe maɓɓe woodani, mawnii konngol wonungol e yaltude e kunnduɗe maɓɓe, ɓe wowlaali si wanaa fenaande
18|6|Bala jo'o an a tanpinay hoore-maa e dow batteeji maɓɓe, si gomɗinaali ndee Yewtere ka suno
18|7|Menen Men waɗii ko woni kon ka hoore leydi cuɗaari mayri, fii yo Men jarribo ɓe ko hommbo e maɓɓe ɓurata moƴƴinnde golle
18|8|Menen ko Men waɗooɓe ko woni kon e hoore mayri boowol yoorungal
18|9|Kaa a sikku no yimɓe fammeere=wimmba nden e binndi ɗin, ɗun wonu immorde e Aayeeje Amen hawniiɗe
18|10|Tuma nde sukaaɓe ɓen sorunoo ka fammeere, ɓe wi'i: "Joomi amen okku men immorde ka Maaɗa Hinnayee=yurmeende newinaNaa men kadi e fiyaake amen peewal
18|11|Men piyi e dow noppi maɓɓe ɗin ka nder fammeere limoore duuɓi
18|12|Refti Men immintini ɓe fii yo Men fenñinir gonndal ko honnde e mojobe=pelle ɗen ɗiɗi ɓuri moftude [limoore] ko ɓe ñiiɓi kon dummunne
18|13|Menen Meɗen fillanaade ma kumpital fii maɓɓe e Goonga, ɓen ɗon, ko sukaaɓe gomɗinɓe Joomi maɓɓe Men ɓeydani ɓe Peewal
18|14|Men haɓɓi e dow ɓerɗe maɓɓe tuma nde ɓe darinoo, ɓe wi'i: "Joomi amen ko Jeyɗo On kammuuli ɗin e leydi ndin, men noddataa ko woori Mo reweteeɗo, gomɗii haray men wi'ii ontuma [konngol] fantungol
18|15|Ɓee yimɓe amen, ɓe jogitike ko woori Mo reweteeɗi, ko haaanunoo ko yo ɓe addu e dow maɓɓe dalil ɓannguɗo. Ko hommbo ɓuri tooñude ko foti e on fefindiiɗo fenaande o fawi e Alla
18|16|Tuma nde woɗɗitinoɗon ɓe e ko ɓe rewata kon ko woori Alla, ɓe soroyi ka fammeere Joomi mon fontani on e Yurmeende Makko nden O newinani on e fiyaake mon neweende
18|17|Hiɗa yi'a naangi ngen si nge ƴellitike hinge naayora ka fammeere maɓɓe senngo ñaamo, si hinge mutude nge mutiranay ɓe ka senngo nano, kamɓe hiɓe e yaajeende e ɗun, ɗun ko jeyaaɗun e Aayeeje Alla, on mo Alla fewni ko on woni feewuɗo, kala moO majjini a heɓantaa mo hettuɗo fewnoowo. @Corrected
18|18|Hiɗa sikka ɓe ko ɓe finuɓe, hara kamɓe ko ɓe ɗaaniiɓe, Meɗen waylitira ɓe senngo ñaamo e senngo nano, rawaandu maɓɓe ndun no fonti kayɗe mun ɗen ka dammbugal, si a ƴellitike e maɓɓe a huccitayno e maɓɓe dogaa a heewayno kulol immorde e maɓɓe
18|19|Ko nii Men immintiniri ɓe fii yo ɓe lanndondir hakkunde maɓɓe, wi'oowo wi'i immorde e maɓɓe: "No foti hewde ko ñiiɓuɗon?" Ɓe wi'i: "Men ñiiɓii ñallal maa goɗɗun e ñallal." Ɓe wi'i: "Ko Joomi mon woni Annduɗo emmbere ko ñiiɓuɗon, nulee goɗɗo e mon wonndude e ɗii kaaki=ceede mon ɗoo ka saare, yo o ndaaru ko hommbo e maɓɓe ɓuri laaɓude ñaamitee, yo o addan on ñaametee immorde e on ɗon, yo o molto wata gooto so'u fii mon
18|20|Pellet, kamɓe si ɓe ƴellitike e mon ɓe rajmay on, maaɗun ɓe rutta on e laawol maɓɓe ngol, ontuma hara on maletaake poomaa
18|21|Ko nii Men yaltiniri fii maɓɓe, fii yo ɓe anndu pellet, Fodoore Alla nden ko nde Goonga, Pellet, Darngal ngal sikke alaa e maggal. Tuma nde ɓe pooɗondiraynoo hakkunde maɓɓe fiyaake maɓɓe ɗen, ɓe wi'i: "Mahee e hoore maɓɓe maadi, ko Joomi maɓɓe woni Annduɗo fii Maɓɓe." Ɓen fooluɓe e fiyaake mu'un wi'i: "Men jogitoto e dow maɓɓe Juulirde
18|22|Aray ɓe wi'a: "Ko ɓe tato nayaɓo maɓɓe ko rawaandu maɓɓe ndun." Ɓe wi'a kadi: "Ko ɓe njowo njeegaɓo maɓɓe ko rawaandu maɓɓe ndun ko fampaangol ka niɓe." Ɓe wi'a kadi: "Ko ɓe njeeɗiɗo njeetataɓo maɓɓe ko rawaandu maɓɓe ndun." Maaku: "Ko Joomi an woni Annduɗo limoore maɓɓe, anndaa ɓe si wanaa seeɗaaɓe." Wata a wennju fii maɓɓe si wanaa yewtere feeñunde, wata a lanndo fii maɓɓe hay e gooto e maɓɓe
18|23|Wata a wi'an huunde: "Min mi waɗay ɗun janngo
18|24|Si wanaa si Alla Muuyii, janto Joomi maaɗa si a yejjitii, maaku: "No tijjaa nde Joomi an Fewnan mi ko ɓuri ɓadaade immorde e ɗun Peewal
18|25|Ɓe ñiiɓi ka fammeere maɓɓe duuɓi teemeɗɗe tati, ɓe ɓeydi jeenay
18|26|Maaku: "Ko Alla woni Annduɗo emmbere ko ɓe ñiiɓi, ko Kanko heeranii ko wirnii kon ka kammuuli e ka leydi kaawes ko yi'iri wa Makko e ko naniri, alanaa ɓe gaanin Makko giɗo, O kafidaa ka Ñaawoore Makko hay e gooto
18|27|Janngu ko wahayinaa e maaɗa kon immorde e Deftere Joomi maa nden, alaa wattitoowo Daaluyeeji=konngudi Makko ɗin, a heɓataa gaanin Makko fattorde
18|28|Tabintin wonkii maaɗa kin wonndude e ɓen noddooɓe Joomi maɓɓe ka bimmbi e ka kiikiiɗe hiɓe faandii Jaati Makko Kin, wata gite maa ɗe yawtu gaayi maɓɓe hara hiɗa faandii cuɗaari ngurdan aduna, wota a ɗofto on mo Men welsindini ɓernde mun gaayi jantagol Men o jokki beleeɗe makko fiyaake makko on woni halkaare
18|29|Maaku Goonga kan immorde ka Joomi mon, mono faalaa yo o gomɗin mono faalaa yo o yeddu, Menen Men heblanii tooñooɓe ɓen Yiite no hunnditi ɓe ɗenɗe magge ɗen si ɓe ɗaɓɓii faabo, ɓe faaboree ndiyan wa'uɗan wa sila taynaaɗo ɗan juɗa geece ɗen, bonii njaram bonii werde
18|30|Pellet, ɓen gomɗinɓe ɓe golli moƴƴi ɗin, Menen Men yeebataa njoddi kala moƴƴinɗo golle
18|31|Ɓen ɗon no woodani ɓe Aljannaaji ñiiɓal canɗi no ila ley maɓɓe, hiɓe cuɗiree ton immorde e jawe kanŋe ɓe ɓornoo conci haakiɗuɗi ɗewluɗi e jalbuɗi ko ɓe soɓɓindiiɓe=tuugiibe ton e hoore julle, moƴƴii mbarjaari moƴƴii kadi fowtorde
18|32|fiyan ɓe misal,worɓe ɗiɗo Men waɗani goɗɗo e maɓɓe gese ɗiɗi inab Menhunndintini =hurliride ɗe tamarooje Men waɗi hakkunde majje remuru
18|33|Ɗen gese ɗiɗi kala addi ñaametee majje, ɗe tooñaali hay e huunde e ɗun, Men seeki hakkunde majje [gese ɗen ɗiɗi] caangol

18|56|Men Nuliraali Nulaaɓe ɓen si wanaa ko weltinooɓe e jertinooɓe, ɓen heeferɓe hiɓe wennjana meere nden fii yo ɓe fuynir nde Goonga kan, ɓe jogitii Aayeeje An ɗen e ko ɓe jertiniraa kon jalnori
18|57|Alaa fotayɗo tooñude on waajuraaɗo Aayeeje Joomi makko o ɗuurii=fali e gaayi majje o yejjiti ko juuɗe makko ɗen ardini kon. Menen Men waɗii e ɓerɗe maɓɓe ɗen cokooɗe fii wota ɓe faamu nde, ka noppi maɓɓe kadi pahu, hay si a noddii ɓe faade e Peewal ɓe feewataa ontuma haapoomaa

21|97|Fodoore Goongaare nden ɓadike, tawi kayre puttini giiɗe ɓen yedduɓe, [ɓe wi'a:] "Eeyoo bone amen, gomɗii men laatinoke e nder welsindaare immorde e ɗu'um, ko woni, men laatike tooñuɓe

21|102|Ɓe nanoytaa wuuɗaango magge kamɓe hiɓe e nder ko wonkiiji maɓɓe ɗin lokaa(wooɗa) kon, ko ɓe duumotooɓe
21|103|Suninoytaaɓe ɗenƴere mawnde nden, Malaa'ikaaɓe ɓen no jaɓɓooɓe [ɓe wi'a:] "Ko ndee woni Ñalaande mo'on, nden nde laatinoɗon hiɗon fodee
21|104|Ñalnde Men taggoyta kammu ngun wano taggugol ɗerol defte. Ko wano Men fuɗɗori non ka arannde tagu Men ruttirta ngu, [ɗum] ko Fodoore e dow Amen, pellet, Menen Men laatike gollooɓe

21|109|Si tawii ɓe ɗurnike, maaku: "Mi anndinii on e dow fotondiral, pellet, mi anndaa si no ɓadii maaɗum si no woɗɗi kon ko fodaɗon
21|110|Pellet, Kanko hiMo Anndi ko feeñi kon e konngol ngol, hiMo Anndi kadi ko suuɗoton
21|111|Mi anndaa non, belejo'o ɗum ko jarrabuyee mo'on, e dakamme haa e dummunne
21|112|Maaku: "Jooma, Ñaawir Goonga kan ko Joomi amen Hinnorante On woni Wallitorteeɗo On e dow kon ko sifotoɗon
22|1|Ko onon yo yimɓe, hulee Joomi mo'on, pellet, dillannde Darngal ngal ko huunde mawnde
22|2|Ñalnde yi'oton ngal, yejjitoyay kala muyninoowo ko o muyninaynoo kon, fukka kala sowiiɗo ko o sowiinoo kon, a yi'ay yimɓe ɓen no siwri, hara kamɓe ɓe siwraa, kono Lepte Alla ɗen ko saɗtuɗe
22|3|No e yimɓe ɓen on mo no wennja e fii Alla ko aldaa e ganndal, o jakka kala Seytaane canndallo
22|4|Winndaama e hoore-makko wonnde pellet, kala welduɗo e makko pellet, o majjinay mo, o ɗowa mo haa ka Lepte Sa'iiri
22|5|Ko onon yo yimɓe, si tawii on laatike e sikke immorde e immital ngal, pellet, Menen Men Tagii on immorde e mbullaari refti e toɓɓere maniiyu, refti e heɗɗere refti e huyre timmunde tagu e nde wonaa timmunde tagu fii yo Men ɓannginan on, Meɗen Ñiiɓina ka renngaaji ko Men Muuyi kon haa e happu innaaɗo, refti Men yaltini on ko on boobooɓe, refti fii yo on yotto sagatalaaku mo'on no e mo'on ɓen ɓe no maaya no e mo'on kadi ɓen ɓe no ruttee faade ka ɓuri jaasude e ngurndan ɗam fii wata ɓe anndu ɓaawo ganndal hay e huunde. A yi'ay leydi ndin ko yoorunde si Men jippinii e dow mayri ndiyam ɗan ndi dilla ndi ƴura ndi fuɗina immorde e kala noone wooɗuɗo
22|6|Ɗum, ko tawde pellet, Alla ko Kanko woni Goonga kan, pellet, O wurnitay mayɓe ɓen, tawde pellet, ko O Hattanɗo e dow kala huunde. @Corrected
22|7|Pellet, Darngal ngal ko aray ngal sikke alaa e maggal, wonnde pellet, Alla immintinay ɓen wonɓe ka genaale
22|8|No e yimɓe ɓen on mo no wennja e fii Alla ko aldaa e ganndal wanaa peewal wanaa deftere nurɗunde(jalbunde)
22|9|Hofuɗo balaaji mu'un [mawnintiniiɗo] fii yo o majjin gaayi Laawol Alla ngol, no woodani mo ka aduna oyeere Men meeɗinoyay mo kadi Ñalnde Darngal Lepte sumoowe ngen
22|10|Ɗum ko sabu ko juuɗe maaɗa ɗen ardini kon. E wonnde pellet, Alla wonaali Tooñoowo jeyaaɓe ɓen
22|11|No e yimɓe ɓen on mo no rewa Alla e dow selindaare; si moƴƴere heɓii mo o tabitira sabu ɗum si jarrabuyee kadi heɓii mo o waylitoo e yeeso makko, o hayrii aduna on e Laakara on ko ɗum tigi woni hayrere ɓanngunde nden
22|12|Himo rewa gaanin Alla kon ko lorrataa mo e kon ko nafataa mo kadi. Ɗum [ko jaŋtaa ɗoo], ko ɗum woni majjere woɗɗunde nden
22|13|Himo rewa on mo lorra muuɗum no ɓuri ɓadaade diini nafa muuɗum kan, bonii welddiɗo bonii kadi wuuridaaɗo
22|14|Pellet, Alla hiMo naada ɓen gomɗinɓe ɓe golli moƴƴi ɗin Aljannaaji no ila sengo ley majji canɗi ɗin, pellet, Alla hiMo waɗa ko O faandii kon. @Corrected
22|15|On wonɗo no sikka wonnde Alla wallataa mo ka aduna e ka Laakara; haray yo o fontu ɓoggol faade ka kammu refti o taƴa ngol yo o ndaaru taw si pewje makko ɗen ittay ko tikkini kon
22|16|Ko wano nii Men Jippiniri nde Aayeeje ɓannguɗe. Pellet, Alla hiMo Fewna on Mo O faandii
22|17|Pellet, ɓen gomɗinɓe e ɓen Yahuudinkooɓe e Saabi'iyankooɓe e Annasaarankooɓe e Majuusinkooɓe e ɓen sirkooɓe, pellet, Alla O seerndoowo hakkunde maɓɓe Ñalnde Darngal. Pellet, Alla e dow kala huunde ko O Seediiɗo
22|18|Enee a yi'aali, wonndema Alla no sujjannde Mo ɓen wonɓe ka kammuuli e ɓen wonɓe ka leydi, naange ngen kadi e lewru ndun e koode ɗen e pelle ɗen e leɗɗe ɗen e daabeeji ɗin e ko ɗuuɗi immorde e yimɓe ɓen, ko ɗuuɗi kadi wajibike e mu'un Lepte ɗen. 22|19|Ɓee ɗoo ɗiɗo ko wennjondirɓe, ɓe wennjondirii fii Joomi maɓɓe ɓen yedduɓe non, taƴanoyte ɓe conci immorde e Yiite fatuɗam yuppee ka dow ko'e maɓɓe
22|20|Hiɗam honciniree(hayniree) ko woni kon ka deedi maɓɓe e guri ɗin kadi

22|24|Ɓe fewnaama faade e ko laaɓi immorde e konngol ngol, ɓe fewnaa kadi faade e Laawol Yettiniingol ngol
22|25|Pellet, ɓen yedduɓe hiɓe faddaade gaayi Laawol Alla ngol e Juulirde Horminnde nden, nden nde Men waɗani ɗum yimɓe ɓen, no fota ter ñiiɓuɗo on e mayre e liigotooɗo on. Kala faalaaɗo ooñorde e mayre tooñe, Men meeɗinay mo immorde e Lepte muusuɗe
22|26|E tuma nde Men Jippinnoo Ibraahiima nokku Suudu ndun, [Men Daali:] Wata a kafidu e Am hay e huunde, laɓɓin Suudu Am ndun fii wanngotooɓe ɓen e darotooɓe ɓen [juula] e ruƴƴooɓe sujja ɓen
22|27|Noddin e yimɓe ɓen fii Hajju ngun, ɓe aray e maaɗa ko ɓe seppooɓe e dow kala ɗehiimba reedu, ɓe aray immorde e kala laawol woɗɗungol
22|28|Fii yo ɓe seedo nafoore maɓɓe, ɓe jaŋtoo Innde Alla e nder ñalɗi anndaaɗi e dow ko O arsiki ɓe kon immorde e muumi neemoraaɗi, ñaamee e majji, ñamminon kadi baaso ɓilliiɗo on
22|29|Refti yo ɓe ittu tuundi maɓɓe ndin, yo ɓe humnu takke maɓɓe ɗen, yo ɓe wanngo Suudu rimdinaa- dun
22|30|Ɗum [ko yamiraɗon], kala mawninɗo Hurumji Alla ɗin haray ɗum ko moƴƴere makko ka Joomi makko. Daginanaama on neemoraaɗi ɗin, si wonaa kon ko janngaa e taweede mo'on, woɗɗitee soɓudi ɗin immorde e sanamuuji, woɗɗitoɗon kadi konngol fenaande ngol
22|31|Newaniiɓe Alla ɓe wanaali sirkanooɓe Mo, kala sirkanɗo Alla no wa'ita wa si o uuyu immorde ka kammu sonndu biftoo mo maaɗum henndu ndun ruuyida e makko [naɓa] e nokkure woɗɗunde

22|33|No woodani on e majji nafaaji haa e dummunne innaaɗo, refti nokku majji on ko ka Suudu Ndimuru
22|34|Men waɗanii kala mofte laawol fii yo ɓe jaŋto Innde Alla e dow ko O arsiki ɓe kon immorde e muumi neemoraaɗi. Reweteeɗo mon On ko Reweteeɗo Gooto ko Kanko jebbilatoɗon, weltinir ɗoftiiɓe ɓen
22|35|Ɓen [tawɓe] si Alla jaŋtaama ɓerɗe maɓɓe ɗen hulay, e muññiiɓe ɓen e dow kon ko heɓi ɓe e ñinnooɓe Julde nden hiɓe nafka goɗɗum e ko Men arsiki ɓe kon
22|36|E gelooɗi [fayɗi] ɗin Men waɗanii on ɗi jeyaaɗum e Maandeeji Alla no woodani on e majji moƴƴere, jaŋtee Innde Alla e dow majji ko ɗi saffiniiɗi si becce majji ɗen yanii haray ñaamee immorde e majji ñamminon kadi yonndiniiɗo e weeɓitotooɗo, ko wano nii, Men eltirani on ɗi belajo'o onon on jarnay
22|37|Hewtoytaa Alla tebbuuli majji wanaa ƴiiƴe majji kadi, kono hewtoy Mo kulol ngol immorde e mo'on. Ko wano nii O eltani on ɗi fii yo on mawnin Alla e dow ko O fewni on kon, weltin moƴƴinɓe ɓen
22|38|Pellet, Alla O solnanay(dunyanay) ɓen gomɗinɓe, pellet, Alla O yiɗaa kala hodoowo heewuɗo geddi

22|40|Ɓen yaltinaaɓe ka galleeji mu'un ko aldaa e goo- nga si wanaa fii tun ɓe wi'ii: "Joomi amen ko Alla". 22|41|Ɓen tawɓe si Men newinanii ɓe ka leydi ɓe ñinnay Julde nden ɓe totta askaal on ɓe yamira ko moƴƴi kon ɓe haɗa ko boni kon. Ko Alla woodani ɓattane fiyakuuji ɗin
22|42|Si ɓe fennii ma, haray gomɗii fenniino ado maɓɓe yimɓe Nuuhu ɓen e Aadinkooɓe ɓen e Samuudinkooɓe ɓen
22|43|E yimɓe Ibraahiima ɓen e yimɓe Luutu ɓen

22|45|No foti hewde e Saare nde Men halki ɗum tawi ko nde tooñunde, hara hinde ajjii e hoore kippudiiji mayre, e woyndu yirbundu e huɓeere toowunde [eggaande]

22|50|Ɓen gomɗinɓe ɓe golli moƴƴi ɗin no woodani ɓe haforanal e arsike tedduɗo

22|52|Men Nulaali ado maaɗa immorde e Nulaaɗo wanaa kadi Annabaajo si wanaa si o janngii Seytaane werloto e nder janki makko kin. Alla itta ko Seytaane werlii kon, refti Alla tabintina Aayeeje Makko ɗen. Alla ko O Annduɗo Ñeeñuɗo
22|53|Fii yo O waɗu ko Seytaane werlotoo ko njarraboye wonannde ɓen ɓe nawnaare woni ka ɓerɗe mu'un e ɓe ɓerɗe mu'un yoori ɓen. Pellet, tooñooɓe ɓen ɓe wonii e lurral woɗɗungal
22|54|Fii yo ɓen okkaaɓe Ganndal ngal anndu pellet, ko [Alqur'aanaare nden woni] Goonga kan immorde ka Joomi maaɗa ɓe gomɗina nde, ɓerɗe maɓɓe ɗen yankinanoo ɗum. Pellet Alla Fewnay ɓen gomɗinɓe faade e Laawol Focciingol
22|55|Ɓen yedduɓe seerataa hiɓe e nder sikke [fii Alqur'aana] haa Darngal ngal ara e maɓɓe e juhayee maaɗum ara e maɓɓe Lepte Ñalaande saɗtunde
22|56|Laamu ngun nden Ñalnde ko Alla heeranii O Ñaawoyay hakkunde maɓɓe, ɓen gomɗinɓe ɓe golli ko moƴƴi ɗin hiɓe e nder Aljannaaji Neemiiɗi
22|57|Ɓen yedduɓe, ɓe fenni kadi Aayeeje Amen ɗen, ɓen ɗon no woodani ɓe lepte hoynooje
22|58|Ɓen feruɓe e Laawol Alla refti ɓe waraa maaɗum ɓe maayi Alla arsikoyay ɓe arsike moƴƴo. Pellet, Alla ko Kanko woni ɓuri Moƴƴude Arsikooɓe
22|59|Ma O naadoyɓe naatirgal ngal ɓe welaa ɗum. Pellet, Alla ko O Annduɗo Muññiiɗo
22|60|Ɗum [ko jaŋtaa ɗoo], kala leptuɗo yeru ko o leptaa kon, refti bewaa e hoore-makko ma Alla wallu mo. Pellet, Alla ko O Yaafotooɗo Surroowo
22|61|Ɗum [ko jaŋtaa ɗoo], ko fii pellet, Alla hiMo naada jemma on e nder ñalorma on, hiMo naada kadi ñalorma on e nder jemma on. Pellet, Alla ko O Nanoowo Yi'oowo
22|62|Ɗum [ko jaŋtaa ɗoo], ko fii pellet, Alla ko Kanko woni Goonga kan pellet, kon ko ɓe noddata gaanin Makko ko ɗum woni meere nden. Pellet, ko Kanko woni Toowuɗo Mawnuɗo On
22|63|Enee, a tinaali wonndema Alla O jippinii ndiyam immorde ka kammu, leydi ndin wonti hecciɗundi? Pellet, Alla ko O Newiiɗo Humpitiiɗo

22|65|Enee, a tinaali wonndema Alla eltani on ko woni kon ka leydi, laaɗe ɗen no dogira ka maaje Yamaruyee Makko on, hiMo jogitii kammu ngun fii wata ngu yanu e hoore leydi ndin si wonaa e duŋayee Makko. Pellet, Alla ko O newaniiɗo yimɓe ɓen Yurmteeɗo [ɓe]

22|68|Si ɓe wennjii ma, Maaku: "Ko Alla woni Annduɗo ko golloton kon

22|70|Enee, a anndaali wonndema Alla hiMo Anndi ko woni kon ka kammu e ka leydi, pellet, ɗum no e nder Deftere. Pellet, ɗum [ko jaŋtaa ɗoo] no newanii Alla
22|71|Hiɓe rewa gaanin Alla kon ko Dalil jippinaaka e fii mu'un, e kon ko ganndal alanaa ɓe e mu'un. Alanaa tooñooɓe ɓen walloowo
22|72|Si jannganaama ɓe Aayeeje Amen ɗen ɓannguɗe a annday e geece ɓen yedduɓe mettinaare hiɓe ɗeɓa yanude e ɓen jannganayɓe ɓe Aayeeje Amen ɗen. Maaku: "Yo mi habru on ko ɓuri bonde e ɗum mooɗon [ko jaŋtanaɗon kon] ko Yiite ngen Alla fodii nge ɓen yedduɓe bonii ruttorde
22|73|Ko onon yo yimɓe, misal piyaama jentee ngal, pellet ɓen ɓe noddoton gaanin Alla, ɓe tagaa hay coongil, hay sinndo ɓe mooɓondiriino fii ɗum. Si coongil(mbuubu)ngil jattii ɓe goɗɗum ɓe hattantaake jaɓtugol ngil ɗum. Ɗaɓɓuɗo on e ɗaɓɓaaɗo on fow no lo'i
22|74|Ɓe mawniniraali Alla no O haani Mawninirde non. Pellet, Alla ko O Dolnuɗo Tedduɗo
22|75|Alla no suɓoo immorde e Malaa'ikaaɓe ɓen Nulaaɓe e yimɓe ɓen kadi. Pellet, Alla ko O Nanoowo Yi'oowo
22|76|Himo Anndi ko woni kon hedde yeeso maɓɓe e ko woni kon hedde ɓaawo maɓɓe, ko faade ka Alla fiyakuuji ɗin ruttetee
22|77|Ko onon yo ɓen gomɗinɓe, Ruƴƴee Sujjon Rewon Joomi mo'on, gollon ko moƴƴi kon belajo'o onon on maloyte
22|78|Waɗiree Jihaadi fii Alla no Jihaadi haaniri non, Kanko O Suɓike on O waɗanaali on ɓitteende ka nder Diina, Diina baaba mooɗon Ibraahiima ko Kanko inni on julɓe ko adii [ndee Alqur'aanaare] e nder mayre kadi, fii yo Nulaaɗo on laato seedo e hoore-mo'on onon kadi wonon seeditoytooɓe e hoore yimɓe ɓen. Ñiiɓnee e Julde nden totton Jakka on jogitee Alla, ko Kanko woni Giɗo mooɗon moƴƴii giɗo moƴƴii walloowo on
23|1|Gomɗii malaama gomɗinɓe ɓen
23|2|Ɓen hulooɓe ka nder Julde maɓɓe koɓe yankiniiɓe
23|3|E ɓen ɗurniiɓe gaayi rayrayti( bolle meere)
23|4|E ɓen ittooɓe jakka on
23|5|E ɓen reenuɓe farjuuji maɓɓe ɗin
23|6|Si wanaa e dow sonnaaɓe maɓɓe maaɗum ɓe ñaame maɓɓe ɗen jeyi(horbe), haray kamɓe ɓe wonaa feleteeɓe
23|7|On mo ɗaɓɓi ɓaawo ɗum, haray ko ɓen woni jaggitooɓe ɓen
23|8|E ɓen aynuɓe koolaaje maɓɓe e aadiiji maɓɓe ɗin
23|9|E ɓen ɓe kañun koɓe reenuɓe e dow Julɗe maɓɓe ɗen
23|10|Ɓee [siforɓe ɗii sifaaji ɗoo] ko kamɓe woni ronooɓe ɓen
23|11|Ɓen ronoyayɓe Firdawsi on kamɓe ko ɓe duumotooɓe e nder makko
23|12|Gomɗii Men tagii neɗɗanke on immorde e lasili loopal
23|13|Refti Men waɗi mo toɓɓere [maniiyu] e nder ñiiɓirde huɓindiinde
23|14|Refti Men Tagi toɓɓere nden heɗɗere, Men Tagi heɗɗere nden huyre, Men Tagi huyre nden ƴi'e, Men holtini ƴi'e ɗen teewu. Refti Men fuɗɗanii mo Tagu woo, barkanii Alla Moƴƴo Taguɗo
23|15|Refti onon ɓaawo ɗum ko on maayooɓe
23|16|Refti pellet, onon Ñalnde Darngal on imminoyte
23|17|Gomɗii Men Tagii dow mooɗon ɗati jeeɗiɗi, Men wonaali kadi welsindiiɓe gaayi tagu ngun
23|18|Men jippini immorde ka kammu ndiyam e emmbere [haaju tagu ngun], Men ndewni ɗam ka leydi, pellet, Menen ko Men Hattanɓe e dow naɓugol ɗam
23|19|Men fuɗɗani on sabu majjam gese immorde e tamarooje e inabuuje, no woodani on nder ton dimɗe ɗuuɗuɗe ko e majje ñaamoton
23|20|E leggal ngal no yalta immorde to Tuuri Siinaa hingal fuɗina guƴam [nebban wujeteeɗam] e li'am [maafirɗam] wonannde ñaamooɓe
23|21|Pellet, no woodani on e neemoraaɗi ɗin tasakuyee, Meɗen yarna on goɗɗun e ko woni kon ka deedi majji, no woodani on e majji nafaaji ɗuuɗuɗi, ko immorde e majji kadi ñaamoton
23|22|Ko e hoore-majji e hoore laaɗe ɗen ronndeteɗon
23|23|Gomɗii Men Nulii Nuuhu e yimɓe makko ɓen, o maaki : "Ko onon yo yimɓe am, rewee Alla. Reweteeɗo alanaa on ko woori Mo. Enee, on hulatah
23|24|Hooreeɓe mbatu ngun wi'ani ɓen yedduɓe immorde e yimɓe makko ɓen: "Oo wonaali si ko o ɓanndinke yeru mo'on himo faalaa nde o ɓurnotoo e dow mooɗon. Sinndo Alla muuyino O jippinayno Malaa'ikaaɓe, men naniraali ɗum baabiraaɓe amen aranɓe ɓen
23|25|Kanko o wonaali si wanaa ko o gorko mo jinna woni e mu'un, habbitee mo tun haa seeɗa
23|26|O maaki: "Joom am, wallam e ko ɓe fennimi kon
23|27|Men wahayini faade e makko yo o lesu laana kan e dennka Amen e Wahayu Amen, si Yamiroore Amen nden arii huɓɓinirde nden pullitike [ndiyam] naadu e nder makka immorde e kala nooneeji ɗin ɗiɗi-ɗiɗi. E koreeji ma, si wanaa ɓen konngol ngol aditii e mu'un, wata a haaldu e am fii ɓen tooñuɓe, pellet, kamɓe ko ɓe yooleteeɓe
23|28|Si a fotondirii an e ɓen wonnduɓe e maaɗa e dow laana kan, haray maaku: "Yettoore nden ko Alla woodani, On dannduɗo Men immorde e yimɓe tooñooɓe ɓen
23|29|Maaku: "Joomam, jippinam e jipporde barkinaande ko An woni Moƴƴo Jippinoowo

23|33|Batu e yimɓe makko ɓen yedduɓe ɓe fenni hawroygol e Laakara on, Men neemini ɓe ka ngurdan aduna wi*i: "Oo wonaali si wanaa ɓanndunke yeru mooɗon himo ñaama ko ñaamoton kon himo yara kadi ko yaroton kon

23|45|Refti Men Nuli Muusaa e musiɗɗo makko on Haaruuna wonndude e Aayeeje Amen ɗen e hujja ɓannguɗo

23|51|Ko onon yo Nulaaɓe, ñaamee immorde e laaɓuɗi ɗin gollon ko moƴƴi, pellet Min, Miɗo Anndi ko golloton kon
23|52|E pellet, kaa Diina mo'on ko Diina woota, ko Min woni Joomi mo'on hulee Lam
23|53|Ɓe taƴi fiyaake maɓɓe on hakkunde maɓɓe dente, kala fedde no farnora ko woni kon ka mayre
23|54|Ɗalu ɓe e siwrere nden haa e dummunne
23|55|Enee, hara ɓe sikku wonndema ko Men ɓeydiri ɓe kon immorde e jawdi e ɓiɗɓe
23|56|Men yaccinanay ɓe e moƴƴereeji, ko woni ɓe so'aa
23|57|Pellet, ɓen ɓe kañum immorde e kulol Joomi maɓɓe hara ko ɓe huluɓe

23|61|Ɓen [sifaaɓe ɗii sifaaji ɗoo] hiɓe yaccoo e moƴƴereeji ɗin, hara kamɓe ko ɓe adotooɓe e majji
23|62|Men fawaali wonkii si wanaa fodde bawɗe makki, no ka Amen Deftere wowlaynde Goonga kan, hara kamɓe ɓe tooñoytaake
23|63|Ko woni, ɓerɗe maɓɓe ɗen no e welsungo immorde e ɗum, no woodani ɓe kadi golle gaanin ɗum ko kamɓe gollate ɗe
23|64|Haa si Men nanngirii neeminaaɓe maɓɓe ɓen Lepte ɗen jaka yoo kamɓe hiɓe haaca
23|65|Wata on haacu hannde, pellet onon, on wallataake immorde e Amen

23|68|Enee, hara ɓe teskaaki konngol ngol, kaa hara aru e maɓɓe ko araali e baabiraaɓe maɓɓe adinooɓe ɓen
23|69|Kaa ɓe anndaali Nulaaɗo maɓɓe on, hara kamɓe ko ɓe faytuɓe mo
23|70|Kaa hara ɓe wi'ay feetere no e makko? Ko woni, o addanii ɓe Goonga kan ɓurɓe heewude e maɓɓe ko añuɓe Goonga kan
23|71|Sinndo Alqur'aana jokkuno beleeɗe maɓɓe ɗen, kammuuli ɗin e leydi ndin bonayno e ɓen wonuɓe e majji, ko woni, Men addaniiɓe waaju maɓɓe ngun, kamɓe koɓe ɗurniiɓe gaayi waaju maɓɓe ngun
23|72|Kaa a tori ɓe ngeenaari? [Awa] ko ngeenaari Joomi maaɗa ndin ɓuri moƴƴude, ko Kanko woni Moƴƴo Arsikoowo
23|73|Pellet, an hiɗa noddude faade e Laawol Focciingol

23|75|Sinndo Men Yurmino ɓe, Men hunci ko heɓi ɓe kon immorde e lorra, ɓe duumotono e nder bewre maɓɓe hiɓe wemmboo
23|76|Gomɗii Men nanngirii ɓe Lepte ɗen, ɓe hoykinanaaki Joomi maɓɓe ɓe yankinaaki
23|77|Haa si Men udditii e dow maɓɓe dammbugal marungal Lepte saɗtuɗe, e jaka, kamɓe e nder ɗum ko ɓe taƴii ɓe
23|78|Ko Kanko woni On fuɗɗanƊo on nanɗe ɗen e giiɗe ɗen e ɓerɗe ɗen, fanɗii ko yettoton

23|80|Ko Kanko woni On Mo no wurna O wara no woodani Mo luutindirgol jemma on e ñalorma on, enee, kaa on hakkiltah

23|91|Alla jogitaaki ɓiɗɗo, reweteeɗo laataaki wonndude e Makko, e jaka [si waɗum waɗuno] kala reweteeɗo yaadayno e ko o tagi kon, yoga e maɓɓe townitotono e dow yoga. Senayee wonanii Alla e gaayi kon ko ɓe sifotoo
23|92|Annduɗo ko wirnii kon e ko seedaa kon O Toowii e gaayi ko ɓe sirkata kon
23|93|Maaku: "Jooma am si A hollii lam ko ɓe fodaa kon

23|96|Duñir nden huunde ɓurnde moƴƴude [huunde] bonunde nden, ko Menen Anndi ko ɓe sifoto kon

23|100|Belajo'o men, mi gollay ko moƴƴi e nder kon ko mi accunoo, ɗum waɗataa, ngol ko kanngol ko kanko wowli ngol, no hedde ɓaawo maɓɓe heedo haa Ñalnde nde ɓe imminoytee
23|101|Si wuttaama ka alaadu, haray askaaji alah hakkunde maɓɓe nden Ñalnde, ɓe lanndandirtah
23|102|Kala on mo jisti(teddi) manndake (peesirgal)muuɗum, haray ko ɓen ɗon woni maloyteeɓe ɓen

23|104|Yiite ngen no sunna geece maɓɓe ɗen, hara kamɓe e nder magge ko ɓe ñirɓiniiɓe

23|118|Maaku: "Jooma am, Yaafo Yurmo ko An Ɓuri Moƴƴude Yurmeteeɓe ɓen
24|1|Simoore, Men jippinii nde Men farlii nde, Men jippini e nder mayre Aayeeje ɓannguɗe belajo'o onon on waajitoto
24|2|Debbo jinoowo on e gorko jeenoowo on foccee gooto kala e maɓɓe paatawol(looci) teemedere, wata yurmeende maɓɓe nanngu on e fii Diina Alla kan, si tawii on laatike hiɗon gomɗini Alla e Ñalaande Laakara nden. Yo seedo foccugol ɓe ngol jamaa immorde e gomɗinɓe ɓen
24|3|Gorko jinoowo on o resataa si wonaa debbo jeenoowo maaɗum sirkoowo, debbo jinoowo on resatah mo si wanaa gorko jinoowo maaɗum sirkoowo, ɗum harminaama e dow gomɗinɓe ɓen
24|4|E ɓen ɓe no tukka rewɓe saŋiiɓe ɓen refti hara ɓe addaali seedeeɓe nayo, haray piyee ɓe paatawol(looci) cappanɗe jeetati. Wata on jaɓan ɓe seedagol poomaa. Ɓen ɗon, ko kamɓe woni Faasiqiiɓe ɓen
24|5|Si wanaa ɓen tuubuɓe ɓaawo ɗum ɓe moƴƴini. Pellet, Alla ko O Surroowo Yurmeteeɗo
24|6|E ɓen ɓe no tukka sonnaaɓe maɓɓe ɓen hara laatanaaki ɓe seedeeɓe si wanaa wonkiiji maɓɓe ɗin, ko yo goɗɗo e maɓɓe seedo seedeeji nayi [o woondira] Alla pellet, kanko ko e goonguɓe ɓen o jeyaa
24|7|Jowaɓun ɗum, wonndema yo kuddi Alla wonu e dow makko si o laatike jeyaaɗo e fenooɓe ɓen
24|8|Ɓe dunyira e [sonnaajo on] lepte ɗen, nde o seedotoo seedeeji nayi [o woondira] Alla, pellet [gorko on] ko e fenooɓe ɓen o jeyaa
24|9|Jowaɓun ɗum, ko nde Alla tikkata e dow makko si [gorko on] laatike ko e goonguɓe ɓen o jeyaa
24|10|Sinndo wanaano Ɓural Alla ngal e dow mooɗon e Yurmeende Makko nden, e wonndema Alla ko O jaɓoowo tuubuubuye Ñeeñuɗo
24|11|Pellet, ɓen adduɓe penaale ɗen ko ɓe jamaa jeyaaɗo e mooɗon, wata on sikku ɗum ko bone mo'on; ko woni ɗum ko moƴƴere mo'on. No woodani kala neɗɗo immorde e maɓɓe ko o faggitii kon e junuubu, on fawtiiɗo mawɗum [junuubu on] immorde e maɓɓe, no woodani mo Lepte mawɗe
24|12|Ko haanunoo tuma nde nanuɗon ɗum, worɓe gomɗinɓe ɓen e rewɓe gomɗinɓe ɓen ɓe yananee ka wonkiiji maɓɓe ko moƴƴi, ɓe wi'a: "Ɗum ko penaale ɓannguɗe nii
24|13|Ko haanunoo ko nde ɓe addata e ɗum seedeeɓe nayo, si ɓe addaali seedeeɓe ɓen; haray ɓen ɗon, ka Alla ko kamɓe woni fenooɓe ɓen
24|14|Sinndo wonaano Ɓural Alla ngal e Yurmeende Makko nden e dow mooɗon ka aduna e ka laakara Lepte mawɗe meemayno on fii kon ko ukkiɗon e muuɗum
24|15|Tuma nde werloraynoɗon ɗum ɗennɗe mooɗon, wowliron kunnduɗe mooɗon kon ko ganndal alanah on e muuɗum sikkon ɗum kadi ko newiiɗum, hara non ɗum ko mawnuɗom ka Alla
24|16|Ko haanunoo tuma nanuɗon nde, wi'on: "Haanaa men nde men wowlata e dum, Senayee woodanii Ma, ɗum ko fenaande mawnde nii
24|17|Alla no waajaade on fii wata on fillo sugu [ndee fenaande] poomaa, si tawii on laatike gomɗinɓe
24|18|Alla no ɓannginannde on Aayeeje ɗen Alla ko O Annduɗo Ñeeñuɗo
24|19|Pellet, ɓen yiɗuɓe yo bone ɗen saako e [hoore] ɓen gomɗinɓe; no woodani ɓe Lepte muusuɗe ka aduna e ka Laakara. Alla no Anndi, onon on anndah
24|20|Sinndo wanaano Ɓural Alla ngal e dow mooɗon e Yurmeende Makko nden e tawde pellet, Alla ko O Newiiɗo Hinndotooao
24|21|Ko onon ɓen gomɗinɓe, wata on jokku ɗate Seytaane ɗen, kala jokkuɗo ɗate Seytaane ɗen, pellet, o yamiray [mo] ko boni kon e ko añaa kon. Sinndo wonaano Ɓural Alla ngal e dow mooɗon e Yurmeende Makko nden; hay e gooto e mooɗon laaɓataano poomaa, kono Alla hiMo laɓɓina on mo O Muuyi. Alla ko O Nanoowo Annduɗo
24|22|Wata joomiraaɓe ɓural ngal e yaajeende nden e mooɗon woondu wonndema ɓe okkortaa ɓadondiraaɓe ɓen e ɓilliiɓe ɓen e feruɓe ɓen ka Laawol Alla, yo ɓe yaafo. Kaa on yiɗaa yo Alla yawtan on? Alla ko O Yawtoowo Yurmeteeɗo
24|23|Pellet, ɓen wonuɓe tukkude [sonnaaɓe] saŋiiɓe welsindiiɓe gomɗinɓe, ɓe huɗaama ka aduna e ka Laakara no woodani ɓe Lepte mawɗe
24|24|Ñalnde seedoytoo e dow maɓɓe ɗenɗe maɓɓe ɗen e juuɗe maɓɓe ɗen e koyɗe maɓɓe ɗen, ko ɓe laatinoo kon hiɓe golla
24|25|Nden Ñalnde Alla huuɓinanay ɓe [njoɓdi] Diina maɓɓe Goongaha kan, ɓe annda pellet, Alla ko Kanko woni Goonga Ɓannguka kan
24|26|Rewɓe soɓuɓe ɓen ko fii worɓe soɓuɓe ɓen. Worɓe soɓuɓe ɓen ko fii rewɓe soɓuɓe ɓen. Rewɓe laaɓuɓe ɓen ko fii worɓe laaɓuɓe ɓen, worɓe laaɓuɓe ɓen ko fii rewɓe laaɓuɓe ɓen. Ɓee ɗoo ko hisnaaɓe e kon ko ɓe wowlata, no woodani ɓe haforaneede e arsike tedduɗo
24|27|Ko onon yo gomɗinɓe, wata on naatu e cuuɗi tanaa cuuɗi mo'on ɗin haa duŋinoɗon salminon e dow yimɓe majji ɓen, ko ɗum ɓuri moƴƴannde on. Bela jo'o onon on waajitoto
24|28|Si on tawaali nder ton goɗɗo, wata on naatu ton haa duŋaneɗon, si on wi'aama: "Yiltee" haray yiltee, ko ɗum ɓuri laaɓannde on. Alla non hiMo Anndi ko golloton kon
24|29|Bakkaatu fawaaki on nde naatoton e cuuɗi ɗi hoɗiraaka hara no e nder majji miranhoy mo'on, Alla non hiMo Anndi ko wonɗon e feññinde e ko wonɗon e suuɗude
24|30|Maakan worɓe gomɗinɓe ɓen yo ɓe heltu ndarɗe maɓɓe ɗen ɓe reena farjuuji maɓɓe ɗin, ko ɗum ɓurata laɓɓinnde ɓe. Pellet, Alla ko O Humpitiiɗo ko ɓe huuwata
24|31|Maakan rewɓe gomɗinɓe ɓen yo ɓe heltu ndarɗe maɓɓe ɗen, ɓe reena farjuuji maɓɓe ɗin, wata ɓe feññin cuɗaari maɓɓe ndin si wanaa ko feeñi kon e mayri. Yo ɓe fawu tiggaaje maɓɓe ɗen ka becce maɓɓe, wata ɓe feññinan cuɗaari maɓɓe ndin si wanaa genndiraaɓe maɓɓe ɓen maaɗum baabiraaɓe maɓɓe maaɗum baabiraaɓe genndiraaɓe maɓɓe maaɗum ɓiɗɓe maɓɓe, maaɗum ɓiɗɓe genndiraaɓe maɓɓe maaɗum musiɗɓe maɓɓe, maaɗum ɓiɗɓe musiɗɓe maɓɓe, maaɗum ɓiɗɓe banndiraaɓe maɓɓe, maaɗum sonnaaɓe maɓɓe, maaɗum ɓen ɓe ɓe jeyiri ñaame maɓɓe maaɗum ɓen worɓe jokkooɓe ɓe haaju mun alaa e rewɓe, maaɗum boobo mo ƴellitaaki e awraaji sonnaaɓe ɓen. Wata ɓe tappindir koyɗe maɓɓe ɗen fii yo Annde ko ɓe suuɗi kon immorde e cuɗaari maɓɓe. Tuubee ruttoɗon ka Alla on fow mo'on, ko onon yo gomɗinɓe bela jo'o on malete
24|32|Resinee ɓe resaali ɓen e mooɗon e moƴƴuɓe ɓen immorde e muccuɓe mooɗon e horɓe mooɗon, si ɓe laatike waasuɓe Alla alɗinay ɓe immorde e Ɓural Makko ngal, Alla ko O Yaajuɗo Annduɗo
24|33|Ɓe heɓaali feere resugol ɓen yo ɓe habbo haa Alla alɗinira ɓe Ɓural Makko ngal. Ɓen wonuɓe ɗaɓɓude soottaade e ɓen ɓe ñaame mooɗon jeyi, soottaadede ɓe si on anndii e maɓɓe moƴƴere, jonnee ɓe immorde e jawdi Alla ndin, ndin ndi O jonni on, wata on waawnu horɓe mooɗon ɓen e fii jeeno, si ɓe faandike saŋaade, wata on ɗaɓɓu jawkal ngurndam aduna, kala waawnuuɗo ɓe pellet, Alla ɓaawo baawnugol ɓe ko O Surroowo Yurmiteeɗo
24|34|Gomɗii Men jippinii e mooɗon Aayeeje ɓannguɗe e misal immorde e ɓeya wulinooɓe ko adii on e waaju wonannde hulooɓe [Alla] ɓen
24|35|Ko Alla woni Ndaygu kammuuli ɗin e leydi ndin, sifa Ndaygu Makko ngun ko wano tuɗɗere hara no e mayre pitilol(lampu), pitilol ngol wona e nder biiniiri, biiniiri ndin hara hindi wa'i wa hoodere jalbunde hinde huɓɓa immorde e leggal barkinaangal nebbantewal ngal wonaa funnaangeyankowal ngal wonaa hirnaangeyankowal nebban maggal ɗan no ɓadoo jalbude, hay si yiite meemaali ɗan, ndaygu e hoore ndaygu, Alla no fewnira ndaygu Makko ngun on mo O Muuyi, Alla no piyana yimɓe ɓen mise, Alla ko O Annduɗo kala huunde. @Corrected
24|36|E nder cuuɗi ɗi Alla duŋii(sakkiti) yo darne Innde Makko jantee e nder majji Subunhinanee Mo nder majji ka bimmbi e ka kiikiiɗe
24|37|Worɓe ɓe njulaaku e ngeyngu maapintaa ɗum gaayi jaŋtagol Alla e ñimnugol Julde nden e tottu- gol Jakka on, hiɓe huli Ñalaande nde waylitoytoo e muuɗum ɓerɗe ɗen e giiɗe ɗen
24|38|Fii yo Alla yoɓoyɓe ko ɓuri moƴƴude ko ɓe gollunoo kon, O ɓeydana ɓe e Ɓural Makko ngal. Alla no arsika on mo O Muuyi ko Aldaa hasboore
24|39|Ɓen yedduɓe, golle maɓɓe ɗen no wa'i wa merere wonunde e boowal, ɗonɗaaɗo on no sikka ko nde ndiyam, haa si o arii e mayre o tawataa hay e huunde, o tawa Alla ka Makko O huuɓinana mo hasboore makko nden, Alla ko O Yaawuɗo Hasboore. @Corrected
24|40|Maaɗum ko wano niɓe e maayo luggungo, no suddi ngo benpeƴƴe no dow maggo benpeƴƴe no dow majje duule, niɓe yoga e majje no e dow yoga, si o yaltinii junngo makko ngon o ɓadotaako yi'ugol ngo. On mo Alla waɗanaali ndaygu hara o alaa ndaygu
24|41|Enee, a yi'aali wonndema Alla no subuhinanaade Mo ɓen wonuɓe ka kammuuli e ka leydi e colli ɗin kadi ko saffiniiɗi? Gooto kala e ɗii gomɗii anndii julde mu'un nden e subuhinaali mu'un ɗin, Alla ko O Annduɗo ko ɓe Huuwata
24|42|Ko Alla heeranii Laamu kammuuli ɗin e leydi ndin, ko faade ka Alla woni waɗtinirde nden
24|43|Enee, a yi'aali wonndema Alla hiMo sogga duulere, refti O hawtindira nde, refti O waɗa nde fawondirnde hiɗa yi'a toɓo ngon no yalta e nder mayre, ngo jippoo immorde ka kammu, immorde e pelle no e nder mayre marmalle hiMo hewtina ɗe on mo O Muuyi, hiMo pottina ɗe on mo O Muuyi? Ndaneeri maƴe mayre no do'a naɓude giiɗe ɗen
24|44|Alla hiMo waylita jemma on e ñalorma on, pellet, na wonii e ɗum tasakuyee wonannde joomiraaɓe giiɗe ɓen
24|45|Ko Alla tagii kala daabe hun immorde e ndiyam, no e majji yaarooji reedu muuɗum, no e majji yaarooji koyɗe muuɗm no e majji kadi yaarooji [koyɗe] nayi. Alla hiMo Taga ko O Muuyi, pellet, Alla ko O hattanɗo kala huunde
24|46|Gomɗii Men jippinii Aayeeje ɓannguɗe, Alla no fewna on mo O muuyii faade e Laawol foccii ngol
24|47|Hiɓe wi'a: "Men gomɗinii Alla e Nulaaɗo on, men ɗoftike, refti huccita fedde goo e maɓɓe, ɓaawo ɗum, ɓen wonaali gomɗinɓe
24|48|Si ɓe noddaama faade ka Alla e Nulaaɗo Makko on fii yo o ñaawu hakkunde maɓɓe, tawa fedde goo e maɓɓe ko ɓe ɗuurniiɓe
24|49|Si tawii ko kamɓe mari goonga kan, ɓe aray ka makko ko ɓe ɗoftiiɓe
24|50|Enee, ko nawnaare woni ka ɓerɗe maɓɓe, kaa ɓe sikkiti, kaa ɓe hulu wata Alla e Nulaaɗo Makko on tooñu ɓe? Ko woni, ɓee ko kamɓe woni tooñooɓe ɓen
24|51|Anndu ko woni konngol gomɗinɓe ɓen si ɓe noddaama faade ka Alla e Nulaaɗo Makko on fii yo o ñaawu hakkunde maɓɓe, ko nde ɓe wi'ata: "Men nanii men ɗoftike." Ɓen ɗon ko kamɓe woni malaaɓe ɓen
24|52|Kala ɗoftiiɗo Alla e Nulaaɗo Makko on o huli Alla o rentii [e Lepte Makko ɗen] haray ɓen ɗon ko kamɓe woni malaaɓe ɓen
24|53|Ɓe woondiri Alla, e hattirde goondooje maɓɓe, si a yamirii ɓe ma ɓe yaltu sanne. Maaku: "wata on woondu, ɗoftaare no anndaa, pellet, Alla ko humpitiiɗo ko golloton
24|54|Maaku: "Ɗoftee Alla ɗoftoɗon Nulaaɗo on". Si ɓe huccitii(runtiima) anndu ko fawii mo ko, ko o roondaa kon, no fawii on ko roonda ɗon kon, si on ɗoftike mo on feeway, fawaaki Nulaaɗo on si wanaa yottinngol ɓanngungol
24|55|Alla Fodii ɓen gomɗinɓe e mooɗon ɓe golli moƴƴi ɗin O lontinay ɓe ka leydi wano O lontinirnoo non ɓen adiiɓe ɓe, ma O weeɓinan ɓe diina maɓɓe ka O welanaa ɓe, ma O wattitan ɓe ɓaawo kulol maɓɓe ngol hoolaare, Yo ɓe rewam wata ɓe sirkanam hay e huunde. Kala yedduɗo ɓaawo ɗum haray ɓen ɗon ko kamɓe woni faasiqiiɓe ɓen
24|56|Ñiiɓee e Julde totton Jakka on ɗoftoɗon kadi Nulaaɗo on, bela jo'o on Yurmete
24|57|Wata a sikku ɓeen yedduɓe ɓe laawoto ka leydi, jaaƴorde maɓɓe nden ko ka Yiite, pellet, bonii wattnde
24|58|Ko onon yo gomɗinɓe, yo sakkintino e mooɗon ɓen ɓe ñaame mooɗon jeyi, e ɓen ɓe yottaaki koyɗol immorde e mooɗon, laabi tati ko adii Julde Peeral nden, e tuma wallinton conci mooɗon ka njolloro e ka ɓaawo Julde geeƴe ko awraaji mooɗon tati non. Bakkaatu fawaaki on fawaaki ɓe ɓaawo majji, jinndooɓe hakkunde mooɗon, yoga e mooɗon e dow yoga. Ko wano nii Alla ɓanngini- rani on Aayeeje ɗen Alla ko O Annduɗo Ñeeñuɗo
24|59|Si sukaaɓe mooɗon yottike kellefuyee, yo ɓe sakkitinono wano duŋinornoo non ɓen adiiɓe ɓe, ko wano nii Alla ɓannginiranta on Aayeeje Makko ɗen, Alla ko O Annduɗo Ñeeñuɗo
24|60|E sonnaaɓe jottiiɓe ɓen, ɓen ɓe jortaaki desal bakkaatu fawaaki ɓe nde ɓe wallinta conci maɓɓe ɗin hara ɓe wonaa feññinɓe cuɗaari, ko nde ɓe nantotoo ɓuri moƴƴannde ɓe, Alla ko O Nanoowo Annduɗo
24|61|Bakkaatu fawaaki bunɗu on, bakkaatu fawaaki laƴuɗo on, bakkaatu fawaaki nawnuɗo on, fawaaki e wonkiiji mooɗon nde ñaamoton ka cuuɗi mooɗon maaɗum ka cuuɗi baabiraaɓe mooɗon, maaɗum ka cuuɗi neeniraaɓe mooɗon, maaɗum ka cuuɗi musiɗɓe mooɗon, maaɗum ka cuuɗi banndiraaɓe mooɗon, maaɗum ka cuuɗi bappiraaɓe mooɗon, maaɗum ka cuuɗi yaayiraaɓe mooɗon, maaɗom ka cuuɗi kaawiraaɓe mooɗon, maaɗum ka cuuɗi neeniraaɓe mooɗon ka dewol, maaɗum ɗin ɗi jogiɗon cottirɗe muuɗum, maaɗum giɗo mooɗon. Bakkaatu fawaaki on nde hawtoton ñaamon maaɗum ñaamon ko on sertuɓe. Si on naatay e cuuɗi salminee e dow wonkiiji mooɗon, hiwraango immorde ka Alla barkinaango laaɓungo, ko wano nii Alla ɓannguniranta on Aayeeje ɗen belajo'o onon on haqqilay
24|62|Anndu gomɗinɓe ɓen ko ɓen gomɗinɓe Alla e Nulaaɗo Makko on, si ɓe laatike hiɓe wonndi e makko e dow fiyaake moftuɗo, ɓe yahatah haa ɓe duŋinoo e makko, pellet, ɓen ɗaɓɓirayɓe ma duŋayee ko ɓen ɗon woni gomɗinɓe Alla e Nulaaɗo Makko on, si ɓe ɗaɓɓirii ma duŋayee fii yoga e fiyaake maɓɓe, duŋano on mo yiɗuɗaa [duŋanaade] e maɓɓe, insinanoɗaa ɓe ka Alla. Pellet, Alla ko O Surroowo Yurmeteeɗo
24|63|Wata on waɗu noddugol Nulaaɗo on hakkunde mooɗon wano noddugol yoga e mooɗon yoga. Gomɗii Alla no Anndi ɓen sortotooɓe e mooɗon e moltagol, ɓen wonuɓe lunndaade yamaruyee makko on, yo ɓe rento fii wata fitina hiɓu ɓe maaɗum Lempte muusuɗe heɓa ɓe
24|64|Ko non woniri, pellet, ko Alla heeranii ko woni kon ka kammuuli e ka leydi gomɗii hiMo Anndi ko wonuɗon e hoore mu'un kon, Ñalnde ɓe ruttetee faade ka Makko O yeetoo ɓe ko ɓe gollunoo kon. Alla ko O Annduɗo kala huunde
25|1|Mawnii On Jippinɗo Serndoore nden e dow jeyaaɗo Makko on fii yo wonan winndire nden jertinoowo
25|2|On Mo woodanii ɗum Laamu kammuuli ɗin e leydi ndin, o jogitaaki ɓiɗɗo laatanaaki Mo kadi kafidaaɗo ka Laamu. O tagii kala huunde O eɓɓindiinde e eɓɓugol
25|3|Ɓe jogitii gaanin Makko reweteeɗi ɗi tagaani huunde kannji ko ɗi tagaaɗi, ɗi maranah ko'e majji lorra wanaa nafa ɗi marah mayde wanaa ngurndan wanaa Immital
25|4|Ɓen yedduɓe wi'i: "Ndee [Alqur'aanaare] wonaali si wonah pene ɗi o fefindii ɗum, walli mo e hoore majje yimɓe goo". Gomɗii ɓe addii tooñe e bagamma
25|5|Ɓe wi'i: "Ko nde tinndi adinooɓe o winnditi ɗi hiɗi fidanee mo bimmbi e kiikiiɗe
25|6|Maaku: "Jippinii nde On Annduɗo ngunndoo on ka kammuuli e ka leydi, pellet, Kanko O Laatike Surroowo Yurmeteeɗo
25|7|Ɓe wi'i: "Ko heɓi oo Nulaaɗo, himo ñaama ñaametee himo yaha kadi ka lokooji(jeereeji)°? Ko haanunoo ko nde jippintee e makko Maalaa'ikaajo o laatoo wonndude e makko jertinoowo
25|8|Maaɗum werlee e makko ngalu, maaɗum laatanoo mo ngesa o ñaama e mabba. Tooñooɓe ɓen wi'i: "On jokkaali si wonaa gorko mbilɗaaɗo
25|9|Ndaarii [yo Nulaaɗo] ko honno ɓe piyiranay maa mise, ɓe majjii ɓe hattantaake [heɓude] laawol
25|10|Mawnii On tawɗo si O Muuyii O waɗane moƴƴere, no e ɗum gese no ila ley majje canɗe ɗen, O waɗane kadi kuɓeeje
25|11|Ko woni, ɓe fennu Darngo ngo, Men heblorani ɓen fennuɓe Darngal ngal Yiite ooyunge
25|12|Si nge yi'ii ɓe immorde e nokkuure woɗɗunde nananee nge tikkere e faraango
25|13|Si ɓe werlaama e nder magge e nokkuure ɓittunde ko ɓe sinndindiraaɓe, ɓe nodda ton halakuyee
25|14|Wata on noddu hannde halakuyee gooto, noddee halakuyeeji buy
25|15|Maaku: "Enee, ko ɗum ɓuri moƴƴude, kaa ko Aljanna luttoowo on, on mo hulooɓe Alla ɓen fodaa? O laatanike ɓe njoɓdi e wattinirde
25|16|No woodani ɓe nder ton ko ɓe welaa, ko ɓe ñiiɓooɓe, ɗum laatike e dow Joomi maaɗa Fodoore lannditeteende
25|17|Ñalnde O mooɓidoyta ɓe e ko ɓe rewaynoo kon gaanin Alla, O Daala: "Enee, ko onon majjini ɓee jeyaaɓe Am, kaa ko kamɓe majji Laawol ngol
25|18|Ɗi wi'a: "Senayee wonanii Ma, haananah men nde men jogitotoo gaanin Maaɗa immorde e reweteeɓe, kono, A dakmintinii ɓe e baabiraaɓe maɓɓe ɓen haa ɓe yejjiti waaju ngun ɓe laatii yimɓe halkiiɓe
25|19|Gomɗii ɓe fennii on, sabu ko wi'oton kon, ɓe hattantah yiltugol [Lepte ɗen] wanaa wallude, kala tooñuɗo e mooɗon Men meeɗinay mo Lepte mawɗe
25|20|Men Nulaali ado maaɗa immorde e Nulaaɓe si wanaa kamɓe hiɓe nafoo ñaametee hiɓe seenoo kadi ka luumaaji, Men waɗi yoga e mooɗon fitina yoga, fii yo on muñño. Joomi maaɗa laatike ko O Yi'oowo
25|21|Ɓen ɓe jortaaki hawroyde e Amen wi'i: "Ko hannoo jippinee e makko Malaa'ikaaɓe ɓen, maaɗum men yi'a Joomi amen?" Gomɗii ɓee mawnintinike ka wonkiiji maɓɓe, ɓe townitii townitaare mawnunde
25|22|Ñalnde ɓe yi'oyta Malaa'ikaaɓe ɓen weltaare alanaa bomɓe ɓen nden Ñalnde, ɓe wi'a: "Heedo heedaango
25|23|Men ardini faade e ko ɓe gollunoo kon immorde e gollal, Men waɗi ngal punndi caraandi
25|24|Yimɓe Aljanna ɓen nden Ñalnde ɓuri moƴƴude ñiiɓirde ɓuri labeede kadi ñallirde
25|25|E Ñalnde nde kummu ngun seekorta duule ɗen Malaa'ikaaɓe ɓen jippinee jippineede
25|26|Laamu GoongAawu ngun nden Ñalnde ko Hinnorante On ngu woodani, laatoo Ñalnde saɗtunde e dow yedduɓe ɓen
25|27|E Ñalnde tooñuɗo on ŋatoyta junngo makko ngon, o wi'a: "Eeh jalla min, mi jogitino wonndude e Nulaaɗo on Laawol
25|28|Eeh bone am haaniino min, mi jogitanooki kaariijo sehilaajo
25|29|Gomɗii o majjinii lam gaayi Deftere nden ɓaawo nde arii a am, Seytaane laatike ko o jaasinoowo neɗɗanke on
25|30|Nulaaɗo on maaka: "Ko ann yo Jooma pellet, yimɓe am ɓen ɓe jogitike ndee Alqur'aanaare wikkaande(accaande)
25|31|Ko wano nii, Men waɗirani kala Annabaajo gaño immorde e bonɓe ɓen, Joomi maaɗa yonii Fewnoowo e Ballo
25|32|Ɓen yedduɓe wi'i: "Ko hanno Alqur'aanaare nden jippinee e makko e jumla gooto?" Ɗum ko wano nii, fii yo Men tabintinir nde ɓernde maaɗa nden Men rewnindira nde rewnindirgol
25|33|Ɓe addantaa ma misal, si wanaa Men addanii ma Goonga kan e ko ɓuri moƴƴude firo
25|34|Ɓen mooɓoyteeɓe e dow geece muuɗum faade ka Jahannama, ko ɓen ɗon woni ɓuruɓe bonde nokkuure e ɓuruɓe majjude kade laawol
25|35|Gomɗii Men okkii Muusaa Deftere nden, Men waɗi wonndude e makko Musiɗɗo makko on Haaruuna ballo
25|36|Men Daali: "Yahee ka ɓen yimɓe fennuɓe Aayeeje Amen ɗen, Men yirbini ɓe yirbinndee
25|37|E yimɓe Nuuhu tuma nde ɓe fennunoo Nulaaɓe ɓen, Men yooli ɓe Men waɗi ɓe maande fii yimɓe ɓen, Men heblani tooñooɓe ɓen Lepte muusuɗe
25|38|E Aadinkooɓe ɓen e Samuudinkooɓe ɓen e yimɓe ɓunndu ndun e gire ɗuuɗuɗe hakkunde ɗum
25|39|Gooto kala e maɓe Men piyani ɗum mise, gooto kala e maɓɓe men halki ɗum halkugol
25|40|Gomɗii ɓe arii e nden saare toɓaande toɓo bonngo. Kaa ɓe laataaki hiɓe yi'a ɗe? Ko woni, ɓe laatinoke ɓe jortaaki Immotal
25|41|Si ɓe yi'ii ma, ɓe jogitotaako ma si wanaa jalnori. Enee, ko oo Alla Immini Nulaaɗo
25|42|Fii kala hari o ɓadike(ɗesi) majjinnde en gaayi reweteeɗi me'en ɗin si tawiino wanaa ko muññi ɗen kon e dow majji. Aray ɓe anndoyat tuma ɓe yi'ata Lepte ɗen ko hommbo ɓurɗo majjude laawol
25|43|Enee, a tinii on jogitiiɗo reweteeɗo makko on beleeɗe makko ɗen. E hara ko an laatotoo e dow makko fawtiiɗo
25|44|Kaa a sikku wonnde ko ɓuri heewude e maɓɓe hiɓe nana maaɗum hiɓe hakkila? Anndu kamɓe ɓe wonaali si wanaa wano neemoraaɗi, toode, ko kamɓe ɓuri majjude laawol
25|45|Kaa a tinaali faade e Joomi maaɗa honno O fontiri ɗowdi ndin? Sinndo O Muuyuno O waɗayno ndi deeƴundi, refti Men waɗi naange ngen tinndinaynge e mayri
25|46|Refti Men tami ndi ka Amen tamannde newiinde

25|48|Ko Kanko woni On accituɗo keni ɗin ko ɗi weltinooji hakkunde Yurmeende Makko nden, Men jippini immorde ka kammu ndiyam laaɓuɗam
25|49|Fii yo Men wurnitir ɗam leydi maayundi, Men yarnaɗam kadi kon ko Men tagi neemoraaɗi e yimɓe ɗuuɗuɓe
25|50|Gomɗii Men fensitii nde hakkunde maɓɓe fii yo ɓe waajito, salii ɓurɓe ɗuuɗude e yimɓe ɓen si wanaa yeddugol
25|51|Sinndo Men Muuyuno Men Nulayno e kala saare jertinoowo

25|54|Ko Kanko woni on Taguɗo ɓanndunke immorde e ndiyam ɗam, O waɗi mo dammbe e esiraawo, Joomi maaɗa laatike ko O Hattanɗo
25|55|Hiɓe rewa gaanin Alla kon ko nafataa ɓe lorrataa ɓe, yedduɗo on laatike ko o teeɗiiɗo Joomi makko

25|60|Si wi'anaama ɓe: "Sujjanee Hinnorante On" Ɓe wi"a: "Ko hommbo woni Hinnorante On? Enee, hara men sujjanay kon ko yamirɗaa men?" Ɗum ɓeydi ɓe foɗɗitaare

25|64|E ɓen waalooɓe sujjannde Joomi maɓɓe e daragol [juula]

27|1|Taa Siin, ɗen ko Aayeeje Alqur'aanaare nden e Deftere ɓanngunde

27|17|Sulaymaana mooɓanaa koneeli makko ɗin immorde ka jinnaaji e ka yimɓe e ka colli, kamɓe ko ɓe yuɓɓinaaɓe

27|60|Kaa ko hommbo tagi kammuuli ɗin e leydi ndin O jippinani on immorde ka kammu ndiyam? Men fuɗiniri ɗam gese joomiraaje ŋari. Wonantaa on nde fuɗinon leɗɗe majje. Enee, hara reweteeɗo no woodi wonndude e Alla? Ko woni, kamɓe ko ɓe yimɓe ooñotooɓe
27|61|Kaa ko hommbo waɗi leydi ndin ñiiɓundi, O waɗi hakkunde mayri calluɗi O waɗani ndi pelle O waɗi hakkunde maaje ɗen ɗiɗi heedo? Enee, hara na woodi reweteeɗo [goo] wonndude e Alla? ko woni, ɓurɓe ɗuuɗude ɓen e maɓɓe ɓe anndaa

27|63|Kaa ko hommbo fewnata on ka niɓe njoorndi e ka maayo, e ko hommbo accitata keni ɗin wewlinirayɗi fii Yurmeende Makko nden? Enee, ko reweteeɗo goo wonndude e Alla? Alla Toowii gaayi ko ɓe sirkata kon. @Corrected
27|64|Kaa ko hommbo woni fuɗɗuɗo tagu ngun refti O rutta ngu, e ko hommbo arsikata on immorde ka kammu e ka leydi? Enee, ko reweteeɗo goo wonndude e Alla? Maaku: "Addee daliili mooɗon on si tawii ko on goonguɓe

27|66|Ko woni, ganndal maɓɓe ngal hattii fii Laakara on, ko woni, kamɓe hiɓe e sikke fii [Laakara], ko woni, kamɓe ko ɓe wumuɓe fii ɗum

27|71|Hiɓe wi'a: "Ko honnde tuma woni ndee Fodoore, si on laatike goonguɓe
27|72|Maaku: "No tijjaa nde tawata ɓadanike on yoga e kon ko ɗaɓɓuɗon yaccinaneede
27|73|Pellet, Joomi maaɗa ko O Jom Ɓural e dow yimɓe ɓen, kono ɓurɓe ɗuuɗude ɓen e maɓɓe ɓe jarnataa [Alla]
27|74|Pellet, Joomi maaɗa hiMo Anndi ko ɓerɗe maɓɓe ɗen soomi e ko ɗe feññinta kon
27|75|Alaa e wirniikun ka kammu e ka leydi si wanaa [fii makkun] no e nder Deftere ɓanngunde
27|76|Pellet ndee Alqur'aanaare, hinde filloo e dow ɓiɗɓe Israa'iila ɓen fii huunde nde ɓe ɓuri luutondirde nden e fii muuɗum
27|77|Pellet, kayre ko nde peewal e Yurmeende wonannde gomɗinɓe ɓen
27|78|Pellet, Joomi maaɗa O ñaawiray hakkunde maɓɓe Ñaawoore Makko ngal, ko Kanko woni Tedduɗo Annduɗo
27|79|Wakkilo e Alla, pellet, an hiɗa e hoore Goonga ɓannguka kan
27|80|Pellet, an a nanintaa mayɓe ɓen, a nanintaa faaɗuɓe ɓen noddaandu ndun si ɓe ɗuurnike ɓe huccitii
27|81|An a wonaali fewnoowo bumɓe ɓen e gaayi majjere maɓɓe nden. A nanintaa si wanaa ɓen gomɗinɓe Aayeeje Amen ɗen hara kamɓe ko ɓe jebbiliiɓe
27|82|Si konngol ngol yanii e dow maɓɓe, Men yaltinana ɓe daabewa immorde ka leydi himba haalana ɓe wonnde yimɓe ɓen laatike ɓe yananaaka Aayeeje Amen ɗen
27|83|E ñalnde Men mooɓoyta immorde e kala mofte dental jeyaaɓe e ɓen fennooɓe Aayeeje Amen ɗen hara kamɓe hiɓe soggee
27|84|Haa si ɓe arii, O Daala: "Eyoo, on fenniino Aayeeje Am ɗen, hara on huɓindoraali ɗi ganndal. Kaa ko honɗum wonɗon e gollude
27|85|Konngol [Lepte] ngol yani e maɓɓe sabu ko ɓe tooñi kon, kamɓe ɓe wowlataa
27|86|Enee, hara ɓe yi'aali, Menen Men waɗii jemma on fii yo ɓe deeƴu e maako, e ñalorma on yi'irɗo? Pellet, wonii e ɗum Aayeeje wonannde yimɓe gomɗinooɓe ɓen
27|87|E Ñalnde wuttoytee ka alaadu, ɗenƴoo ɓen wonuɓe ka kammuuli e ɓen wonuɓe ka leydi, si wanaa ɓen ɓe Alla muuyi, gooto kala e maɓɓe aray e Makko hara ko ɓe hoykiniiɓe
27|88|Hiɗa tina pelle ɗen, sikka ko ɗe fenndiiɗe, hara le kannje hiɗe wuloo wulagol duule ɗen, ɗum ko kuugal Alla, On ŋarɗinɗo kala huunde, pellet, Kanko ko O Humpitiiɗo ko golloton kon
27|89|Mo ardii e moƴƴere nden haray no woodani mo ko ɓuri nde moƴƴude, hara kamɓe ko ɓe hooliiɓe immorde e ɗenƴere nden Ñalnde
27|90|Mo ardii kadi e bone ɗen, geece maɓɓe ɗen hippete ka Yiite. Yalli on yoɓete si wanaa kon ko laatinoɗon hiɗon golla
27|91|Anndu ko mi yamiraa ko yo mi Rewu Jooma ndii leydi ndi Alla harmini ɗum, no woodani Mo kala huunde. Mi yamiraama kadi yo mi laato jeyaaɗo e jebbiliiɓe ɓen
27|92|E yo mi janngu Alqur'aanaare nden, mo feewii haray ko hoore-makko o feewani, mo majjii kadi haray maaku: "Min dey, ko mi jeyaaɗo e jertinooɓe ɓen
27|93|Maaku kadi: "Yettoore nden woodanii Alla, aray O holla on Aayeeje Makko ɗen anndon ɗe". Joomi maaɗa wonaali welsindiiɗo gaay e kon ko golloton
28|1|Taa, Siin, Miim
28|2|Ɗee ko Aayeeje Deftere ɓanngunde nden
28|3|Meɗen janngira e maaɗa hoore goonga, kumpital Muusaa e Fir'awna, wonannde yimɓe gomɗinooɓe ɓen
28|4|Pellet, Fir'awna townitino ka leydi; o waɗi yimɓe mayri ndin pecce-pecce: himo lo'ina fedde goo e maɓɓe, o hirsa ɓiɗɓe maɓɓe worɓe ɓen o acca rewɓe maɓɓe ɓen. Pellet, ko e bonnooɓe ɓen o jeyanoo
28|5|Meɗen faandinoo moƴƴagol e lo'inanooɓe ɓen ka leydi; Men waɗa ɓe koohooɓe, Men waɗa ɓe kadi ronooɓe ɓen
28|6|Men huɓindina ɓe e leydi ndin, Men holla Fir'awna e Haamaana e koneeli maɓɓe ɗin, kon ko ɓe hulaynoo
28|7|Men wahayini e yumma Muusaa, wonnde: "Muynin mo". Si a hulanoyii mo, ko yo a bugoyo mo ka maayo. Wata a hulu, wata a suno; pellet, Men ruttay mo ka maaɗa, Men waɗoya mo gooto e Nulaaɓe ɓen
28|8|Yimɓe Fir'awna ɓen hocci mo, fii yo laatano ɓe gaño e suno. Pellet, Fir'awna e Haamaana e koneeli maɓɓe ɗin, ɓe laatino woopuɓe
28|9|Debbo Fir'awna on wi'i: "(Kun entum ko) ɓuuɓeendi gite am e an kadi! Wata on waru mo, hino gasa ka o nafata en, maa jogitoren mo ɓiɗɗo". Hari ɓe so'aani
28|10|Ɓernde yumma Muusaa nden wonti yeewunde. Haa o eɓɓi feññinde fii makko, si wanaano Men tabintinnde ɓernde makko nden, fii yo o laato e gomɗinɓe ɓen
28|11|[Yumma Muusaa] wi'ani banndiraawo makko on: "Jokkitu mo"; o haynii mo ka deestii, hari ɓe so'aa-anndude
28|12|Men harminani mo ko adii, (enɗi) muynirɗi ɗin, (banndiraawo makko on) wi'i: "On accay mi tinndinay on fii yimɓe suudu, ɓe ne'ana on mo, hara kadi ko laaɓanay ɓe mo
28|13|Men rutti mo ka yumma makko, fii yo ɓernde makko ɓuuɓu, hara o sunaaki, e fii yo o anndu pellet, fodoore Alla nden, ko goonga. Kono ɓurɓe ɗuuɗude e maɓɓe anndaa
28|14|Nde o yottinoo sagatalaaku makko ngun, o fotondi- ri, Men okki mo faamu e ganndal. Ko wano non Men yoɓirta moƴƴinooɓe ɓen
28|15|O naatiri e saare nden, fewndo welsindaare yimɓe mayre; o tawi worɓe ɗiɗo no haɓa ton: goɗɗo on ko jeyaaɗo e leñol makko, oya on ko jeyaaɗo e ayɓe makko ɓen. Jeyaaɗo e leñol makko ngol ɗaɓɓiri faabo e hoore jeyaaɗo e gaño makko on. Muusaa uttii mo, nde gayni fii makko. [Muusaa] maaki: "Ɗum ɗoo, ko jeyaaɗum e kuuɗe seytaane. Pellet, ko o gaño, majjinoowo ɓannguɗo
28|16|O maaki: "Joomi am, mi tooñii hoore-am; haforanam." O haforani mo. Pellet, ko Kanko woni Haforoowo, Hinnotooɗo On
28|17|O maaki: "Joomi am, sabu ko neeminɗaa kon e am, mi wontataa ballo bomɓe ɓen
28|18|O wonti hulɗo ka saare, himo habbii [nanngeede]. Tawi faabinornooɗo mo on hanki, hino faabinora mo [hannde kadi]. Muusaa maakani mo: "Pellet, ko a bewɗo ɓannguɗo
28|19|Nde Muusaa faandinoo nanngugol tawɗo on ko gaño maɓɓe kamɓe ɗiɗo, o wi'i: "Ko an yo Muusaa, a faala warugol lam, wano ittirnoɗaa wonkii non hanki? A faandaaki, si wanaa wonugol dunndarankeejo ka leydi, a faandaaki jeyeede e moƴƴinooɓe ɓen
28|20|Gorko iwri ka ɓuri woɗɗude e saare nden, himo yaccoo, o wi'i: "Ko an yo Muusaa, mbatu ngun no fewjana fii warugol maa. Yaltu (e leydi ndin). Ko mi jeyaaɗo e laaɓanooɓe ma
28|21|O yalti ton, ko o huluɗo, himo tijjii [nanngeede]. O maaki: "Joomi am, danɗndam e yimɓe tooñooɓe ɓen
28|22|Nde o fewtunoo hella Madyana, o maaki: "Hino hasii ka Joomi am fewnirta lam, e laawol focciingol ngol
28|23|Nde o hewtunoo ka ɓunndu Madyana, o tawi ɗon dental yimɓe, hiɓe yarna [daabeeji maɓɓe], o tawi gaanin maɓɓe, rewɓe ɗiɗo, no sogga [dammi maɓɓe], o maaki: "Ko honɗum habbi-ɗon?" Ɓe wi'i: "Men yarnataa haa aynooɓe ɓen deestoo, baaba amen, ko mawɗo nayeejo
28|24|O yarnani ɓe [dammi ɗin], refti o huccitiri ka ɗowdi, o maaki: "Joomi am, min ko jippinɗaa e am woo e moƴƴere, ko mi hatonjiɗo
28|25|Gooto e [jiwɓe] ɓen ari e makko, himo yahra hersa, o wi'i: "Baaba am no nodde, fii yo o yoɓe njoɓdi kon ko yarnan-ɗaa men". Tuma o hewtunoo ka [mawɗo] on, o sifanii mo fii [makko], o maaki: "Wata a hulu, a daɗii yimɓe tooñooɓe ɓen
28|26|Gooto e [jiwɓe] ɓen wi'i: "Ƴettu mo golle, yo baaba. Pellet, ko ɓuri moƴƴude e mo ƴettataa golle, ko doolnuɗo hoolniiɗo
28|27|[Mawɗo] on maaki: "Miɗo yiɗi resingol ma gooto e jiwɓe am ɓen ɗoo ɗiɗo, e hoore yo a golla-nam duuɓi jeetati. Si a timminii sappo, haray ko e sago maa; mi faalaaka saɗtinannde ma. A taway lam, si Alla jaɓii, ko e moƴƴinooɓe ɓen mi jeyaa
28|28|[Muusaa] maaki: "Ɗum wonii hakkunde am e mon. Happu woo e majji ɗiɗi, ɗi mi hunni, haray ɓiɗteede alanaa e lam. En waɗii Alla fawtiiɗo e ko wowluɗen kon
28|29|Nde Muusaa timminnoo happu ngun, o yahdi e ɓeydnuure makko, o haynii yiite ka senngo (fello) Tuuri, o maaki ɓeunguure makko nden: "Wonee ɗoo, min mi haynike yiite. Belajo'o mi addana on e magge kumpital maa te'annde(docotal) yiite ngen, belajo'o iwloron
28|30|Nde o hewtunoo nge, o noddiraa ka fonngo ñaamo aynde, ka tummbere barkinaande, ka (takko) lekki, wonnde: "Ko an yo Muusaa! Ko Min woni Alla, Jeyɗo winndere nden
28|31|Kadi: "Bugo tuggordu maa ndun"; nde o tinunoo hindu dillira wa mboddi,o huccitiri dogudu, o yeƴƴitaaki. [O noddaa]: "Ko an yo Muusaa! Artu, wata a hulu; ko a jeyaaɗo e hooliiɓe ɓen
28|32|Naadu juungo maa ngon ka jayba maa, ngo yaltay ranewo, ko aldaa e ñawu. Bakaa e maaɗa, juuɗe maa ɗen, fii kulol ngol. Ɗin ko hujjaaji ɗiɗi, immorde ka Joomi maa, haa e Fir'awna e dental mun, pellet, ɓen laatike yimɓe faasiqiiɓe
28|33|O maaki: "Joomi am, mi ittiino wonkii e maɓɓe, miɗo huli nde ɓe warata lam
28|34|Ko musiɗɗo am on Haaruuna, ɓuri lam laaɓude ɗemngal. Immindin-mo e am, ko wallitoo lam, goonginan-mi; miɗo huli nde ɓe fennata lam
28|35|[Alla] daali: "Men semmbiniray tere maa ɗen, musiɗɗo maa on, Men waɗana on hujja (e cemmbe); ɓe hewtirtaa on ɗiɗo, sabu Aayeeje Amen ɗe [Men nuli e] mo'on, e ɓen jokkuɓe on fooluɓe
28|36|Nde Muusaa ardunoo e maɓɓe Aayeeje Amen ɗen ɓannguɗe, ɓe wi'i: "Ɗum wonaali, si wanaa mbilewu fefindaangu. Men naniraali ɗum baabiraaɓe amen adinooɓe ɓen
28|37|Muusaa maaki: "Ko Joomi am ɓuri anndude on arduɗo e peewal, immorde ka Makko, e on mo battane moƴƴe woodani ka laakara. Pellet, O malnataa tooñooɓe ɓen
28|38|Fir'awna wi'i: "Ko onon dental, mi anndanaa on reweteeɗo, si wanaa min. Ko an yo Haamaana, huɓɓinanam [yiite] e loopal ngal, mahiranaa lam huɓeere toowunde, no gasa ka mi ƴellitoo e Reweteeɗo Muusaa On; tawde miɗo sikki mo e fenooɓe ɓen
28|39|O townitii ka leydi, kanko e koneeli makko ɗin, ko aldaa e goonga. Ɓe sikki wonde ɓe ruttitetaako ka Amen
28|40|Men nanngi mo, kanko e koneeli makko ɗin, Men bugii ɓe ka maayo. Tasko, ko honno battane tooñuɓe ɓen wa'unoo
28|41|Men waɗi ɓe ardiiɓe, noddoo ɓe e Yiite. Ñalnde Darngal, ɓe walletaake
28|42|Men jokkintiniri ɓe ka aduna ɗoo, kuddi. Ñalnde Darngal, ko ɓe jeyaaɓe e woɗɗintinoyteeɓe [e yurmeende Alla]
28|43|Gomɗii Men okkii Muusaa Deftere nden, ɓaawo nde Men halkunoo gire arane ɗen, ko nde ndayginorde yimɓe ɓen, e peewal e yurmeende. Belajo'o, ɓe waajitoray
28|44|A tawanooka ka senngo hiirnaange, fewndo Men wahyinnoo e Muusaa yamiroore nden, a jeyanooka kadi e seediiɓe ɓen
28|45|Kono Menen woni taguɓe gire, duuɓi maɓɓe juuti. A hoɗaano kadi e yimɓe Madyana ɓen, hiɗa janngana ɓe Aayeeje Amen; ko Menen woni nulɓe
28|46|A tawanooka ka senngo Fello Tuuri, fewndo Men noddunoo; ko yurmeende immorde ka Joomi maa [woni ko Men nulir-maa], fii no jertiniraa yimɓe, ɓe reentinoowo araali e maɓɓe, ado maaɗa, belajo'o, ɓe waajitoto
28|47|Si wanaano fii yo lepte yanir e maɓɓe, sabu ko juuɗe maɓɓe ardini, ɓe wi'ayno: "Joomi amen, ko haɗno imminaa Nulaaɗo e amen? Men jokka nun Aayeeje Maa ɗen, men jeyee e gomɗimɓe ɓen
28|48|Nde o addirannooɓe goonga kan, immorde ka Amen, ɓe wi'i: "Ko haɗno o okkee yeru ko Muusaa okkanoo kon?" Kere ɓe yeddaano ko Muusaa okkanoo kon ko adii? Ɓe wi'i: "Ko mbileeji ɗiɗi, ɗi no wallindira!" Ɓe wi'i kadi: "Ko men yedduɓe fow e mun
28|49|Maaku: "Addee Deftere immorde ka Alla, hara hinde ɓuri ɗee ɗiɗi feewude, mi jokkaynde, si on laatike goongunɓe
28|50|Si ɓe jaabaaki ma, anndu ko mbeleeɗe maɓɓe ɓe jokkata. Ko hommbo ɓuri majjude ɓuri on jokkirɗo mbeleeɗe mun, ko aldaa e peewal immorde ka Alla? Pellet, Alla fewnataa yimɓe tooñooɓe ɓen
28|51|Gomɗii Men hewtinii ɓe Konngol ngol, belajo'o, ɓe waajitora
