28|53|Si nde janngaama e dow maɓɓe, ɓe wi'a: "Men gomɗinii nde. Ko nde goonga immorde ka Joomi amen. Pellet men woniino jebbiliiɓe, ado mayre
28|54|Ɓen ɗon, ɓe jonniroyte njoɓdi maɓɓe ndin, laabi ɗiɗi, sabu ko ɓe muñinoo kon, hiɓe duñiraynoo moƴƴere nden, bone on, e huunde nde Men arsiki ɓe nden, hiɓe nafqa
28|55|Si ɓe nanii meerente, ɓe ɗuurnoo e ɗum, ɓe wi'a: "Ko menen golle amen woodani, ko onon kadi golle mon woodani. Kisal wonii e mo'on. Men ɗaɓɓataa wonndugol e majjuɓe ɓen
28|56|Pellet, an (Nulaaɗo), a fewnataa mo yiɗuɗaa; kono Alla no fewna on Mo O muuyi. Ko Kanko ɓuri anndude feewuɓe ɓen
28|57|Ɓe wi'i: "Si men jokkidii peewal ngal e maa, men biftete ka leydi amen". E Men hoɗiniraali ɓe e nokku horminaaɗo, hoolniiɗo, mo dimɗe noone kaka addetee e mun, arsike immorde ka Amen? Si ko woni, ko ɓuri ɗuuɗude e maɓɓe, ɓe anndaa
28|58|Ɗuuɗii ko Men hakli, e yimɓe ca'e, bewrunooɓe nguuree mun, e hino non galleeji maɓɓe ɗin, hoɗiraaka ɓaawo maɓɓe, si wanaa seeɗa. Men laatii wonnde ronooɓe ɓen
28|59|Joomi maa siforaali wonde halkoowo yimɓe ca'e, haa O immina e lenyol maɓɓeɗen, Nulaaɗo, ko janngana ɓe Aayeeje Amen ɗen. Men siforaali kadi halkugol yimɓe ca'e, si wanaa hara yimɓe majje ko tooñuɓe
28|60|Kala ko okkaɗon e huunde, ko dakamme nguurndam aduna e cuɗaari mun; ko ko woni ka Alla kon, ɓuri moƴƴude, woni kadi ko luttata. E on haqqiltaa
28|61|E ko on mo Men fodi fodaari moƴƴuri, ndi o hawrata e mu'un, wa'ata wa on mo Men dakmitiri dakamme nguurndam aduna, refti hara kanko on, Ñalnde Darngal, ko e tawneteeɓe (ka Yiite) ɓen o jeyaa
28|62|Ñalnde O noddoyta ɓe, O wi'a: "Ko honto kafidaaɗi am, ɗin ɗi aaƴoraynoɗon woni
28|63|Ɓen ɓe Konngol jojji e mu'un wi'a: "Joomi amen, ko ɓee woni ko men bewinnoo. Men bewinirno ɓe, wano men bewirnoo. Men daɗndinike e Maaɗa. Wanaa menen ɓe rewaynoo
28|64|[Ɓe] wi'anee: "Noddee non kafidaaɗi mon ɗin". Ɓe nodda ɗi, kono ɗi jaabotaako ɓe. Ɓe yi'a lepte ɗen, (ɓe yeloo) sinno hara ɓe feewuno
28|65|Ñalnde O noddoyta ɓe, o wi'a: "Ko honɗum jaabinoɗon Nulaaɓe ɓen
28|66|Lamitorɗi ɗin wumiɗana ɓe nden ñalnde, ɓe lamndondirtaa
28|67|Si ko tuubuɗo, o gomɗini, o golli moƴƴuɗi, hino hasii ka o jeyee e malaaɓe ɓen
28|68|Joomi maa no taga ko O muuyi, O suɓoo; suɓagol alanaa ɓe. Senaade woodanii Alla! O toowii e kon ko ɓe sirkata
28|69|Joomi maa no anndi ko ɓerɗe maɓɓe ɗen suuɗata, e kon ko ɓe feññinta
28|70|Ko Kanko Alla woni, Mo reweteeɗo alaa, si wanaa Kanko. Ko Kanko yettoore woodani aduna e laakara. Hino woodani Mo ñaawoore nden. Ko ka Makko rutteteɗon
28|71|Maaku: "Yeetee lam, Si Alla waɗiranii on jemma on, duumiiɗo haa Ñalnde Darngal, ko reweteeɗo hommbo, tanaa Alla, addanta on ndayngu? E on nanataa
28|72|Maaku: "Yeetee lam, Si Alla waɗiranii on ñalorma on, duumiiɗo haa Ñalnde Darngal, ko reweteeɗo hommbo, tanaa Alla, addanta on jemma, mo deeƴoton e mun? E on yi'ataa
28|73|Hino jeyaa e yurmeende Makko, O waɗiranii on jemma e ñalorma; fii no deeƴiron e (jemma) on, e no ɗaɓɓiron ( e ñalorma on), ɓural Makko, e no belajo'o yettiron [Mo]
28|74|Ñalnde O noddoyta ɓe, O wi'a: "Ko honto kadidaaɗi(renndidiiɗi) am, ɗin ɗin aaƴoraynoɗon woni
28|75|Men ɗoofi e kala mofte, seedotooɗo, Men wi'a: "Addee hujjaajji mon ɗin". Ɓe anndi wonnde goonga kan, ko Alla woodani; ko ɓe fefindotonoo kon majjitora ɓe
28|76|Pellet,Qaaruuna ko e yimɓe Muusaa ɓen jeyanoo,kono o bewi e maɓɓe.Men okki mo ngaluuji taway-ɗi soktirɗe mun,no teddana jamaa doolnuɗo.Nde yimɓe makko ɓen,wi'anno mo:Wata a weltor townitaare.Pellet Alla yiɗaa weltortooɓe toownitaare
28|77|Ɗaɓɓir ko Alla okku-maa kon, galle laakare ɗen. Wata a yejjitu geɓal maa ngal aduna. Moƴƴir no Alla moƴƴorii non e maaɗa. Wata a ɗaɓɓu bonnugol ka leydi. Anndu pellet, Alla yiɗaa bonnooɓe ɓen
28|78|O wi'i: "Ko mi okkiraa ɗum, ko e hoore ganndal ngal mi jogii". E o anndaa wonnde gomɗii Alla halkiino gire, adiiɓe mo, ɓurɓe doole, ɓuri mo ɗuuɗude jawle? Ɓe lamndoytaake fii junuubi maɓɓe, kamɓe bomɓe ɓen
28|79|O yaltitiri e yimɓe makko ɓen, cuɗaari makko ndin. Yiɗuɓe nguurndam aduna ɓen wi'i: "Hara nun men heɓayno sugu koo ko Qaaruuna okkaa. Kanko on, pellet, ko o jom-geɓal mawnungal
28|80|Okkaaɓe ganndal ɓen kan wi'i: "Ee bone mon! Ko mbarjaari Alla ndin ɓuri moƴƴannde on gomɗinɗo o golli ko moƴƴi". Kono hawrataa e ɗum, si wanaa muññiiɓe ɓen
28|81|Men mutindini mo e galle makko ɗen, ka leydi. Fedde woo alanaa mo, ko faaboo mo gaanin Alla, o wonaano faabotooɗo hoore-mun
28|82|Ɓen yelinooɓe nokku makko on hanki mun, ɓe waɗti wiide: "Ee bone! Alla no wertana arsike on, Mo O muuyani e jeyaaɓe Makko ɓen, O ɓiɗtinana [Mo O muuyani]. Si wanaa Alla moƴƴinoo e amen, O mutinayno men. Ee bone! Jaka O malnataa yedduɓe ɓen
28|83|Ɗen galle laakara, Men waɗanii ɗe ɓen ɓe yiɗaa townitaare ka leydi, wanaa kadi bonnugol. Battane moƴƴe ɗen, ko fii gomɗuɓe ɓen
28|84|Kala arduɗo e moƴƴere, hino woodani mo ko ɓuri nde moƴƴude; kala kadi arduɗo e bonannde, (yo o anndu) huuwuɓe bonɗi ɗin yoɓetaake, si wanaa ko ɓe huuwaynoo kon
28|85|Pellet, jippinɗo Alqur'aana on e maaɗa, ko ruttoo-wo ma ka woowaandi maa. Maaku: "Ko Joomi am ɓuri anndude arduɗo e peewal, e wonɗo e majjere ɓanngunde
28|86|A wonaano tamƴininooɗo jippineede Deftere nden e maaɗa. Si wanaa tun, ko yurmeende immorde ka Joomi maa. Wata wonu muk, walloowo heeferɓe ɓen
28|87|wata ɓe falo ma kadi e Aayeeje Alla ɗen, ɓaawo ɗe jippineede e maaɗa. Noddu (yimɓe ɓen) faade e Joomi maa, wata a wonu muk, jeyaaɗo e sirkooɓe ɓen
28|88|Wata a rewudu e Alla, reweteeɗo goo. Reweteeɗo goo alaa, si wanaa Kanko. Huunde fow re'ay, si wanaa Jaati Maako Kin. Ko Kanko woodani ñaawugol; ko ka Makko kadi rutteteɗon. @Corrected
29|1|Alif, Laam, Miim
29|2|E yimɓe ɓen sikku ɓe accirte nii, fii ɓe wi'ii: "Men gomɗinii!" Hara ɓe fitninaaka
29|3|Gomɗii, Men fitninii ɓen adinooɓe ɓe. Maa Alla feññin, fii goonguɓe ɓen, maa O feññin kadi, fii fenooɓe ɓen
29|4|Kaa huuwuɓe bonɗi ɓen sikku, wonnde ɓe laawoto Men? ko ɓe ñaawata kon bonii
29|5|Kala tawɗo himo jortii hawroygol e Alla, ko pellet, lajal Alla ngal, ko hewtaygal. Ko Kanko woni Nanoowo, Annduɗo On
29|6|Kala kadi tiiɗniiɗo, ko hoore-makko o tiiɗnanii, tawde pellet, Alla ko yonndiniiɗo e tageefo ngon
29|7|Ɓen non gomɗimɓe, ɓe golli golle moƴƴe, ma Men momtan ɓe bonɗi maɓɓe ɗin, Men yoɓitra ɓe, ko ɓuri moƴƴude e ko ɓe gollaynoo kon
29|8|Men yamirii neɗɗanke on, moƴƴugol e mawɓe makko ɓen. Si ɓe doolii maa fii sirkangol Lam, ko a alanaa ɗum ganndal, wata a ɗofto ɓe ! Ko ka Am, woni ruttorde mon, Mi habra on, ko gollaynoɗon
29|9|Ɓen gomɗimɓe Alla, ɓe golli golle moƴƴe, ma Men waɗtiduɓe e moƴƴuɓe ɓen
29|10|Hino e jimɓe ɓen, wi'oowo: "Men gomɗinii Alla"; hara non si o tampiniraama fii Alla, o waɗay lorra yimɓe ɓen, wano lepte Alla ɗen. Si ballal kadi immorii ka Joomi maa, pellet, ɓe wi'ay: "Meɗen wondunoo e mo'on!" Kere wanaa Alla ɓuri anndude ko woni e ɓerɗe tageefo ngon
29|11|Ma Alla anndin fii gomɗimɓe ɓen, ma O feññina kadi fii naafiqiiɓe ɓen
29|12|Heeferɓe ɓen wi'ani gomɗimɓe ɓen: "Jokkee laawol amen ngol, men fawtoto fii goopi mon ɗin". Kono ɓe wonaali fawtotooɓe hay huunde e goopi maɓɓe. Pellet, ko ɓe fenooɓe
29|13|Kono maa ɓe fawtoo fii teddeendi junuubi maɓɓe ɗin, e teddeendi goo, wonndude e teddeendi maɓɓe ndin. Ko maa ɓe lamndoyee, Ñalnde Darngal, gaay e kon ko ɓe fefindotonoo
29|14|Gomɗii Men nulii Nuuhu e yimɓe makko ɓen, o ñiiɓi hakkunde maɓɓe, duuɓi ujunere, ŋakkuɗum duuɓi cappanɗe jowi. Waame on nanngi ɓe, hari ko ɓe tooñuɓe
29|15|Men daɗndi mo, kanko e yimɓe laana kan; Men waɗi ka kaawisa tageefo ngon
29|16|(Janto) kadi Ibraahiima, nde o wi'annoo yimɓe makko ɓen: "Rewee Alla, hulon Mo; ko ɗum ɓuri moƴƴannde on, si woni hiɗon anndi
29|17|Anndee ko reweton kon gaanin Alla, ko sanamuuji, hiɗon taƴa fenaande. Pellet, ɗin ɗi rewoton gaanin Alla, ɗi waawaa on arsikude; ɗaɓɓiree arsike on ka Alla, rewon Mo, yetton Mo. Ko ka Makko woni rutteteɗon
29|18|Si on fennii, haray mofte adinooɓe kadi fenniino (Nulaaɓe mun). Alaa ko fawii e Nulaaɗo on, si wanaa yottingol ɓannginngol
29|19|E ɓee yi'aali no Alla fuɗɗorta tagu ngun, refti O ruttay ngu? Pellet, ɗum wonii ko newanii Alla
29|20|Maaku: "Yiilee ka leydi, ndaaron no O fuɗɗori tagu ngun. Refti Alla taga tagu sakkitoru ngun. Pellet, Alla ko hattanɗo kala huunde
29|21|Himo lepte mo O muuyani, O yurmo mo O muuyani; ko ka Makko rutteteɗon
29|22|On wonaali laawotooɓe ka leydi, wanaa ka kammu; alanaa on gaanin Alla, woni giɗo, wanaa ballo
29|23|Ɓen yedduɓe Aayeeje Alla ɗen, e hawroygol e Makko ngol, ɓen taƴike e yurmeende Am, ɓen ɗon, hino woodani ɓe lepte muusuɗe
29|24|Jaabawol yimɓe makko ɓen wonaano, si wanaa wiide ɓe: "Waree mo, maa sunnon mo". Kono Alla daɗndi mo e yiite ngen. Pellet, wonii e ɗum, maandeeji, wonannde yimɓe gomɗimɓe
29|25|O maaki: "Anndee ko rewoton kon gaanin Alla, ko sanamuuji, fii yiɗindiro hakkunde mon, ka nguurndam aduna, hooti non, Ñalnde Darndal, yoga mon yeddoyay yoga, yoga mon kadi huɗo yoga, hara non, jaaƴorde mon nden, ko ka Yiite, hara wallooɓe alanaa on
29|26|Luutu gomɗini mo. O maaki: "Min on, ko mi feroowo ka Joomi am, ko Kanko woni Fooluɗo, Ñeeño On
29|27|Men yeɗi mo Ismaa'iila e Yaaquuba, Men waɗi e geyngol makko ngol, Annabaaku e Daftere. Men okki mo mbarjaari makko ndin aduna, pellet, kanko on ka laakara, ko o jeyaaɗo e moƴƴuɓe ɓen
29|28|(Janto) kadi luutu, nde o maakannoo yimɓe makko ɓen : " E on aray e pankare, ɗe gooto e winndere nden adaaki on e mun
29|29|E on aray yottagol e worɓe ɓen? paloɗon kadi e laawol? Huuwon ko mbatirdu mon ko añinii?" Kono jaabawol yimɓe makko ɓen wonaano, si wanaa wiide ɓe: "Addan men lepte Alla ɗen, si tawii ko a jeyaaɗo e goonguɓe ɓen
29|30|O maaki: "Joomi am, wallam e hoore yimɓe bonnooɓe ɓen
29|31|Tuma nde Imminaaɓe Amen ɓen addannoo Ibraahiima welo-welo ngon, ɓe wi"i: "Menen, ko men halkooɓee yimɓe ndee saare. Tawde pellet, yimɓe mayre laatike tooñooɓe
29|32|O maaki: "Kono Luutu no ton!" Ɓe wi'i: "Ko menen ɓuri anndude fii wonɓe ton. Ko ma men daɗndu mo, kanko e yimɓe makko ɓen, si wanaa debbo makko on, o jeyaama e helketeeɓe ɓen
29|33|Tum nde imminaaɓe Amen ɓen hewtunoo ka Luutu, o saɗtiraa fii maɓɓe, ɓernde makko ɓiɗtorii fii maɓɓe. Ɓe wi'i: "Wata a hulu, wata a suno. Ko men daɗndooɓe ma an e ɓeynguure maa nden, si wanaa debbo maa on, o jeyaama e halkaaɓe ɓen
29|34|Ko men jippinooɓe lepte e yimɓe ndee saare, immorde ka kammu, sabu ko ɓe yaltunoo e ɗoftaare kon
29|35|Gomɗii Men accii e nden (saare), maande ɓanngunde, wonannde yimɓe haqqilooɓe ɓen
29|36|(Men nuli) kadi e Madyana, musiɗɗo maɓɓe on, Shu'aybu. O maaki: "Ko onon yo yimɓe am, rewee Alla, jortoron Ñalannde sakkitiinde nden, wata woniri e leydi ndin, bonnooɓe
29|37|Kono ɓe fenni mo. Dillannde nden nanngi ɓe, ɓe waɗtini ka koɗooli maɓɓe, ko ɓe jicciiɓe-maayi
29|38|(Men halki) kadi Aadi'en, e Saamuda'en. Gomɗii caambbeje maɓɓe ɗin ɓannganii on. Seytaane cuɗinani ɓe, golle maɓɓe ɗen, ndu sakkii ɓe e laawol ngol; tawi le, ko ɓe rentunooɓe
29|39|(Men halki) kadi Qaaruuna, e Fir'awna e Haamaana. Gomɗii le, Muusaa addanii ɓe ɓanngannduyeeji, kono ɓe townitii ka leydi, ɓe wonaano laawotooɓe
29|40|Kala maɓɓe, Men leptirno junuubi mun ɗin: no e maɓɓe, ɓe Men wuurti henndu e mun; no e maɓɓe, ɓe haacaango halki; no e maɓɓe, mo Men mutini ɗum ka leydi, no e maɓɓe kadi, ɓe Men yoolunoo. Kono non, Alla siforaali tooñoowo ɓe; si ko woni, ko kamɓe tooñunoo ko'e maɓɓe
29|41|Misal ɓen jogitiiɓe gaanin Alla reweteeɗi, ko wano marijaawowal(njomblo) saccungal suudu. Ko ɓuri lo'ude non e cuuɗi ɗin, ko suudu marijaawo. Sinno ɓe annduno
29|42|Pellet, Alla no anndi kala huunde nde ɓe noddata gaanin Makko. Ko Kanko woni Fooluɗo, Ñeeño On
29|43|Ɗee ko mise ɗe Men piyanta yimɓe ɓen; ko woni tun, faamataa ɗen, si wanaa annduɓe ɓen
29|44|Alla tagirii kammuuli ɗin e leydi ndin, e hoore goonga. Pellet, wonii ɗum, maande, wonannde gomɗimɓe ɓen
29|45|Janngu kon ko waayinaa e maaɗa ka Deftere, ñiiɓaa e julde nden. Pellet, juulde nden no haɗa pankare e ko añinii. Ko jantagol Alla ngol ɓuri (huunde kala) mawnude. Alla no anndi ko golloton kon
29|46|Wata on wennjir yimɓe Defte ɓen si wanaa e no ɓuri e moƴƴirde, si wanaa hara ko ɓen tooñuɓe e maɓɓe. Wi'on: "Men gomɗinii nden jippinaande e amen e ɗen jippinaaɗe e mon. Reweteeɗo amen On e reweteeɗo mon On ko gooto, menen non, ko Men jebbilanii ɓe Mo
29|47|Ko wano non Men jippiniri e maaɗa Deftere nden. Ɓen ɓe Men okki Deftere nden, hiɓe gomɗini nde. Hino e maɓɓe on gomɗinɗo nde. Yeddataa Aayeeje Amen ɗen, si wanaa heeferɓe ɓen
29|48|A wonaano hiɗa janngaynoo deftere ado mayre, a winndirtaano ñaamo maa ngon. Harayno, bonnooɓe ɓen sikkittono
29|49|Si ko woni, ko nde Aayeeje ɓannguɗe e ɓerɗe ɓen okkaaɓe ganndal. Yeddataa Aayeeje Amen ɗen, si wanaa tooñuɓe ɓen
29|50|Ɓe wi'i: "Hanno jippinee e makko maandeeji immorde ka Joomi makko?" Maaku: "Aayaaji ko joomam addata, anndee min, ko mi jertinoowo ɓannguɗo
29|51|Kere yonaali ɓe wonnde Men jippinii e maaɗa Deftere nden hinde janngee e maɓɓe? Wonii e ɗum, yurmeende e waaju wonannde yimɓe gomɗinooɓe
29|52|Maaku: "Alla yonii hakkunde am e mooɗon seedee Hino anndi ko woni kon ka kammuuli e ka leydi. Ɓen non gomɗimɓe meere nden ɓe yeddi Alla, ko ɓen woni sooyuɓe ɓen
29|53|Hiɓe hawjirane lepte ɗen. Si wanaano fii lajal innaangal, lepte ɗen ardirayno e maɓɓe juhal, hara kamɓe ɓe so'aa-anndude
29|54|Hiɓe hawjirane lepte ɗen, hara non pellet, Jahannama ko fiiltiinge heefereɓe ɓen
29|55|Ñalnde lepte ɗen suddiroyta ɓe senngo dow maɓɓe e ka ley koyɗe maɓɓe, O daala[na ɓe]: "Meeɗee ko gollaynoɗon kon
29|56|Ko onon yo jeyaaɓe Am gomɗimɓe! Anndee leydi Am ndin ko yaajundi. Ko Min woni ko rewoton
29|57|Kala wonkii meeɗay maayde. Refti ko ka Amen rutteteɗon
29|58|Ɓen gomɗimɓe ɓe golli golle moƴƴe, ma Men hoɗnu ɓe ka Aljanna e cuuɗi ɗi canɗi ilata senngo ley majji, koɓe duumotooɓe ton. Iskin(heskey)° moƴƴere njoɓdi gollunooɓe, @Corrected
29|59|ɓen muññiiɓe, ɓe tuugii e Joomi maɓɓe
29|60|Ɗuuɗii e ruugayɗi ɗi yooɓotaako arsike majji! Ko Alla arsikata ɗi wonndude e onon. Ko Kanko woni Nanoowo, Annduɗo
29|61|Pellet, si a lanndike ɓe: "Ko hommbo tagi kammuu- li ɗin e leydi ndin, O elti naange ngen e lewru ndu?" Ma ɓe wi'u: "Ko Alla". Ko honno ɓe ferlitoraa (e gomɗingol ngol)
29|62|Alla no yaajinana arsike on Mo O muuyi e jeyaaɓe Makko ɓen, Himo ɓittana mo. Pellet, Alla ko Annduɗo kala huunde
29|63|Pellet, si a lanndike ɓe: "Ko hommbo jippiniri ndiyam ka kammu ɗam O wuurnitiri leydi ndin ɓaawo ndi yoorude?", ma ɓe wi'u: "Ko Alla". Maaku: "Yettoore woodanii Alla!". Si ko woni, ko ɓuri ɗuuɗude e maɓɓe haqqiltaa
29|64|Ɗam nguurndam aduna wonaali, si wanaa mbeleeɗe e fijindaaru. Pellet, ko hoɗo laakara ngon woni nguurandam. Sinno ɓe annduno
29|65|Si ɓe waɗɗike ka laana, ɓe nodda Alla ɓe laɓɓinano Mo noddaandu ndun. Tuma nde O daɗndi ɓe ka njorndi, ontuma ɓe sirka
29|66|No ɓe yeddira ko Men okki ɓe kon, awa yo ɓe dakmito! Aray kaɓe annda
29|67|E ɓee yi'aali wonnde Men waɗii hormorde hoolniinde, yimɓe ɓen no cifee(bifte) bannge maɓɓe? E ko meere nden ɓe gomɗinta ɓe yedda neemaaji Alla ɗin
29|68|E ko hommbo ɓuri tooñirde wa on fefindiiɗo fenaande e hoore Alla, maa o fenni goonga kan nde ka arunoo e makko? E wonaa ka Jahannama woni jaaƴorde yedduɓe ɓen
29|69|Ɓen tiiɗnorɓe e (weltingol) Men, ma Men fewnirɓe e laawi Amen, ko pellet, Alla no wonndi e moƴƴinooɓe ɓen
30|1|Alif, Laam, Miim
30|2|Ruumiyankooɓe ɓen foolaama
30|3|ka ɓuri ɓadaade e leydi ndin, kamɓe kadi ɓaawo ɓe fooleede, ɓe fooloya
30|4|e nder duuɓi seeɗaaji. Ko Alla woodani fiyaaku (poolal ngal) ado e ɓaawo (maggal). Nden ñalnde, gomɗimɓe ɓen weltota
30|5|ballal Alla ngal. Himo walla mo O muuyi. Ko Kanko woni Fooloowo, Hinnotooɗo
30|6|[Ɗum] ko fodoore Alla. Alla lunndotaako fodoore Makko nden. Kono ko ɓuri ɗuuɗude e yimɓe ɓen ɓe anndaa
30|7|Hiɓe anndi ko feeñi e nguurndam aduna, kono kamɓe e fii laakara on, ko ɓe welsindiiɓe
30|8|E ɓee miijitaaki fii ko'e-maɓɓe? Alla tagiraali kammuuli ɗin e leydi ndin e ko woni hakkunde ɗin ɗiɗi, si wanaa goonga e lajal innaangal. Anndee ko ɗuuɗi e yimɓe ɓen, ko yedduɓe hawroygol e Joomi maɓɓe
30|9|E ɓee yillaaki ka leydi ɓe taskoo ko honno battane ɓen adinooɓe ɓe wa'unoo? Ɓen wonuno ɓurɓe ɓe doole ɓe remi e leydi ndin ɓe wuuri e mayri ɓuri ko ɓee wuuri e mayri kon. Nulaaɓe maɓɓe ɓen addani ɓe ɓanngannduyeeji. Alla wonaali tooñoowo ɓe, kono non ko ko'e maɓɓe ɓe wonno e tooñude
30|10|Refti ko wonunoo battane bonnuɓe ɓen, ko bonande fii ɓe fennii Aayeeje Alla ɗen, ɓe laatii e jalkitugol ɗe
30|11|Ko Alla fuɗɗi tagu ngun; refti O rutta ngu; refti ko ka Makko rutteteɗon
30|12|Ñalnde Darngal ngal darii, bomɓe ɓen taƴoto
30|13|Woodanoytaaɓe e kafidiiɗi maɓɓe ɗin tefooji, ɓe woniino yedduɓe kafiduɓe ɓen
30|14|Ñalnde Darngal ngal darii,nden ñalnde ɓe seertoyay
30|15|Si ko ɓen gomɗimɓe ɓe golli golle moƴƴe, ɓen ɗon wonoyay e beeli (Aljanna) hiɓe saɗnee(weltine)
30|16|Si tawii non ko ɓen yedduɓe ɓe fenni Aayeeje Amen ɗen e hawrugol ngol e laakara, ɓen ɗon ko tawnoyteeɓe e lepte ɗen
30|17|Subbunhinanee Alla, tuma hiiroton e tuma weetoton
30|18|Ko Kanko yettoore woodani ka kammuuli e ka leydi, e kiikiiɗe e saaga ñalloton
30|19|Himo yaltina ko wuuri e ndr ko maayi, O yaltina kadi ko maayi e nder ko wuuri. Himo wuurnita leydi ndin ɓaawo ndi yoorude. Ko wano non yatainirte- ɗon (e genaale mon)
30|20|Hino jeyaa e maandeeji Makko ɗin: wonnde O tagii on immorde e mbum-mbuldi, refti jaka ko on ɓanndike saakotooɓe [e leydi ndin]
30|21|Hino jeyaa e maandeeji Makko ɗin : wonnde O tagiranii on e wonkiiji mon ɗin, resondirɓe, fii yo on deeƴu e maɓɓe, O waɗi hakkunde mon giggol e yumeende. Wonii e ɗum, maandeeji wonannde yimɓe miijitotooɓe
30|22|Hino jeyaa e maandeeji Makko ɗin: tagugol kammuuli ɗin e leydi ndin, e luutondirgol ɗemɗe mon e mbaadiiji mon. Wonii e ɗum, maandeeji anduɓe ɓen
30|23|Hino jeyaa e maandeeji Makko ɗin: ɗoyngol mon ngol jemma e ñalorma, e ɗaɓɓugol mon ɓural Makko. Wonii e ɗum, maandeeji wonannde yimɓe nanooɓe
30|24|Hino jeyaa e maandeeji Makko ɗin: Himo hollira on maƴe ɗen kulol e tama'u (toɓo), Himo jippinira ka kammu ndiyam, O wuurnitira ɗam leydi ndin ɓaawo ndi yoorude. Wonii e ɗum, maandeeji, wonannde yimɓe haqqilooɓe
30|25|Hino jeyaa e maandeeji Makko ɗin: nde kammu ngun e leydi ndin daroto e yamiroore Makko. Refti si O noddii on noddaandu ka leydi, e jaka onon hiɗon yalta (e genaale mon)
30|26|Hino woodani (laamagol, e tagugol e toppitagol) ɓen wonɓe ka kammuuli e ka leydi: kala maɓɓe ko ɗoftiiɓe Mo
30|27|Ko Kanko woni fuɗɗuɗo tagu ngun, refti O ruttita ngu; ko ɗum ɓuri newanaande Mo. Hino woodani sifa ɓurɗo toowude ka kammuuli e ka leydi. Ko Kanko woni on Fooluɗo, Ñeeñuɗo on
30|28|O piyanii on misal immorde e ko'e-mon: hara no woodani on e ɓen ɓe jeyruɗon ñaame mon, immorde e kafidal e kon ko Men arsiki on, hara hiɗon fota e ɗum, hiɗon hulira ɓe wano hulirton ko'e-mon? Ko woni nii Men fensitirta Aayeeje ɗen, wonannde yimɓe haqqilooɓe
30|29|Si ko woni, tooñuɓe ɓen jokkirii beleeɗe maɓɓe ɗen ko aldaa e ganndal. Ko hommbo fewnata mo Alla majjini? Alanaa ɓe wallooɓe
30|30|Fewtinir yeeso maa ngon e diina kan ñiiɓugol [e mun]. [Ɗum] ko tagu Alla ngu O tagiri yimɓe ɓen e mun - waɗtitugol alaa e tagu Alla ngun -. Ko ɗum woni diina focciika kan; kono ɓurɓe ɗuuɗude e yimɓe ɓen anndaa
30|31|Hara ko on ruttotooɓe e Makko; hulon Mo, ñinnon julde nden, wata on jeye e sirkooɓe ɓen
30|32|(wano) ɓeya senndunooɓe diina mun kan, ɓe woni pecce-pecce, kala fedde no weltora ko woni ka mun kon
30|33|Si saɗteende memii yimɓe ɓen, ɓe noddira Joomi maɓɓe ko ɓe ruttitiiɓe e Makko; refti si O meeɗinii ɓe yumeende immorde e Makko, e jaka fedde goo e maɓɓe no kafida e Joomi mun
30|34|Yoɓe yeddu ko Men okki ɓe kon. "Awa dakmitee, arma anndon
30|35|Kaa Men jippin e maɓɓe hujja (Deftere), hara honde yewta fii ko ɓe sirkaynoo kon
30|36|Si Men meeɗinirii yimɓe ɓen neema, ɓe weltoroo mo. Si bone memirii ɓe sabu ko juuɗe maɓɓe ɗen ardiniri kon, e jaka hiɓe taƴoo
30|37|E ɓe yi'aali wonnde Alla no yaññana arsike on mo O muuyani, O ɓillina? Wonii e ɗum, maandeeji wonannde yimɓe gomɗinooɓe
30|38|Jonnu jom-ɓadiido o hakke makko on, e ɓilliiɓe e ɓii-laawol. Ɗum ɓuri moƴƴude wonande ɓeen faalaaɓe yarluyee Alla on; ko ɓen woni maloyteeɓe ɓen. @Corrected
30|39|Kala ko jonnuɗon e riba, fii on ɓeydor e jawle yimɓe ɓen, ɗum ɓeydotaako ka Alla, kala non ko okkuɗon e Jakka, mo faandoriɗon welayee Alla, ɓen ɗon, ko sowanoyteeɓe [njoɓdi] ɓen. @Corrected
30|40|Ko Alla woni taguɗo on, refti O arsiki on, refti O wara on, refti O wuurnita on. Hara no e kafidaaɗi mon ɗin waɗayɗi goɗɗum e ɗum? Senayeewoo-dani Mo! O toowii e kon ko ɓe sirkata
30|41|Bone on feeñiri ka njoorndi e ka maaje, sabu ko juuɗe yimɓe ɓen faggitii kon; fii yo O meeɗin ɓe yoga e ko ɓe huuwi; belajo'o, ɓe ruttoto
30|42|Maaku: "Yiilee ka leydi, ndaaron ko honno battane adinooɓe ɓen wa'unoo. Tawno ko ɓuri ɗuuɗude e maɓɓe ko sirkooɓe
30|43|Fewtinir yeeso maa ngon e diina focciika kan, ado ñalaande arde immorde ka Alla nde ruttetaake. Nde ñalnde, ɓe seeday
30|44|Kala yedduɗo, haray geddi makko ɗin no fawii mo. Kala non golluɗo moƴƴere, haray ko ko'e-maɓɓe ɓe hebilani (Aljanna)
30|45|fii yo O yoɓu ɓen gomɗimɓe ɓe golli moƴƴuɗi, e ɓural Makko ngal. Kanko On, O yiɗaa heeferɓe ɓen
30|46|Hino jeyaa e maandeeji Makko ɗin: Wurtugol Mo keneeli ɗin wewlinooji, e fii yo O meeɗin on e yurmeende Makko nden, e no laaɗe ɗen dogira e yamiroore Makko, e fii yo o ɗaɓɓu e ɓural Makko. Belajo'o, on yettay [Mo]
30|47|Gomɗii Men nulii ado maaɗa Nulaaɓe haa e yimɓe maɓɓe ɓen, ɓe addani ɓe ɓanngannduyeeji. Men yottii e ɓen bonnuɓe; tawi no jojji e Amen faabagol gomɗimɓe ɓen
30|48|Ko Alla woni nuloowo keneeɗi ɗin, ɗi sogga duule ɗen; O saakitira ɗum ka weeyo no O yiɗiri; O waɗta ɗum taƴe-taƴe. A yi'ay toɓo ngon no yalta hakkude mun. Si O hewtinii ngo e on Mo O muuyi e jeyaaɓe Makko ɓen, e jaka kamɓe hiɓe weltoo
30|49|Gomɗii ɓe laatinoke ado (toɓo) ngon jippineede e maɓɓe, ko taƴinooɓe
30|50|Ndaarii e battane yurmeende Alla nden, no O wuurnitorta leydi ɓaawo ndi yoorude. Pellet, waɗoowo ɗum On, ko wuurnitoowo maayɓe ɓen, Kanko Ko O hattanɗo kala huunde
30|51|[Hay] si Men nulii henndu, ɓe yi'i [gese maɓɓe] ɗen no soyɗi, ɓe jokkay ɓaawo ɗum, hiɓe yedda
30|52|Pellet, an a nanintaa maayɓe ɓen, a nanintaa faaɗuɓe ɓen kadi noddaandu ndun, si ɓe runtiima ɓe huccinii ɓabbe (maɓɓe)
30|53|A wonaali fewnoowo wumɓe ɓen e majjere maɓɓe. A nanintaa si wanaa ɓen gomɗimɓe Aayeeje Amen ɗen, hara ko ɓe jebbiliiɓe
30|54|Ko Alla woni taguɗo on e lo'ere, refti O waɗi ɓaawo lo'ere nden cemmbe, refti O waɗi ɓaawo cemmbe ɗen lo'ere e puri(dandanndi). Himo taga ko O muuyi, Ko Kanko woni Annduɗo, Hattanɗo
30|55|Ñalnde Darngal nal darotoo, bomɓe ɓen woonday ɓe ñiiɓaali si wanaa saanga. Ko wano nii ɓe wonanoo ferliseede (e goonga)
30|56|Okkaaɓe ganndal e gomɗinal ɓen wi'a: "Gomɗii on ñiiɓii e ko Alla winndi kon, haa ñalnde ummital. Ko ndee woni ñalaande ummital, kono onon on anndaano
30|57|Nden ñalnde, ngantooji ɗin nafoytaa tooñuɓe ɓen, wanaa kamɓe woni ko ɗaɓɓiretee welayee [Alla]. @Corrected
30|58|Gomɗii Men piyanii yimɓe ɓen e nde Alquraanaa- re, kala misal. Pellet, si a addanii ɓe Aaya, ɓen yedduɓe wi'ay: "On wonaali, si wanaa meerenteeɓe
30|59|Ko wano nii Alla notira e ɓerɗe ɓen ɓe anndaa

31|1|Alif, Laam, Miim
31|2|Ɗee, ko Aayeeje Deftere ñeñaande nden
31|3|Ko nde peewal e yurmeende wonannde moƴƴinooɓe ɓen

31|5|Ko ɓen woni e peewal immorde e Joomi maɓɓe ɓe, ko kamɓe woni malaaɓe ɓen
31|6|Hino woodi e yimɓe ɓen, soodiroowo mbeleeɗe konnguɗi haa o majjira e laawol Alla ngol ko aldaa e ganndal, o jogitora (Aayeeje) ɗen jalnitgol. Ɓen ɗon, hino woodani ɓe lepte hoynooje
31|7|Si Aayeeje Amen ɗen janngaama e makko, o huccitira(runtora) townitaare, wa si tawii o nanaali ɗe, wa si tawii ko pahu woni e noppi makko. weltanir-mo lepte muusuɗe
31|8|Pellet, ɓen gomɗimɓe ɓe golli moƴƴi ɗin, hino woodani ɓe Aljannaaji neema

31|10|O tagirii kammuuli ɗin ko aldaa e tugaale, ɗe yi'oton; O werlii ka leydi pelle fii wata ndi dillidu e mon; O saaki e mayri kala ruugayngel. Men jippiniri ndiyam ka kammu, Men fuɗini e mayri kala nooneeji tedduɗi
31|11|Ɗum ɗoo ko tagu Alla. Hollee Lam ko ɗi (rewoton ɗin) gaanin Makko tagi?" Si ko woni, tooñuɓe ɓen no e majjere ɓanngunde
31|12|Gomɗii Men okkii Luqmaan ñenƴal: "Wonnde yettu Alla. Kala yettuɗo, haray ko hoore-makko o yettani; kala non yedduɗo, anndu pellet, Alla ko Galo, Yettiniiɗo
31|13|Janto tuma Luqmaana wi'annoo geɗal makko on, hari himo waajoo mo: "Ko an ɓinngel am, wata a sirkan Alla. Pellet, sirku on ko tooñe mawɗe
31|14|Men yamirii neɗɗanke on [ɗoftagol] jibimɓe mo ɓen; yumma makko saawirii mo lo'ere e hoore lo'ere: entugol mo ngol, ko e nder duuɓi ɗiɗi. "Wonnde yettam e jinnaaɓe maa ɓen. Ko ka Am woni waɗtinirde nden
31|15|Si ɓe tiiɗnorii ma fii sirkangol Lam e ko a alanaa ɗum ganndal, wata a ɗofto ɓe; wonndir e maɓɓe ka aduna ɗoo moƴƴere. Jokku laawol on ruttiiɗo e Am. Refti ko ka Am woni ruttorde mon, Mi yeetitoo on, ko gollaynoɗon
31|16|Ko an ɓinngel am, anndu ɗen [golle bonɗe maa moƴƴe], si fotii wa abbere, immorde e nenndi foññe, ɗum wona e fetere, maa ka kammuuli maa ka leydi, Alla artiray nde. Pellet, Alla ko Newiiɗo, Humpitiiɗo
31|17|Ko an yo ɓinngel am, ñiiɓnu julde nden, yamiraa moƴƴere, haɗaa ŋiñere(pankare), muñño-ɗaa e ko heɓu-maa. Pellet, ɗum ko jeyaaɗum e fiyakkuji mawɗi. @Corrected
31|18|Wata fal yimɓe ɓen yeeso maa ngon, wata a yahru ka leydi ñaaƴagol. Pellet, Alla yiɗaa kala ñaaƴotooɗo mantoo
31|19|Hakindo e yahdu-maa ndun, joltinaa(ustu) hito maa ngon; ko ɓuri añeede e hitooji ɗin, pellet, ko luukaadu mbabba
31|20|E on yi'aali wonnde Alla eltanii on ko woni kon ka kammuuli e ka leydi? O huuɓitiri on neemaaji Makko feeñuɗi e suuɗiiɗi. Hino woodi e yimɓe ɓen, on wennjiroowo e fii Alla, ko aldaa e gannndal, wanaa peewal, wanaa Deftere jabunde
31|21|Si ɓe wi'anaa:"Jokkee kon ko Allah Jippini", ɓe wi'a: "Si ko woni, men jokkay ko men tawri kon baabiraaɓe amen ɓen"; e hay si tawii seytaane wonii hino nodda ɓe e lepte dulboowe ngen
31|22|Kala jebbiluɗo yeeso mun ngon faade e Alla, hara ko o moƴƴinɗo, gomɗii o jaggiima e ɓoggol tiiɗungol. Ko ka Alla woni battane fiyakuuji ɗin
31|23|Kala yedduɗo, wata keeferaaku makko sunine. Ko ka Amen woni ruttorde maɓɓe, Men humpita ɓe ko ɓe huuwunoo. Pellet, Alla ko Annduɗo jaati ɓerɗe
31|24|Men dakmitay ɓe seeɗa, refti Men forsaɓe e lepte tekkuɗe
31|25|Pellet, si a lamndike ɓe : "Ko hommbo tagi kammiili ɗin e leydi ndin?" Ma ɓe wi'u: "Ko Alla!" Maaku: "Yettoore woodanii Alla!". Kono ko ɓuri ɗuuɗude e maɓɓe anndaa
31|26|Ko Alla woodani kala ko woni kammuuli e ka leydi. Pellet, Alla, ko Kanko woni Galo, Yettiniiɗo
31|27|Hay si tawii ko woni ka hoore leydi kon e leɗɗe, [settiraama] karambi, maayo ngon ɓeydora (wontugol ndaha) ɓaawo ɗum, yeru maaje jeeɗiɗi, konnguɗi Alla ɗin lannataa. Pellet, Alla ko Fooluɗo, Ñeeñuɗo
31|28|Tagugol on e immintingol wonaali, si wanaa wa (tagugol) wonkii gooti. Pellet, Alla ko Nanoowo, Yi'oowo
31|29|E a yi'aali wonnde Alla no naada jemma on e nder ñalora on, O naada ñalorma kadi e nder jemma on, O eltii kadi naange ngen e lewru ndun, kala majji no doga haa e lajal innaangal? E wonnde Alla ko Humpitiiɗo ko golloton kon
31|30|Ɗum [ko jaŋtaa ɗoo], ko tawde pellet, Alla ko Kanko woni Goonga, e wonnde kon ko ɓe noddata gaanin Makko, ko ɗum woni meere nden, e wonnde ko Alla woni Toowuɗo, Mawnuɗo On
31|31|E a yi'aali wonnde laaɗe ɗen hino dogira ka maayo e neema Alla, fii yo O hollu on maandeeji Makko ɗin? Wonii e ɗum, maandeeji, wonannde kala heewuɗo-muñal, yettoowo (neema)
31|32|Si tawii morlooɗe(bempejje) hippiriiɓe wa duule [maa pelle], ɓe nodday Alla, hara hiɓe laɓɓinani Mo dewal; tuma nde O daɗndunooɓe ka njorndi, tawi no e maɓɓe hakindiiɗo. Yeddataa Aayeeje Amen ɗen, si wanaa kala heewuɗo janfa, keefeero
31|33|Ko onon yo yimɓe! Hulee Joomi mon, hulon ñalaande, nde baaba duncanoytaa ɓiɗɗo mun, wanaa ɓiɗɗo on kadi duncanoyta ben mun hay huunde. Pellet, fodoore Alla nden ko goonga. Wata nguurndam aduna hodu on, wata hodu on e Alla, (seytaane) hodoowo
31|34|Pellet, ko ka Alla woni anndal Darngal, Himo jippina toɓo; Himo anndi ko woni ka nder renngaaji. Wonkii (woo) anndaa ko ki faggitoto janngo, wonkii (woo) kadi anndaa ko e leydi honndi maayata. Pellet, Alla ko Annduɗo, Humpitiiɗo
32|1|Alif, Laam, Miim
32|2|Jippineede Deftere nden, sikke woo alaa e mu'un, ko immorde ka Jeyɗo winndere nden
32|3|Walla ɓe wi'ay kanko (Muhammadu) o fefindi nde? Si ko woni, ko nde goongaare, immorde ka Joomi maa, fii yo a jertin yimɓe, ɓe jertinoowo araano e mun ado maaɗa, belajo'o, ɓe feeway
32|4|Ko Alla woni taguɗo kammuuli ɗin e leydi ndin, e kon ko woni hakkunde majji, e nder balɗe jeegoo. Refti O fotondiri ka dow "Arski". Alanaa on gaanin Makko, giɗo wanaa tefoowo. E on waajitotaako? @Corrected
32|5|Himo fewja fiyaakuuji ɗin ka kammu haa ka leydi, refti ɗi ƴeenga ka Makko, e ñalaande nde emmbere mun woni, duuɓi ujunere e ko limoton
32|6|On [fewjoowo fii ɗum on], ko Annduɗo wirniiɗi e feeñuɗi, Fooluɗo, Hinnotooɗo
32|7|On labinɗo kala huunde nde O tagi. O fuɗɗi tagude neɗɗanke ndin e loopal
32|8|refti O waɗi geyngol makko ngol, e sortondiral, immorde ndihal [maniiyu] lo'uɗam
32|9|refi O fotndindiri mo, O wutti e makko Ruuhu Makko on. O waɗani on nanɗe, e giiɗe e ɓerɗe. [Kono] fanɗii ko yettonton
32|10|Ɓe wi': "E nee, si min majjii ka leydi, eyoo men wontay e tagu hesu?" Ko woni kamɓe e hawrugol e Joomi maɓɓe, ko ɓe yedduɓe [ɗum]
32|11|Maaku: "Ko hunnata on, ko malaa'ikaajo maayde on wakkilaaɗo on. Refti ko ka Joomi mon rutteteɗon
32|12|Sinno a yi'ayno, tuma nde bomɓe ɓen ugginta ko'e-maɓɓe ka Joomi maɓɓe! [lƁe wi'a]: "Joomi amen, men yi'ii men nanii, rutton men, men golla ko moƴƴi; menen men yananaama
32|13|Sinno Men muuyuno, Men okkayno kala wonkii peewal makki. Ko woni tun, konngol jojjii immorde e An : "Ma Mi hebbiniray Jahannama on jinna e yimɓe, ɓe denndaangal
32|14|Meeɗiree (lepte ɗen) sabu welsindagol mon hawrugol e ndee ñalaande mon ɗoo. Menen (kadi) Men yejjitii on. Meeɗiree lepte luttal, sabu ko huuwaynoɗon kon
32|15|Anndee ko gomɗinta Aayeeje Amen ɗen, ko ɓen tawɓe si ɓe waajoraama ɗe, ɓe suuyiray sujjugol, ɓe subbuhinora yettugol Joomi maɓɓe, kamɓe ɓe townitotaako
32|16|Becce maɓɓe ɗen hino woɗɗitoo e lelorɗe ɗen, hiɓe noddira Joomi maɓɓe kulol e tama'u; e kon ko Men arsiki ɓe, hiɓe wintoo
32|17|Wonkii (woo) anndaa ko maranaa ɓe e ko ɓuɓɓinta ɓernde, ɗum ko njoɓdi ko ɓe gollaynoo kon
32|18|E on laatiiɗo gomɗinɗo wa'ay wa on faasiqe? (aa'aa), ɓe fotataa
32|19|Si ko ɓen omɗimɓe ɓe golli golle moƴƴe, hino woodani ɓe Aljannaaji weerde jipporde, sabu koɓe gollaynoo kon
32|20|Si tawii non ko ɓe faasiqiiɓe, haray femporde ɓen ɗon nden, ko ka Yiite: Tuma kala ɓe faalaa yaltugol e magge, ɓe ruttitee e magge, ɓe wi'anee: "Meeɗee lepte Yiite nge fennayoɗon ngen
32|21|Ma Men meeɗinir ɓe lepte aduna, ado lepte mawɗe ɗen (laakara), belajo'o, ɓe ruttitoto
32|22|Alaa ɓurɗo tooñude wano waajoraaɗo Aayeeje Joomi mun ɗen, refti o ɗuurnii ɗe ! Pellet, Menen, ko Men yoftotooɓe e bomɓe ɓen
32|23|Gomɗii Men okkii Muusaa Deftere nden, - wata a wonu e sikke e fii hawroygol e makko -, Men waɗi nde ɗoworde ɓiɗɓe Israa'iila ɓen
32|24|Men waɗi e maɓɓe ardiiɓe, ɗowirooɓe (yimɓe ɓen) yamiroore Amen, nde ɓe muññinoo, ɓe woni yananaaɓe e Aayeeje Amen ɗen
32|25|Pellet, Joomi maa, ko Kanko senndoyta hakkunde maɓɓe, Ñalnde Darngal, e kon ko ɓe lurraynoo e fii mun
32|26|E feeñanaali ɓe, no foti ɗuuɗude e ko Men halki ado maɓɓe e gire, hiɓe yaha e koɗooli maɓɓe? Pellet, no e ɗum, tasakuyeeji ! E ɓee haqqiltaa
32|27|E ɓe yi'aali, wonnde Meɗen soggira ndiyam ɗam ka leydi hokkundi, Men yaltinira ɗam remuru, ndu neemoraaɗi maɓɓe e kamɓe ñaamata e mun? E ɓe yi'ataa
32|28|Hiɓe wi'a: "Ko honnde tuma woni ngal uddital, si on laatike goonguɓe
32|29|Maaku: "Ñalnde uddial ngal, ko heeferɓe ɓen gomɗinoyta nafoytaaɓe, wanaa kamɓe woni nennanteeɓe
32|30|Ɗuurno ɓe, haɓɓito-ɗaa. Kamɓe kan, ko ɓe haɓɓitiiɓe (lepte)
33|1|Ko an yo Annabiijo! Hulu Alla, wata a ɗofto heeferɓe ɓen e naafiqiiɓe ɓen. Pellet, Alla laatike Annduɗo, Ñeeñuɗo
33|2|Jokku ko wahayinaa kon e maaɗa, immorde ka Joomi maa. Pellet, Alla laatike Humpitiiɗo ko golloton kon
33|3|Fawo e Alla. Alla yonii faweteeɗo e mun
33|4|Alla waɗanaali neɗɗanke ɓerɗe ɗiɗi e nder fulkuru makko. O waɗaali kadi resondiraaɓe mon ɓen ɓe nanndinirton, neeniraaɓe mon. O waɗaali kadi nodditirayɓe on (baaba ɓen), ɓiɗɓe mooɗon. Ɗum mooɗon, ko kongol mon [yaltungol e] kunndule mon. Alla non, no daala goonga, ko Kanko woni fewnoowo e focciingol ngol
33|5|Noddiree ɓe baabiraaɓe maɓɓe ɓen: ko ɗum ɓuri nunɗude ka Alla. Si tawii non on anndaa baabiraaɓe maɓɓe ɓen, haray ko musiɗɓe mon ka diina e heftodiiɓe mon. Bakkaatu fawaaki on e ko woopoton (faayon) e mun, kono (on bakkondinay e) ko faandoriɗon ɓerɗe mon ɗen. Alla laatike Haforoowo, Hinnotooɗo
33|6|Ko Annabiijo on ɓuri hanndude e gomɗimɓe ɓen diini ko'e maɓɓe; suddiiɓe makko ɓen, ko neeniraaɓe maɓɓe. Joomiraaɓe enɗamaaji ɓen, ko yoga maɓɓe ɓuri hanndude yoga [e ndonndi ndin] ka Deftere Alla, diini gomɗimɓe ɓen e feruɓe ɓen, si wanaa hara on waɗan weldiiɓe mon [ɓe ronataa] ɓen moƴƴere. Ɗum wonii ko winndaa ka deftere
33|7|Janto tuma nde Men ƴettidunoo e Annabaaɓe ɓen ahadi maɓɓe, e ma'a an kadi, e Nuuhu, e Ibraahiima, e Muusaa e Iisaa ɓiɗɗo Maryama on: Men ƴettidi e maɓɓe ahadi tiiɗundi
33|8|fii no [Alla] lamdora goonguɓe ɓen e goonga maɓɓe kan. O hebilanii yedduɓe ɓen, lepte muusuuɗe
33|9|Ko onon yo gomɗimɓe ! Annditee neema Alla on e dow mooɗon, tuma nde koneeli arunoo on, Men wurti e maɓɓe henndu e konuuli, ngu on yi'aali. Alla siforii Rentuɗo ko golloton
33|10|Tuma nde ɓe ardirannoo on, ka senngo dow mon e ka ley [saare] mon, e tuma nde gite ooñinoo, ɓerɗe ɗen hewtiri ka lookoƴe, hiɗon jikka Alla (ontuma) jikke luutondirɗe
33|11|Ko ɗon gomɗimɓe ɓen njariba, ɓe dilliniraa dillere saɗtunde
33|12|Janto kadi, tuma nde naafiqiiɓe ɓen, e ɓen ɓe ñawu woni e ɓerɗe mun wi'aynoo: "Alla e Nulaaɗo Makko on fodaali men, si wanaa hodo
33|13|E tuma nde fedde goo e maɓɓe wi'unoo: "Ko onon yo yimɓe Yathrib ! Ñiiɓirde alanaa on (ɗoo), yiltitee [ka mon]". Fedde goo e maɓɓe no waynitoo Annabiijo on, hiɓe wi'a : "Cuuɗi amen ɗin ko na huncii", hara non wanaa ɗi hunciiɗi: ɓe faandaaki, si wanaa dogugol
33|14|Hay si tawno (ayɓe) ɓen naatiranno ɓe ɓannge mayre, refti ɓe lanndaa fitina (yeddugol), pellet, ɓe wonayno e mun, ɓe leelnataano e ɗum, si wanaa seeɗa
33|15|hara le gomɗii ɓe ahodiino e Alla ko adii, wonnde ɓe runtotaako ɓabbe. Ahadi Alla ndin non, ndi laatike lannditorteendi
33|16|Maaku: "Dogugol nafataa on, si on dogu maayde maa hare; haray ɗum, on dakmitetaake, si wanaa seeɗa
33|17|Maaku: "Ko hommbo woni daɗndoowo on e Alla, si O faandanike on bone, maa si O faandanike on yurmeende?" Ɓe heɓantaa ko'e maɓɓe gaanin Alla, giɗo wanaa ballo
33|18|Gomɗii Alla no anndi falaotooɓe ɓen e mon, e ɓen wi'anooɓe musiɗɓe maɓɓe ɓen :"Aree e amen", hara non ɓe arataa e hare nden, si wanaa seeɗa
33|19|ko wuddan ɓe on. Si kulol ngol arii, a yi'ay hiɓe ndaare, hara gite maɓɓe no yiilora wa mo maayde suddaa e mun. Si kulo ngol non yehii, ɓe laggora ɗemɗe muusuɗe, wuddangol moƴƴere nden. Ɓen ɗon, ɓe gomɗinaali, Alla bonnii golle maɓɓe ɗen. Ɗum wonii ko newanii Alla
33|20|Hiɓe sikka koneeli ɗin yahataa. Hay si koneeli ɗin artii, ɓee [naafiqiiɓe] yelotono sinno hara nun hiɓe ka ladde hakkunde yimɓe ladde ɓen, hara hiɓe lanndo fii mon. Hay si ɓe tawtodano e mon, ɓe haɓataano si wanaa seeɗa nii
33|21|Gomɗii laatanike on e Nulaaɗo Alla on, ñemtinal moƴƴal, wonannde on jortiiɗo Alla, e Ñalaande sakkitiinde nden, o jantii Alla ko ɗuuɗi
33|22|Nde gomɗimɓe ɓen yi'unoo koneeli ɗin, ɓe wi'i: "Ko ɗum woni ko Alla e Nulaaɗo Makko on fodi men; haray Alla e Nulaaɗo Makko on goongii". Ɗum ɓeydaali ɓe, si wanaa gomɗinal e jebbilaare
33|23|Hino e gomɗimɓe ɓen, worɓe hunnuɓe ko ɓe ahodi e Alla kon : hino e maɓɓe timminɗo takke mun ɗen (haa o sahodinaa), hino e maɓɓe kadi haɓɓitiiɗo; ɓe waɗtitaali (ahadi ndin) mbattiigu
33|24|Fii yo Alla yoɓir hunnuɓe ɓen sabu goongude maɓɓe, O lepta naafiqiiɓe ɓen, si Mo yiɗi, maa O jaɓana ɓe tuubuubuyee. Tawde pellet, Alla laatike Haforoowo, Hinnotooɗo
33|25|Alla ruttidii yedduɓe ɓen e tikkere maɓɓe nden, ɓe heɓaali moƴƴere. Alla yonii gomɗimɓe ɓen e hare. Alla siforii Cemmbe e Poolal
33|26|O jipiini ɓen wallindirnooɓe jeyaaɓe e yimɓe Defte ɓen, ka tataaji maɓɓe ɗin, O weddii ɗenƴere e ɓerɗe maɓɓe; fedde goo (e maɓɓe) hiɗon wara, hiɗon daha kadi fede goo
33|27|O ronini on leydi maɓɓe, e galleeji maɓɓe, e jawle maɓɓe, e leydi ndi on tippaano e mun. Alla siforii hattanɗo kala huunde
33|28|Ko an yo Annabiijo ! Maakan suddiiɓe maa ɓen: "Si wonii ko nguurndam aduna faalaɗon e cuɗaari majjam, haray aree mi dakmita on, mi seera on [ontuma] cergal moƴƴal
33|29|Si tawii non ko Alla faalaɗon, e Nulaaɗo Makko on, e galle laakara ɗen, haray pellet, Alla maranii moƴƴimɓe ɓen e mooɗon, njoɓdi mawndi
33|30|Ko onon yo suddiiɓe Annabiijo on ! Kala adduɗo e mooɗon bone ɓannguɗo, lepte ɗen sowirante mo cowalle ɗiɗi! Ɗum wonii ko newanii Alla
33|31|Kala e mooɗon ɗoftiiɗo Alla e Nulaaɗo Makko on, o golli ko moƴƴi, Men yoɓiray mo njoɓdi makko ndin laaɓi ɗiɗi, Meɗen marani mo kadi, arsike tedduɗo
33|32|Ko onon yo suddiiɓe Annabiijo! On wa'aa wano gooto e suddiiɓe ɓen. Si on gomɗii, haray wata on yergin konngol, sakko on mo ñawu [tuuyo] woni e ɓernde mun tamƴinoo. Wowlon konngol moƴƴol
33|33|Ñiiɓee ka cuuɗi mon; wata on feññinir cuɗaari mon, wano wirtaare majjere adinooɓe. Ñiiɓnee Julde nden, totton askal on, ɗoftoɗon Alla e Nulaaɗo Makko on. Anndee ko Alla faandii, ko ittanta on e tuuɗe, onon yimɓe suudu [Annabiijo], O laɓɓinira on laɓɓingol
33|34|Jantee ko wonaa e janngeede ka cuuɗi mon, immorde e Aayeeje Alla, e Sunna. Pellet, Alla laatike Newiiɗo, Humpitiiɗo
33|35|Pellet, juulɓe worɓe ɓen e juulɓe rewɓe ɓen, e gomɗimɓe worɓe ɓen e gomɗimɓe rewɓe ɓen, e ɗoftiiɓe worɓe ɓen e ɗoftiiɓe rewɓe ɓen, e goonguɓe worɓe ɓen e goonguɓe rewɓe ɓen, e muññiiɓe worɓe ɓen e muññiiɓe rewɓe ɓen, e yankiniiɓe worɓe ɓen e yankiniiɓe rewɓe ɓen, e sakkotooɓe worɓe ɓen e sakkotooɓe rewɓe ɓen, e hoorooɓe worɓe ɓen e hoorooɓe rewɓe ɓen, e worɓe reenooɓe farjuuji mun e rewɓe reenooɓe farjuuji mun, e worɓe jantotooɓe Alla ko ɗuuɗi ɓen e rewɓe jantotooɓe ɓen: Alla maranii ɓen, haforanal e njoɓdi mawndi
33|36|Alanaa gomɗiɗo gorko, wanaa gomɗinɗo debbo, si Alla e Nulaaɗo Makko on ñaawii fiyaaku, nde suɓagol e fiyaaku maɓɓe on. Kala non yedduɗo Alla e Nulaaɗo Makko on, haray o majjii majjere ɓanngunde
33|37|Janto tuma maakanayno-ɗaa on mo Alla neemini e mun, moƴƴu-ɗaa e makko: "Jogitano suddiiɗo maa on, hoore-maa, hulaa Alla", hiɗa suuɗa e fonndo maa, ko Alla feññinta. Hiɗa hula yimɓe ɓen, kono ko Alla fotu-ɗaa hulude. Tuma Zaydu huntunoo e (suddiiɗo) on haaju, Men resin-maa mo, fii wata ɓittere wonu e gomɗimɓe ɓen, e (resugol) suddiiɓe nodditiraaɓe maɓɓe ɓen, si ɓen huntii e maɓɓe haaju. Yamiroore Alla nden laatike golleteende
33|38|Feloore alanaa Annabiijo on, e kon ko Alla daginai mo, ɗum ko ñaawoore Alla e ɓen feƴƴuɓe ado makko. Ñaawoore Alla nde wonii eɓɓaande hoddiraande
33|39|Ɓen yottiinooɓe nule Alla ɗen, ɓe no hula Mo, ɓe hula goɗɗo goo si wanaa Alla. Alla yonii hasboowo
33|40|Muhammadu wonaali baaba hay goot e worɓe mon, ko [o] woni, ko Nulaaɗo Alla e timmoode Annabaaɓe. Alla laatike Annduɗo kala huunde
33|41|Ko onon yo ɓen gomɗimɓe, jantoree Alla jantoore ɗuuɗunde
33|42|Subhinee Mo bimmbi e kiikiiɗe
33|43|Ko Kanko woni yurmeteeɗo on, -e Malaa'ikaaɓe Makko ɓen (du'orana on), - fii no O yaltinira on e niɓe faade e annoora. O siforii hinnotooɗo gomɗimɓe ɓen
33|44|Hiwrondiral maɓɓe ngal ñalnde ɓe hawrata e Makko, ko "Salaam" [kisiyee], O maranii ɓe mbarjaari teddundi
33|45|Ko an yo Annabiijo ! Men nulirii ma [fii yo wonu] seediiɗo, e wewlinoowo e jertinoowo
33|46|e noddoowo faade e Alla, duŋayee Makko; e pitilol jalɓungol
33|47|Wewlinir gomɗimɓe ɓen, wonnde no woodani ɓe ka Alla, ɓural mawnungal
33|48|Wata a ɗofto heeferɓe ɓen e naafiqiiɓe ɓen, ɗuurno (e) lorra maɓɓe kan, fawo-ɗaa e Alla. Sabu Alla yonii ka fawee
33|49|Ko onon yo ɓen gomɗimɓe ! Si resii rewɓe gomɗimɓe ɓen, refti on seerii ɓe ado on meemondirde e maɓɓe, haray alanaa on e maɓɓe, edda mo ɓe eddinotoo. Dakmitiree ɓe [njooɓa], seeriron ɓe cergal laɓaangal
33|50|Ko an yo Annabiijo ! Men daginanii ma suddiiɓe maa ɓen ɓe jonnu-ɗaa teŋe mun ɓen, e ɓen [horɓe] ɓe jeyru-ɗaa ñaamo maa, e ɓen [dahaaɓe] ɓe Alla neldu-maa, e jiwɓe bappa maa, e jiwɓe yaayiraaɓe maa, e jiwɓe kaawu-maa, e jiwɓe neeniraaɓe maa, - ɓen feridunooɓe e maa, - e suddiiɗo gomɗinɗo, si o yeɗii hoore-makko Annabiijo on, si Annabiijo on kadi faandike resugol mo : ɗum ko ko heerani maa, gaanin gomɗimɓe ɓen. Gomɗii Meɗen anndi ko Men farli e maɓɓe kon, e fii suddiiɓe maɓɓe ɓen, e ko ɓe jeytiri ñaame maɓɓe ɗen, fii wata ɓiɗteende wonu e maaɗa. Alla laatike haforoowo, Hinnotooɗo
33|51|Hiɗa nennintina on mo yiɗu-ɗaa (nennintinnde) e maɓɓe, ɓaɗtinaa e maaɗa on mo yiɗu-ɗaa. E on mo ɗaɓɓu-ɗaa (belagol ka mun) e ɓen ɓe nennitu-ɗaa, bakkaaku woo fawaaki ma. Ko ɗum ɓuri ɓadaade e ko ɓuɓɓinta ɓerɗe maɓɓe, hara ɓe sunotaako, ɓe weltora kadi ko okku-ɗaa ɓe kon, ɓe fow maɓɓe. Alla no Anndi ko woni e ɓerɗe mon. Alla laatike Annduɗo, Muññiiɗo
33|52|Rewɓe ɓen dagitantaako ma ɓaawo [ɓee ɗoo], wanaa nde waɗtitirtaa ɓe genndiraaɓe goo, hay si ŋari ɓen ɗon haawnii ma; si wanaa ɓe jeyru-ɗaa ñaamo maa ɓen. Alla laatike tommbiiɗo kala huunde
33|53|Ko onon yo ɓen gomɗimɓe ! Wata on naatu ka cuuɗi Annabiijo on, si wanaa hara on nodda e ñaametee, hara wanaa yo on habbito ko ɓenndi ka makko. Kono si on noddaa ma, naatee. Si on ñaamii, sentee, hara on ɗaɓɓaali haala. Anndon ɗum mooɗon, hino lorraynoo Annabiijo on, kono o hersa (haalannde) on, Alla non ɗalataa [yamirde] goonga. Si on lanndoto (suddiiɓe makko) ɓen haaju, lanndoree ɓe ɓaawo wirngallo: ko ɗum mooɗon, ɓuri laaɓannde ɓerɗe mon e ɓerɗe maɓɓe. Haananaa on nde lorroton Nulaaɗo Alla on, wanaa nde resoton suddiiɓe maɓɓe ɓen ɓaawo makko, poomaa; pellet, waɗugol mon ɗum, wonii ko mawni ka Alla
33|54|Si on feññinii huunde, maa on suuɗii nde, pellet, Alla laatike annduɗo kala huunde
33|55|Bakkaatu fawaaki ɓe e baabiraaɓe maɓɓe ɓen, wanaa kadi ɓiɗɓe maɓɓe ɓen, wanaa banndiraaɓe maɓɓe ɓen, wanaa e ɓiɗɓe banndiraaɓe maɓɓe ɓen, wanaa e ɓiɗɓe miññiraaɓe maɓɓe rewɓe ɓen, wanaa e rewɓe maɓɓe ɓen, wanaa e ɓen ɓe ɓe jeyiri ñaame maɓɓe. Hulee Alla (yo suddiiɓe). Pellet, Alla siforii seediiɗo kala huunde
33|56|Pellet, Alla e Malaa'ikaaɓe Makko ɓen, hiɓe du'anaade Annabiijo on; ko onon yo ɓen gomɗimɓe, juulee e makko, toranoɗon [Mo] kisiyee
33|57|Pellet, ɓen lorrooɓe Alla e Nulaaɗo Makko on, Alla huɗii ɓen aduna e laakara, O hebilanii ɓe kadi lepte hoynooje
33|58|Ɓen kadi lorrooɓe gomɗimɓe worɓe ɓen e gomɗimɓe rewɓe ɓen, e hoore ko ɓe faggitaaki, gomɗii ɓe ronndike fenaande e bakkaatu ɓannguɗo
33|59|Ko an yo Annabiijo! Maakan suddiiɓe maa ɓen, e jiwɓe maa ɓen, e genndiraaɓe gomɗimɓe ɓen, nde ɓe joltinta e maɓɓe, wutteeji maɓɓe ɗin: ko ɗum ɓurata ɓaɗtaade, nde ɓe annditetee, hara ɓe torraaka. Alla laatike Haforoowo, Hinnotooɗo
33|60|Pellet, si naafiqiiɓe ɓen haɗitaaki, e ɓen ɓe ñawu (sikkitaare) woni e ɓerɗe mun, e fena-fenta'en ka saare Madiina, ma Men wurtite e maɓɓe, refi ɓe kawtirtaa e maaɗa ton, si wanaa seeɗa
33|61|Ko huɗaa ɓe. Kala ka ɓe tawaa, ko ɓe nanngetee ɓe, ɓe waree wargol
33|62|Ɗum ko sunna Alla e ɓen wulinooɓe ko adii. A heɓantaa laawol (sunna) Alla ngol, battiigu
33|63|Yimɓe ɓen o lanndo maa fii Darngal. Maaku : "Anndee ganndal daragol maggal, ko ka Alla woni". E ko anndin maa, wonnde no hasii hara Darngal ngal ɓadike
33|64|Pellet, Alla huɗii heeferɓe ɓen, O kammbiranii ɓe kadi dulboowe
33|65|ko ɓe luttooɓe ton poomaa. Ɓe heɓataa giɗo, wanaa ballo
33|66|Ñalnde geece maɓɓe ɗen waylitetee ka Yiite, ɓe wi'ay: "Ee jalla amen! Hara men ɗoftino Alla, men ɗoftii Nulaaɗo on
33|67|Ɓe wi'a: "Joomi amen, Menen men ɗofti hooreeɓe amen e mawɓe amen, ɓe majjini men e laawol ngol
33|68|Joomi amen, tottu ɓe cowanlle ɗiɗi e lepte ɗen, huɗaa ɓe kuddi mawndi
33|69|Ko onon yo ɓen gomɗimɓe! Wata on wa'u wa ɓen lorrunooɓe Muusaa, Alla woɗɗini mo e ko ɓe wi'i kon, tawde o wonii tedduɗo ka Alla
33|70|Ko on yo ɓen gomɗimɓe! Hulee Alla, wowlon konngol feewungol
33|71|[Si on waɗii ɗum], O moƴƴinanay on golle mon, O haforana on junuubi mon. Kala ɗoftiiɗo Alla e Nulaaɗo Makko on, haray o maliraama maloore mawnde
33|72|Men weeɓitii hoolaare nden e dow kammuuli ɗin, e leydi ndin e pelle ɗen, ɗi haɗitii ronndagol nde, ɗi huli (battane) majji, neɗɗo on kan ronndii nde; tawde pellet, o wonii ɗuuɗuɗo-tooñude [hoore-mun], majjaaɗo [battane ɗum]
33|73|[Neɗɗo on ronndiraama ɗum], no Alla leptira naafiqiiɓe worɓe ɓen e naafiqiiɓe rewɓe ɓen, e sirkooɓe worɓe ɓen e sirkooɓe rewɓe ɓen, e (no) Alla jaɓirana gomɗimɓe worɓe ɓen e gomɗimɓe rewɓe ɓen tuububuyee. Alla laatike Haforoowo, Hinnotooɗo
34|1|Yettoore woodanii Alla, On jeyɗo kala ko woni ka kammuuli e ka leydi. Hino woodani Mo kadi yettoore ka laakara. Ko Kanko woni Ñeeño, Humpitiiɗo
34|2|Himo anndi ko naatata ka leydi, e ko yaltata e mayri, ko jippotoo iwra ka kammu e ko ƴawata e maggu. Ko Kanko woni Hinnotoo, Haforoowo
34|3|Yedduɓe ɓen wi'i: "Darngal ngal arataa men". Maaku: "aa'a! Mi woondirii Joomi am! pellet, ko aray e mon. [Joomi ma] ko Annduɗo wirniiɗi. Huunde wirnanaaki Mo, ko fotata e abbere jarra, woni ka kammuuli maa ka leydi. Wanaa ko ɓuri ɗum fanɗude, wanaa ko ɓuri ɗum mawnude, si wanaa no e deftere feññinnde
34|4|Fii yo O yoɓoy ɓen gomɗimɓe, ɓe golli moƴƴuɗi. Ɓen ɗon, hino woodani ɓe haforaneede, e arsike tedduɗo
34|5|Ɓen non yaccii ɓe e bonnitugol Aayeeje Amen ɗen, ɓen ɗon, hino woodani ɓe lepte, immorde e ɓurɗe muusude
34|6|Ɓen okkaaɓe ganndal hino yi'ira jippiniraande nden e maaɗa, immorde ka Joomi maa, ko kayre woni goonga, hinde fewnira e laawol Fooluɗo, Yettiniiɗo On
34|7|Yedduɓe ɓen kadi wi'i: "On accay men tinndina on fii gorko, mo no humpita on, wonnde si on muncitaama kala muncitannde, on wontoyay e tagu hesu
34|8|O fefindi fenaande e hoore Alla? Kaa hara ko jinna nanngi mo? Si ko woni, ɓen ɓe gomɗinaa laakara on, ɓe wonii e lepte e majjere woɗɗiinde (goonga)
34|9|E ɓee yi'aali ko woni yeeso maaɓe e ko woni ɓaawo maɓɓe immorde ka kammu e ka leydi? Si Men muuyiino, Men munnirayno ɓe leydi ndin, maa Men fukkina e maɓɓe taƴontine (lepte), immorde ka kammu. Wonii e ɗum, maande, wonannde kala jeyaaɗo ruttotooɗo (e Joomi mun)
34|10|Gomɗii Men okkii Daawuuda ɓural, immorde e Amen. [Men wi'i]: "Ko onon pelle e colli, subbunhinodee e makko. Men newinani mo (tafugol) njamndi ndin
34|11|(Men wi'ani mo wonnde): "Gollu wutteeji njamndi, eɓɓaa ka tafoodi. Gollon golle moƴƴe, pellet, ko Mi Reenuɗo ko golloton kon
34|12|(Men eltani kadi) Sulaymaana henndu ndun: dawol mayru ko yeru (yaadu) lewru, kirndol mayru kadi ko yeru (yaadu) lewu. Men honcinani mo ɓunndu sila (kire). Hino jinnaaji ɗin, golliraynooɗi yeeso makko, e duŋayee Joomi Makko. Kala ooñiingii e majji, gaay e yamiroore Amen nden, Men meeɗina ngii lepte dulɓoowe ngen
34|13|Hiɗi gollana mo ko o faalaa: gila e tataaji, e nanndollaaji, e looɗe wa'uɗe wa beeli, e payanɗe feŋiiɗe. "Gollee, onon ɓeynguure Daawuuda, yetton (Alla)", fanɗii e jeyaaɓe Am ɓen, yettoowo (Lam)
34|14|Nde Men ñaawunoo e makko maayde nden, anndinaali ɗi fii maayde makko nden, si wanaa gannguuji leydi(mooƴu) ɗin, hino ñaama tuggordu makko ndun. Nde o fukkinoo, feeñani jinnaaji ɗin, wonnde si ɗi anndunoo ko wirnii, ɗi ñiiɓataano e lepte [jeyaagu] hoynooje
34|15|Gomɗii wonaniino yimɓe Saba'i ɓen e koɗooli maɓɓe ɗin, maande; gese ɗiɗi ka bannge ñaamo e ka nano. (Men wi'ani ɓe): "Ñaamee e arsike Joomi mon, yetton Mo. Leydi ndin ko laaɓundi, e Joomiraawo Haforoowo
34|16|(Kono) ɓe ɗuunii. Men wurti e maɓɓe ndiyam waame, Men waɗtitani ɓe gese maɓɓe ɗen ɗiɗi, gese (goo) ɗiɗi, marɗe ñaametee haaɗuɗo, e (leɗɗe) duɓɓeeje, e huunde e jaaɓe seeɗaaje
34|17|Ngool (yaggingol), Men yoɓirɓe ko ɓe yeddi kon. E hara Men yoɓay si wanaa yedduɓe ɓen
34|18|Men waɗi hakkune maɓɓe e koɗooli ɗi Men waɗi barki e mun ɗin, koɗooli feeñondirɗi, Men eɓɓi e majji yaadu. (Men wi'ani ɓe): "Yehee ton jemmaaji e ñalormaaji, ko on hooliiɓe
34|19|Ɓe wi'i: "Joomi amen, woɗɗindir hakkunde yaaduuji amen", ɓe tooñi ko'e maɓɓe, Men waɗti fillitee ɓe fii mun, Men senndindiri ɓe hattirde e senndirgol. Pellet, wonii e ɗum, maandeeji wonannde kala heewuɗo muñal, yettoowo (neema)
34|20|Gomɗii Ibuliisa goonginii jikke mun ɗen e maɓɓe. Ɓe jokki mo, si wanaa fedde e gomɗimɓe ɓen
34|21|E doole alanaa mo e dow maɓɓe, cemmbe (wurtugol), si wanaa tun, ko fii no Men anndira on gomɗinɗo laakara e on wonɗo e sikke fii mun. Joomi maa non, e dow kala huunde, ko O reenuɗo
34|22|Maaku: "Noddee ɗin ɗi ɗaynitorɗon [ reweteeɗi] gaanin Alla. Ɗi jeyaa hay yeru abbere jarra, ka kammuuli wanaa ka leydi. Alanaa ɗi e ɗin (kammuuli e leydi ndin) kafidaaɗo (geɓal), alanaa Mo e ɗin, hay wallondirteeɗo
34|23|Tefoore woo nafataa ka Makko, si wanaa on Mo O duŋanii. Haa si ɗenƴere nden yaltinaama e ɓerɗe maɓɓe ɗen, ɓe wi'a: "Ko honɗum Joomi mon daali?" Ɓe wi'a: "Ko goonga kan; ko Kanko woni Toowuɗo, Mawɗo On
34|24|Maaku: "Kon hombo woni arsikiroowo on ka kammuuli e ka leydi?" Maaku: "Ko Alla. Ko si ko menen maa si ko onon, woni e peewal maa e nder majjere ɓanngunde
34|25|Maaku: "On lamnditoytaake fii ko men bonni, menen kadi men lamnditoytaake fii ko huuwoton
34|26|Maaku: "Joomi men renndinoyay en, refti O ñaawira hakkunde men goonga; Ko Kanko woni Ñaawoowo, Annduɗo On
34|27|Maaku: "Hollee lam ɗin ɗi waɗtidu-ɗon e Makko kafidiiɗi. Wanaa non woniri! Si ko woni, ko Kanko woni Alla Fooluɗo, Ñeeñuɗo On
34|28|Men nuliraali ma, si wanaa e yimɓe ɓen fow: wewlinoowo e jertinoowo. Kono ko ɓuri ɗuuɗude e yimɓe ɓen, ɓe anndaa
34|29|Hiɓe wi'a: "Ko honnde tuma woni ndee Fodoore, si on laatike goonguɓe
34|30|Maaku: "Hino woodani on fodoore, nde o nennitantaake e mayre fotde saa'i, on ardintinantaake nde kadi
34|31|Yedduɓe ɓen wi'i: "Men gomɗintaa ndee Alqur'aanaare muk, wanaa nden adiinde nde". Sinno a tinayno tuma nde tooñuɓe ɓen darnetee ka Joomi maɓɓe, hara yoga maɓɓe no rutta yoga konngol, lo'inanooɓe ɓen wi'ana townitinooɓe ɓen: "Si wanaano onon nun, men wonayno gomɗimɓe
34|32|Townitinooɓe ɓen wi'ani lo'inanooɓe ɓen: "E ko menen falinoo on e peewal ɓaawo ngal arde e mon? Si ko woni, on woniino bomɓe
34|33|Lo'inanooɓe ɓen kadi wi'ani townitinooɓe ɓen: "Si ko woni, ko pewje (mon) jemma e ñalorma, tuma yamiraynoɗon men yo men yeddu Alla, men waɗana Mo fotondirɗi". Ɓe suuɗi ninse ɗen, nde ɓe yi'unoo lepte ɗen. Men waɗi kolombooje e daaɗe ɓen yedduɓe. Hara ɓe yoɓitete si wanaa ko ɓe huuwaynoo kon
34|34|Men nulaali jertinoowo e yimɓe saare, si wanaa neeminaaɓe mayre ɓen wi'ay: "Menen ko men yedduɓe ko nulidaɗon kon
34|35|Ɓe wi'i kadi: "Ko menen ɓuri ɗuuɗude jawle e ɓiɓɓe, men wonaali kadi lepteteeɓe
34|36|Maaku: "Pellet, Joomi am hino weertana arsike on, mo O muuyi, O ɓillini (mo O muuyi). Kono ɓurɓe ɗuuɗude e yimɓe ɓen, ɓe anndaa
34|37|Wanaa jawle mon, wanaa jiidi mon woni ko ɓaɗtinirta on ka Amen ɓadal. Si wanaa ɓen gomɗimɓe ɓe golli golle moƴƴe; ɓen ɗon, hino woodani ɓe njoɓdi sowaande, sabu ko ɓe golli kon, kamɓe ka soorooji, ko ɓe hooliiɓe
34|38|Ɓen yaccotooɓe e ronkingol (yimɓe ɓen) e Aayeeje Amen ɗen, ɓen ɗon, ka ka nder lepte woni ko ɓe tawnoytee
34|39|Maaku: "Pellet, Joomi am hino weertana arsike on, mo O muuyani e jeyaaɓe Makko ɓen, O ɓillini mo (O muuyi e maɓɓe). Kala non ko wintiɗon e huunde, Kanko O lontinay nde. Ko Kanko woni Moƴƴo Arsikoowo
34|40|Ñalnde O mooɓtindiroyta ɓe dendaangal, refti O daalana Malaa'ikaaɓe ɓen: "E ko ɓee ɗoo (yimɓe) rewaynoo on
34|41|Ɓe wi'a: "Senayee woodanii Ma! Ko An woni giɗo amen gaanin maɓɓe. Toode ko jinnaaji ɗin ɓe rewaynoo, ko ɓuri ɗuuɗude e maɓɓe, ko ɗin (jinnaaji) gomɗini
34|42|Hannde non, yoga mon waawanaa yoga nafa wanaa lorra. Men wi'anoya ɓen tooñuɓe: "Meeɗee lepte Yiite nge fennaynoɗon fii mun
34|43|Si Aayeeje Amen ɓannguɗe ɗen janngaamma e maɓɓe, ɓe wi'a: "Oo wonaali, si wanaa gorko faalaaɗo falagol on e ko baabiraaɓe mon rewayno rewaynoo". Ɓe wi'i: "Ndee (Alqur’aanaare) wonaali, si wanaa fenaande fefindaande". Yedduɓe ɓen wi'ani goonga kan nde ka arunoo e maɓɓe: "Ndee wonaali, si wanaa mbilewu ɓanngu ngu
34|44|Men addanaali ɓee, defte ɗe ɓe janngata. Men meeɗaali nulude e maɓɓe, jertinoowo ado maa
34|45|Adinooɓe ɓe ɓen [kadi] fenniino (nulaaɓe mun). [Yimɓe maa ɓen] yottaaki sappaɓal ko Men okkunoo ɓen kon. Ɓen fenni Nulaaɓe Amen ɓen, taskii no lepte Am ɗen wa'unoo
34|46|Maaku: "Anndee ko mi waajorta on, ko (huunde) wootere: "Ko nde daroranton Alla ɗiɗo ɗiɗo e gooto gooto, refti miijitoɗon. (Anndon) wondiiɗo mon on aldaa e jinna: O wonaali, si wanaa jertinoowo on, e ko woni yeeso (mon), e lepte saɗtuɗe
34|47|Maaku: "Mi lamndaaki on njoɓdi, ɗum ko fii mon. Njoɓdi am ndin wonaali, si wanaa ka Alla. Kanko Ko O Seediiɗo e kala huunde
34|48|Maaku: "Pellet, Joomi am ko werlortooɗo [meere nden, hujjaaji] goonga kan, timminɗo anndugol wirniiɗi
34|49|Maaku: "Goonga kan arii [Iislaamu on], meere [keeferaaku] ngun alaa ka feeña, kadi, nde ruttotaako
34|50|Maaku: "Si mi majjii, haray ko hoore-am mi majjani; si mi feewii kadi, ko sabu ko sabu ko Joomi am wahayini e am kon, tawde pellet, ko O Nanoowo, Ɓadiiɗo
34|51|Sinno a tinayno, tuma nde ɓe ɗenyii, - laaworde alanaa (ɓe), - ɓe nanngiree e nokkuure ɓadiinde
34|52|Ɓe wi'a: "Men gomɗinii [Darngal] ngal", e ko honno gomɗinal woonirani ɓe e nokku woɗɗuɗo
34|53|Hara non ɓe yeddiino nde ko adii, hiɓe werlora ko wirnii e nokku woɗɗuɗo
34|54|Heedee hakkunde e ko ɓe tuuyetee, wano golliranoo e nanndo maɓɓe ko adii, tawde ɓe woniino e sikke cikkiniiɗa
35|1|Yettoore woodanii Alla, Taguɗo kammuuli ɗin e leydi ndin, Waɗuɗo Malaa'ika'en nulaaɓe, marɓe gabitanji(bibje) ɗi ɗiɗi, ɗi tati e nayi. Himo ɓeyda ko O muuyi e tagu Makko ngun, tawde pellet, Alla ko hattanɗo kala huunde
35|2|Kala yurmeende nde Alla udditani yimɓe ɓen, jogitotooɗo nde alaa; kala kadi ko O jogitii, accitoowo ɗum alaa ɓaawo (jogitagol) Makko. Ko Kanko woni Fooluɗo, Ñeeñuɗo
35|3|Ko onon yo yimɓe! jantee neema Alla on e mon. Hara tagoowo ko woori Alla no woodi, mo no arsikira on ka kammu e ka leydi? Reweteeɗo alaa si wanaa Kanko! E ko honno yiilirteɗon [e kaa goonga]
35|4|Si ɓe fennii ma, pellet Nulaaɓe (goo) fennanooma ado maa. Ko faade e Alla, woni ruttorde fiyakuuji ɗin
35|5|Ko onon yo yimɓe! Anndee pellet fodoore Alla nden ko goonga. Wata nguurndam aduna hodu on, wata (seytaane) hodoowo on hodu on e fii Alla
35|6|Pellet, seytaane ko gaño wonani on. Haray jogitoree mo gaño. Anndee ko o noddirta fedde makko nden, ko no ɓe jeydiree e yimɓe dulɓoowe ngen
35|7|Hino woodani yedduɓe ɓen, lepte saɗtuɗe. Ɓeya gomɗimɓe ɓe golli golle moƴƴe, hino woodani ɓe haforaneede e njoɓdi mawndi
35|8|E ko on cuɗinanaaɗo golle mun bonɗe, hara himo yi'a ɗe moƴƴuɗe? - Tawde pellet, Alla no majjina on Mo O muuyi, O fewna Mo O muuyi. Wata a tampinir hoore-maa, sunagol fii maɓɓe. Pellet, Alla ko Annduɗo ko ɓe woni huuwude
35|9|Ko Alla woni wurtuɗo keneeli ɗin, ɗi sogga duule, Men yarnira ɗum leydi yoorundi; Men wuurnitira ɗum leydi ndin, ɓaawo ndi yoorude. Ko wano non ummital ngal
35|10|Kala tawɗo ko teddungal faalaa (yo o ɗaɓɓir Alla), tawde ko Alla jeyi teddungal ngal fow: ko ka Makko woni ko konngol laaɓungol ƴawata, golle moƴƴe ɗen ɓamta ngol. Ɓen fewjooɓe boneeji, hino woodani ɓe lepte saɗtuɗe. Pewje ɓen ɗen, ko bonay ɗe
35|11|Ko Alla tagiri on e mbulbuldi, refti e toɓɓere (maniiyu), refti O waɗi on nooneeji. Deyel saawataa, ngel lelnataa kadi, si wanaa e anndal Makko. Wuurnaaɗo wuurnetaake, ɗuytetaake kadi e nguurndam makko, si wanaa no e deftere. Pellet, ɗum ko newanii ɗum Alla
35|12|Maaje ɗen ɗiɗi fotataa: [Ndiyam] goo ɗoo ɗam, ko welɗam, laaɓungo, newiingo njaram mun, ngoo ɗaa, ko lanɗam haaɗuɗam. Hiɗon ñaama e kala majjam, teewu keccu, hiɗon yaltina kadi hen, cuɗaari ndi ɓoornotoɗon. Hiɗa yi'a laaɗe ɗen no awja e maggo, fii yo on ɗaɓɓiron e ɓural Makko. Belajoo on yettay [Mo]
35|13|Himo naada jemma on e der ñalorma on, O naada ñalorma on e nder jemma on. O elti kadi naange ngen e lewru ndun. Kala mun no doga haa e lajal innaangal. Ko On mooɗon woni Alla, Joomi mon: Ko Kanko Laamu woodani. Ɗiya ɗi noddoton gaanin Makko, ɗi jeytaa yeru gorol tamara
35|14|Si on noddu ɗi, ɗi nanataa noddaandu mon; hay si ɗi nanoy, ɗi jaabitotaako on. Ñalnde Darngal, ɗi yeddoyay sirku mon on. Alaa habroowo ma, wano Humpitiiɗo On
35|15|Ko onon yo yimɓe, ko onon woni hatonjimɓe e Alla ɓen, Alla kan, ko Kanko woni Galo Yettiniiɗo On
35|16|Si O yiɗii, O naɓa on, O adda tagu hesu
35|17|Ɗum wonaali sattuɗum ka Alla
35|18|Wonki ronndotaako doŋgal wonkii goo. Hay si teddiraaki [junuubi] kin noddii e ronndaneede, ki ronndantaake hay huunde, hay si ko ɓadondiraaɗo Anndu ko jertintaa [nana waaju], ko ɓen hulirooɓe Joomi mun ka wirnii, ɓe ñiiɓi e Julde. Kala on laɓɓiniiɗo, haray ko hoore makko o woni laɓɓinanaade. Ko ka Alla woni ruttorde nden
35|19|Bunɗo e yi'oowo fotataa
35|20|wanaa niɓe ɗen e ndaygu ngun
35|21|wanaa ɗowdi ndin e henndu wulndu ndun
35|22|Wanaa kadi wuurɓe ɓen fotata e maayɓe ɓen. Pellet, Alla no nanina on Mo O muuyani. Wanaa an [Nulaaɗo], woni naninoowo, wonɓe ka genaale ɓen
35|23|An a wonaali, si wanaa jertinoowo
35|24|Pellet, Men nulirii ma goonga, ko a wewlinoowo e jertinoowo. Alaa e mofte, si wanaa jertinoowo feƴƴii e maɓɓe
35|25|Si ɓe fennii ma, hari adinooɓe ɓe ɓen fenniino (Nulaaɓe mun), fewndo ɓen Nulaaɓe maɓɓe addannoo ɓanngannduyeeji, e Ɗeri e Deftere ndayginoore
35|26|Refti nanngitir mi yedduɓe ɓen (halakuyee). Taskii no lepte An ɗen waɗtinirnoo
35|27|E a tinaali wonnde Alla jippinirii ndiyam ka kammu? Men fuɗiniri ɗam dimɗe seertuɗe noone. Hino ka pelle, ɗate daneeje e boɗeeje seertyuɗe noone, e pete ɓaleeje
35|28|Hino e yimɓe ɓen, e daabeeji ɗin, e neemoraaɗi ɗin, ɗi nooneeji mun kadi luutondiri. Anndu ko hulata Alla e jeyaaɓe Makko ɓen, ko annduɓe ɓen. Pellet, Alla ko Fooluɗo, Haforoowo
35|29|Ɓen janngooɓe Deftere Alla nden, ɓe ñiiɓi e julde, ɓe nafqii ko Men arsiki ɓe kon gunndoo e kene, hiɓe jortii njulaaku ngu sontataa
35|30|Fii no [Alla] hunnirana ɓe njoɓdiiji maɓɓe ɗin, O ɓeyda ɓe e ɓural Makko ngal. Kanko, ko O Haforoowo, Annditanoowo [on]
35|31|Kon ko Men wahayini e maaɗa e Deftere nden, ko ɗum woni goonga, gomɗinde e ɗen wonɗe yeeso mayre. Pellet, Alla ko Humpitiiɗo Rentuɗo jeyaaɓe Makko ɓen
35|32|Refti Men ronini Deftere nden, ɓen ɓe Men suɓii e jeyaaɓe Amen. Hino e maɓɓe tooñuɓe hoore-mun, hino e maɓɓe hakindinɗo, hino e maɓɓe foolondirooɓe e moƴƴereeji, duŋayee Alla; ko ɗum woni ɓural mawnungal ngal
35|33|Aljannaaji ñiiɓal, ɗi naatata e mun, hara hiɓe cuɗiree ton, jawe kaŋŋe e kaalise e lu’u-lu’u; comci maɓɓe ɗin ton, ko sooyi
35|34|Ɓe wi'a: "Yettoore woodanii Alla, On ittanɗo en suno. Pellet, Joomi men, ko Haforoowo, Warjotooɗo
35|35|On weernirɗo en ɓural Makko ngal, e galle ñiiɓal, tampere (woo) heɓataa en ton, wanaa ronkere heɓata en ton
35|36|Yedduɓe ɓen kan, ko Yiite Jahannama woodani ɓen; maayde ñaawetaake e maɓɓe, sakko ɓe maaya, ɓe hoynantaake kadi lepte magge ɗen. Ko wano nii Men yoɓitirta kala yedduɗo
35|37|Hara hiɓe ooloo nder ton [ɓe wi'a]: "Joomi amen, yaltin men; men golla moƴƴere, hara wonah ko men gollaynoo kon". [O jaaboo ɓe]: "E men wuurnaano on yeru ko waajitotooɗo waajitoranoo e mun? Jertinoowo kadi ari e mon? Awa meeɗee, sabu faabo alanaa tooñooɓe ɓen
35|38|Pellet, Alla ko Annduɗo wirniiɗi kammuuli ɗin e leydi ndin. Ko O Annduɗo ko suuɗii e ɓerɗe
35|39|Ko Kanko woni waɗuɗo on lontiiɓe ka leydi. Kala yedduɗo, ko e makko lorra geddi makko yantata. Yeddugol heeferɓe ɓen, ɓeydataa ɓe ka Joomi maɓɓe, si wanaa tikkere. Yeddugol ɓeydataa heeferɓe ɓen, si wanaa hayrere
35|40|Maaku: "E on yi'ii rendiiɗi mon rewoton gaanin Alla ɗin? Hollee lam ko ɗi tagi ka leydi. Kaa hiɗi mari geɓal e [tagugol] kammuuli ɗin? Kaa Men addan ɓe Deftere, nde ɓe woni e ɓanndannduyee mun? Si ko woni, tooñooɓe ɓen alaa e fodude yoga maɓɓe, si wanaa hodo
35|41|Pellet, ko Alla jogitii kammuuli ɗin e leydi ndin, fii wata ɗi dirtu. Hay si ɗi dirtayno, hay gooto jogitotaako ɗi e ɓaawo Makko. O laatike Muññiiɗo, Haforoowo
35|42|Ɓe woodndiri Alla, hattirde e goondooje maɓɓe, wonnde si jertinoowo arii e maɓɓe, pellet, ɓe wonay ɓurɓe feewude wootere e mofte ɗen. Nde jertinoowo non arunoo e maɓɓe, ɗum ɓeydaali ɓe, si wanaa woɗɗitagol
35|43|[Ɓe waɗiri ɗum] mawnintinaare ka keydi, e pewje ɓenɗe. Pewje bonɗe ɗen non huuɓitataa, si wanaa jom-mun'en. Hara hiɓe sabbitii, si wanaa sunna (Alla) on e adinooɓe ɓen? A heɓantaa sunna Alla on battiigu, a heɓantaa sunna Alla waylirɗum
35|44|E ɓee yiilaaki ka leydi, ɓe taskoo ko honno battane adinooɓe ɓen wonirnoo? Hari no ɓuri ɓe tiiɗude doole. Alla siforaali wonnde goɗɗum no ronkina Mo ka kammuuli maa ka leydi. Tawde pellet, ko O Annduɗo, Hattanɗo
35|45|Si tawno Alla nanngitirayno yimɓe ɓen ko ɓe faggitorii kon, O accataano ruugayngel e dow mayri. Ko woni tun, Himo nennitana ɓe haa e lajal anndaa ngal. Si lajal maɓɓe ngal hewtii, [O nanngay ɓe], tawde pellet, Alla ko Reenuɗo jeyaaɓe Makko ɓen
36|1|Yaa-Siin
36|2|Mi woondirii Al*ur'aana ñeñaande nden
36|3|Pellet, an (Nulaaɗo), ko a jeyaaɗo e Nulaaɓe ɓen
36|4|E dow laawol focciingol
36|5|Jippinannde On Fooluɗo, Hinnotoo
36|6|Fii yo a jertinir nde yimɓe, ɓe baabiraaɓe mun jertinanooka: ɓen ko welsindiiɓe
36|7|Gomɗii konngol [lepte] jojjii e ko ɓuri ɗuuɗude e maɓɓe; ɓen ɗon gomɗintaa
36|8|Menen Men waɗii ka daaɗe maɓɓe kolommbooje, ɗen ko yottiiɗe ka bokkuɗe; hara ko ɓe ŋalliniiɓe
36|9|Men waɗi yeeso maɓɓe heedo, ɓaawo maɓɓe kadi heedo, Men hippi ɓe (gite ɗen); waɗti ɓe yi'ataa [goonga]
36|10|Hino fota e maɓɓe, foti a jertini ɓe, maa a jertinaali ɓe; ɓe gomɗintaa
36|11|Anndu ko jertintaa (jaɓa), ko on jokkuɗo Jantoore (Alqur'aana) nden, o huli Jom-Yurmeende On ka wirnii. Wewlinir mo haforaneede e mbarjaari teddundi
36|12|Ko Menen woni wuurnitooɓe maayɓe ɓen, Men winnda ko ɓe ardini e batteeji maɓɓe. Kala huunde, Meɗen mofti nde e deftere ɓanngunde
36|13|Piyan-ɓe misal, fii yimɓe saare, tuma nde Nulaaɓe arunoo ɓe
36|14|Nde Men nulunoo e maɓɓe, [Nulaaɓe] ɗiɗo, ɓe fenni ɓen, Men sammbiniri ɓen, tataɓo, ɓe wi'i: "Menen, ko men Nulaaɓe e mo'on
36|15|[Yimɓe saare nden] wi'i: "On wonaali, si wanaa ko on ɓanndinke wano menen. Jom-hinaranke On jippinaali hay huunde, on wonaali, si wanaa ko on fenooɓe
36|16|[Nulaaɓe ɓen] wi'i: "Joomi amen no anndi pellet, ko men Nulaaɓe e mo'on
36|17|Fawaaki men non, si wanaa yottingol ɓanngina
36|18|[Yimɓe saare nden] wi'iti: "Men hiitori on kataa. Si tawii non on haɗitaaki, ma men fiɗu on, lepte muusuɗe kadi memira on immorde e amen
36|19|[Nulaaɓe ɓen kadi] wi'iti: "Kiite mon ɗin, hiɗon wonndi e mun. Ko si on waajaama (hiitinoɗon)? Tigi on, ko on yimɓe fantinooɓe
36|20|Gorko iwri ka ɓuri woɗɗude e saare nden, o ari himo yaccoo, o wi'i: "Ko onon yo yimɓe am, kori jokkee Nulaaɓe ɓen
36|21|jokkee ɓen ɓe lamndotaako on njoɓdi, ɓen ko fewnaaɓe
36|22|E ko haɗata lam rewugol On taguɗo Lam? Ko ka Makko woni ruttorde mon
36|23|E mi jogtoto reweteeɗi gaanin Makko? Si Jom-yurmeende On muuyanii lam lorra, tefoore majji duncantaali lam hay huunde, ɗi dɗandataa lam kadi
36|24|Haray min ontuma, mi wonii e majjere ɓanngunde
36|25|Min on, mi gomɗinii Joomi mon, nananee lam
36|26|wi'anaa: "Naatu Aljanna". O wi'i: "Haaniino yimɓe am ɓen annda
36|27|ko Joomi am haforani lam, O waɗi lam e teddinaaɓe ɓen
36|28|Men jippiniraano koneeli ka kammu, e yimɓe makko ɓen, ɓaawo maako. Men wonaanii jippinooɓe [ɗin koneeli]
36|29|(Halkeede maɓɓe) wonaali, si wanaa haacaango wooto, tawi ɓe laatii maayɓe-ɓutti
36|30|Ee hayreede jeyaaɓe [fenunooɓe]! Nulaaɗo araali e ɓɓe, si wanaa ɓe waɗtayno mo jalnori
36|31|E ɓee yi'aali ɗuuɗii e gire ɗe Men halki ado maɓɓe? Wonnde ɓen ruttitotaako e maɓɓe
36|32|Ɓe fow wonaali, si wanaa ko mooɓoyteeɓe ka Amen
36|33|Hino wonani ɓe maande: leydi yoorundi ndin, Men wuurniti ndi, Men yaltini gabbe e mayri, tawi ko e ɗen ɓe ñaamata
36|34|Men waɗi e mayri gese tamarooje e inabuuje, Men ɓulni e mayri ɓulli(ceewle)
36|35|fii no ɓe ñaamira dimɗe mun ɗen e kon ko ɓe golliri juuɗe maɓɓe ɗen. E ɓe yettataa (Alla)
36|36|Senaade woodanii taguɗo nooneeji ɗin On fow: gila e ko leydi ndin fuɗinta kon, haa e wonkiiji maɓɓe ɗin, e kon ko ɓe anndaa
36|37|Maande goo kadi wonanii ɓe: e jemma on, Meɗen sorta e makko ñalorma on, tawa ɓe wontii e niwre
36|38|E naange ngen, hinge doga haa e ñiiɓirde magge; ɗum ko eɓɓoore Fooluɗo, Annduɗo On
36|39|E lewru ndun, Men eɓɓani ndu jipporde, haa ndu waɗtinira wa baaŋal tamaro kiiɗngal
36|40|Wanaa naange ngen woni ko haanini hewtitagol lewru ndun, wanaa jemma on woni ko aditotoo ñalorma on; kala majji non, ko e laawol mun woni dogude
36|41|Maande goo wonanii ɓe, wonnde Men roondike geyngol maɓɓe ngol, ka laana hebbinaaka
36|42|Men tagani ɓe sugu makko, ko ɓe waɗɗoo
36|43|Si Meɗen yiɗuno, Men yoolayno ɓe; hara faabo alanaa ɓe, wanaa kadi ɓe daɗndeteeɓe
36|44|si wanaa yurmeende immornde e Amen, e dakmitagol haa e saanga
36|45|Si ɓe wi'anaama: "Rentee e kon ko woni yeeso mon e ɓaawo mon, belajo'o, on yurminte
36|46|Aaya woo e Aayeeje Joomi maɓɓe ɗen araali e maɓɓe, si wanaa ɓe ɗuurnooɗe
36|47|Si ɓe wi'anaama kadi: "Wintee(nafqe) e kon Alla arsiki on", yedduɓe ɓen wi'ana gomɗimɓe ɓen: "E men ñamminay on tawɗo si Alla muuyuno, O ñamminayno mo? On wonaali, si wanaa e nder majjere ɓanngunde
36|48|Hiɓe wi'a: "Ko honnde tuma woni ndee Fodoore, si on laatike goonguɓe
36|49|Ɓe habbaaki, si wanaa haacaango wooto, nanngayngo ɓe, hara hiɓe yeddondira
36|50|Ɓe waawoytaa wasiyagol ontuma, wanaa ɓe ruttoytooɓe e yimɓe maɓɓe ɓen
36|51|Wutte ka Alaandu, ɓe yaltira e genaale ɗen, ɓe heñora ka Joomi maɓɓe
36|52|hiɓe wi'a: "Ee bone amen! Ko hommbo immini men e genaale amen?" Ko ɗum woni ko Hinaranke On fodunoo; Nulaaɓe ɓen goonginii
36|53|(Ummital) ngal wonaano, si wanaa haacaango gooto, tawi ɓe fow ɓe addaama ka Amen
36|54|Hannde non, wonkii tooñirtaake hay huunde. On yoɓitirtaake, si wanaa kon ko gollaynoɗon
36|55|Yimɓe Aljanna ɓe hannde, pellet, hiɓe e nder soklio, hiɓe neeminoo
36|56|kamɓe e genndiraaɓe maɓɓe ɓen,e ley ɗowɗe, hiɓe soɓɓindii e hoore danɗe
36|57|Hino woodani ɓe ton, ɓiɗɓe leɗɗe, hino woodani kadi, kon ko ɓe noddata
36|58|Salaamun", konngol [kisiyee], immorde e Joomiraaɗo, Hinnotooɗo
36|59|Sertee non hande, onon ɓee bomɓe
36|60|Mi ahodaano e mon, onon ɓiɗɓe Aadama, wonnde wata on rewu seytaane? Tawde pellet, ko o gaño mon ɓannguɗo
36|61|[Mi yamiri on] kadi rewugol Lam. Ko ngol woni laawol focciingol ngol
36|62|Gomɗii o majjinii tagu ɗuuɗungu e mon. E on wonaano haqqilooɓe
36|63|Ko ngee woni Jahannama, nge wonanoɗon fodaneede ngen
36|64|Naatiree nge hannde, sabu kon ko yeddiraynoɗon
36|65|Hannde, Men notay e kunndule maɓɓe ɗen, juuɗe maɓɓe ɗen yewta Men, koyɗe maɓɓe ɗen kadi seeditoo e kon ko ɓe wonunoo e faggitagol
36|66|Si Men yiɗuno, Men mehayno gite maɓɓe ɗen, ɓe adondira e laawol ngol. Kono ko honno ɓe yiirata
36|67|Si Men yiɗuno kadi, Men montayno ɓe e nokku maɓɓe on; hara ɓe hattantaa feƴƴugol ɓe yiltotaako
36|68|Kala mo Men juutni nguurndam mun, Men yiltitay mo e tagu ngun. E ɓee haqqiltaa
36|69|Men anndinaali mo (kanko Muhammadu) gimɗi; ɗum haananaa mo. [Deftere] nden wonaali, si wanaa jantoore e janngeteende ɓanngunde
36|70|fii yo o jertin nde, on wonɗo wuurɗo (ɓernde), Konngol lepte ngol jojja e heeferɓe ɓen
36|71|E ɓe yi'aali, wonnde Men tagiranii ɓe neemoraaɗi, e ko juuɗe Amen golli, hara hiɓe jeyinooɗi
36|72|Men eltani ɓe ɗi: no e majji ɗi ɓe waɗɗotoo, no e majji ɗi ɓe ñaamata
36|73|hino woodani ɓe ton, nafooje e njaram. E ɓee kan yettataa (Mo)
36|74|Ɓe jogitorii gaanin Alla reweteeɗi, jortagol ɓe faabeedee
36|75|Ɗi hattanaa faabagol ɓe; ko ɓe konu tawneteengu e majji
36|76|Wata konngol maɓɓe sunine. Pellet, Meɗen anndi ko ɓe suuɗata e ko ɓe feññinta
36|77|E neɗɗanke on yi'aali, wonnde Men tagirii mo e toɓɓere maniiyu? Kono tawaa mo ko o wennjoowo ɓannguɗo
36|78|O fiyani Men misal, kono o yejjiti tageede makko; o wi'i: "Ko hommbo wuurnitata ƴi'e ɗen, si ɗe rappii
36|79|Maaku: "Ko wuurnitoowo ɗe, ko taguɗo ɗe On ka laawol aranol. Ko Kanko woni annduɗo fii kala tagu
36|80|On waɗanɗo on yiite, iwde e leɗɗe kecce, tawa ko e majje huɓɓirton nge
36|81|Kere taguɗo kammuuli ɗin e leydi ndin wonaali haɗtanɗo tagugol yeru maɓɓe? Ɗum ko pellet! Ko Kanko woni Ɗuuɗuɗo tageefo, Annduɗo
36|82|Anndon fiyaaku Makko On, si O faandanike huunde, ko O wi'anay nde tun: "Laato", nde laatoo

37|1|Mi woondirii saffiniraaɗi ɗin saffaaji
37|2|Mi woondirii soggirayɗi (duule) ɗin soggugol
37|3|Mi woondirii janngirayɗi ɗin, anndintinorgol
37|4|Pellet, reweteeɗo mon On, ko bajjo
37|5|Jeyɗo kammuuli ɗin e leydi ndin, e kon ko woni hakkunde ɗin ɗiɗi, Jeyɗo kadi fuɗirɗe ɗen
37|6|Men cuɗirii kammu (hikkii ngu) aduna ngun: cuɗaari koode ɗen
37|7|e reenirgol (ngu) kala seytaane raɗaandu
37|8|Ɗi haɗtanaaka heɗitagol mbatu [Malaa'ika'en] toowu ngu ngun; tawde hiɗi feroree e kala baŋŋe
37|9|ka raɗagol (ɗi). Hino woodani ɗi kadi, lepte duumiiɗe
37|10|Si wanaa ndun bifti ndu e majji, jilannde [haala], ndu rewniree hoodere tufaynde
37|11|Lamndo ɓe: si ko kamɓe ɓuri saɗtude tagude kaa ko ɓen ɓe Men tagi? Men tagirii ɓe kamɓe, loopal narnungal
37|12|Si ko woni, a haawi, hiɓe jalnora
37|13|Si ɓe waajaama, ɓe waajitortaa
37|14|si ɓe yi'ii maande, ɓe jalkita
37|15|ɓe wi'a: "Ɗum wonaali, si wanaa mbilewu ɓanngu ngu
37|16|Eyoo si men maayii, men wontii mbullaari e ƴi'e, haray ko men immintinoyteeɓe
37|17|Baabiraaɓe amen adinooɓe ɓen kadi e minen
37|18|Maaku: "Pellet! Hara le ko on hoynaaɓe
37|19|Anndon ɗum, ko wuttaandu wooturu pet, tawee jaka yoo, hiɓe ndaara
37|20|Ɓe wi'a: Ee bone amen ! Ko ndee woni Ñalaande njoɓdi kuuɗe
37|21|Ko ndee woni Ñalaande ñaawoore, ko fennaynoɗon fii mun
37|22|Mooɓee tooñuɓe ɓen, e nandadiiɓe maɓɓe ɓen, e kon ko ɓe wonunoo e rewde
37|23|ko wonaa Alla. Soggireeɓe ka laawol Jahiimi
37|24|Darnon ɓe, tawde ko ɓe lamnditeteeɓe
37|25|Ko heɓi on, on wallindirtaa
37|26|Ko woni kamɓe on hannde, ko ɓe jebbilii ɓe
37|27|woɗɓe e maɓɓe fewtita ɓeya, ɓe lamndondira
37|28|ɓe wi'a: "Ko onon woni ko ardiranaynoo men, ka ɓaŋŋe ñaamo
37|29|(Koohooɓe) ɓen wi'a: "Ko woni kon, on meeɗaano wonnde gomɗimɓe
37|30|Doole woo men alanaano on. Si ko woni, on wonuno yimɓe bewɓe
37|31|Konngol Joomi men ngol, jojjii e men; pellet, ko en meeɗooɓe [lepte ɗen]
37|32|Men bewinno on, tawde hay menen, ko men bewnooɓe
37|33|Kamɓe on nden ñalnde, ko ɓe hawtoyteeɓe ka lepte
37|34|Ko nii Menen Men huuwirta bomɓe ɓen
37|35|Kamɓe si ɓe wi'anooma: "Reweteeɗo alaa si wanaa Alla", ɓe mawnintinoo
37|36|ɓe wi'a: "Kere men accitiray reweteeɗi amen ɗin, fii yimoowo haangaaɗo
37|37|Si ko woni, (Nulaaɗo) on ko goonga ardi, o goongini Nulaaɓe ɓen
37|38|Pellet, ko on meeɗay ɓe lepte muusuɗe ɗen
37|39|On yoɓitetaake, si wanaa yeru kon ko huuwaynoɗon
37|40|si wanaa jeyaaɓe Alla laɓɓinaaɓe ɓen
37|41|hino woodani ɓen ɗon, fanndaari anndaandi
37|42|muuyanteeɗi, kadi ko ɓe teddinaaɓe
37|43|ka Aljannaaji neeminiiɗi
37|44|e hoore danɗe, ko ɓe fewtondirɓe
37|45|Hara kore hino wannginii e maɓɓe, immorde e ɓulirde
37|46|daneere, lewñunde, fii yarooɓe
37|47|muusu hoore alaa e majjam, wanaa ɗam siwrinirteeɓe ɗam
37|48|Hino woodani ɓe (ton): raɓɓiduɓe ndaarɗe, yaaja giteeɓe
37|49|wa'uɓe wa boofo maraaɗe

37|51|Goɗɗo e maɓɓe wi'a: "Min miɗo marunoo wonndiiɗo
37|52|wi'aynooɗo: "Kere ko a jeyaaɗo e googimɓe ɓen
37|53|Eyoo si en maayii, en wontii mbullaari e ƴi'e, haray ko en yoɓitoyteeɓe
37|54|O wi'a: "Taw si ɗon yiɗi ƴeewude
37|55|O ƴeewa, o haynoo oya ka tummbo Dulbunge
37|56|o wi'a: "Mi woondirii Alla ! A eɓɓuno fii no mi halkorde
37|57|Si wanaano moƴƴere Joomi am nden, mi tawdeteno e [lepteteeɓe ɓen]
37|58|Wonaa non enen maayataa
37|59|si wanaa maayde men aranere nden, en wonaali kadi lepteteeɓe
37|60|Pellet, ko ɗum ɗoo woni maloore mawnunde nden
37|61|Ko fii sugu ɗum ɗoo, woni yo gollooɓe gollan
37|62|Hara ko ɗum ɓuri moƴƴude jipporde, kaa ko leggal "Zaqquumi" [ngal haaɗungal]
37|63|Men waɗii ngal jarrabuyee tooñuɓe ɓen
37|64|Ngal, ko leggal yaltayngal ka tummbere Dulbunge
37|65|Dimɗe maggal, hino wa'i wa ko'e seytanooji
37|66|Kamɓe on, pellet, ko e maggal ɓe nyaamirta, ɓe hebbinira ngal deedi maɓɓe
37|67|Refti hino woodani ɓe e dow maggal, njaram fatinaaɗam
37|68|Refti ruttorde maɓɓe nden, ko ka Dulɓoowe
37|69|Ɓe tawu baabiraaɓe maɓɓe ɓen, ko majjunooɓe
37|70|ɓe woni e yaccagol jokka baɗteeji maɓɓe
37|71|Gomɗii, ko ɓuri ɗuuɗude e aramɓe ɓen, majjiino, ado maɓɓe
37|72|Gomɗii le, Men nuluno e maɓɓe, jertinooɓe
37|73|Kono ndaaru baɗtane ɓen jertinanooɓe, no wa'unoo
37|74|Si wanaa jeyaaɓe Alla, laɓɓinaaɓe ɓen
37|75|Gomɗii Nuuhu nodduno Men, Men moƴƴii jaabotooɓe
37|76|Men daɗni mo, kanko e yimɓe makko ɓen, e suno mawnungo ngon
37|77|Men waɗi geyngol makko ngol, heddotooɓe ɓen
37|78|Men accani mo mantoore, e sakkitiiɓe ɓen
37|79|Kisal wonii e Nuuhu, e nder winndere nden
37|80|Ko non woni ko Men warjorta moƴƴimɓe ɓen
37|81|Kanko, ko o jeyanooɗo e jeyaaɓe Amen gomɗimɓe ɓen
37|82|Refti Men yooli heddii ɓe ɓen
37|83|Hino jeyanoo e jokkuɓe mo ɓen, Ibraahiima
37|84|Tuma nde ardunoo ka Joomi makko, e ɓernde hisunde
37|85|Nde o maakannoo ben makko e yimɓe mun ɓen: "Ko honɗum rewoton
37|86|E ko reweteeɗi fefindaaɗi, ko wanaa Alla, faalaɗon
37|87|Ko sikkuɗon e Joomiraawo tageefo ngon
37|88|O ndaariri ndaarande ka koode
37|89|o maaki: "Ko mi nawnuɗo
37|90|Ɓe acci mo, ɓe hucciti
37|91|O moltii e reweteeɗi maɓɓe ɗin, o maaki: "E on ñaamataa
37|92|Ko heɓi on, on wowlataa
37|93|O moltorani ɗi, piyirgol ɗi ñaamo ngon
37|94|Ɓe fewri ka makko, hiɓe yaawno
37|95|O maaki: "E on reway kon ko lesuɗon
37|96|hara le ko Alla tagi on, e kon ko golloton
37|97|Ɓe wi'i: "Mahanee mo maadi, bugoɗon mo ka dulɓayange
37|98|Ɓe faandanii mo feere; kono Men waɗi ɓe sooyube ɓen
37|99|O maaki: "Min on, ko mi feroowo ka Joomi am, aray nde O fewnata lam
37|100|Joomi am, yeɗam geɓal moƴƴuɓe
37|101|Men wewliniri mo, geɗal muññiiɗo
37|102|Nde on yottinoo e makko jahal, [Ibraahiima] maaki: "Ko an ɓiɗɗo am, min mi yi'ii e ɗoyngol, wonnde miɗo hirse. Ndaaru ko yi'uɗaa". [Ismaa'iila] maaki: "Ko onon yo baaba'en, waɗee ko yamiraɗon kon, on tawoyay lam, si Alla jaɓii, jeyaaɗo e muñiiɓe ɓen
37|103|Nde ɓe jebbilaninoo (ymiroore Alla nden), o hippiri mo tiinde nden

38|1|Saad. Mi woondirii Alqur'aana, jom waaju

38|23|Oo ko musiɗɗo am: himo jogii baali cappanɗe jeenay e jeenay, min miɗo jogii baalii gootii. O wi'i: "Henndinam ngii"; o foolimi e yewtere
38|24|O maaki: "Pellet, o tooñirii ma lamndagol baalii maa ngii, waɗtugol e baali makko ɗin". Ɗuuɗii ko hawtuɓe tooñindirta hakkunde maɓɓe, si wanaa ɓen gomɗimɓe, ɓe golli moƴƴuɗi - ɓen non no fanɗi. - Daawuuda felliti, wonnde Men jarribike mo. O insinanii Joomi makko, o suuyiri sujjugol, o tuubi
